
-----title
谷城 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0d3f163cba0c4ebc91d21590f5b10985_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0d3f163cba0c4ebc91d21590f5b10985");'><span id='0d3f163cba0c4ebc91d21590f5b10985_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1122')">1114-1122年</a>　居乡谷城。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4e0e1532486c4761a94b26228bb5bd32_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4e0e1532486c4761a94b26228bb5bd32");'><span id='4e0e1532486c4761a94b26228bb5bd32_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1131')">1127-1131年</a>，24-28岁</div><div id='4e0e1532486c4761a94b26228bb5bd32' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1128')">1127-1128年</a>　在谷城，丧父。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月</a>　在谷城，居父丧。十一月，范宗尹除参知政事，王之望赠之以诗。作品：赠范觉民。<div id='poem_66622' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_66622' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/66622?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠范觉民</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_66622")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_66622_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_66622'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_66622'>范子廊庙器，至宝非凡璞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_66622'>胸怀吞云梦，豪气低华岳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_66622'>昔在童稚时，树立已卓卓。<div id='poem_sentence_2_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_66622'>曳裾桥门内，崭然见头角。<div id='poem_sentence_3_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_66622'>岁行在辛丑，帝策询民瘼。<div id='poem_sentence_4_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_66622'>造庭百千人，衣带矜褒博。<div id='poem_sentence_5_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_66622'>平居议执政，至此舌为括。<div id='poem_sentence_6_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_66622'>独馀子范子，雅志不可夺。<div id='poem_sentence_7_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_66622'>吐辞如涌泉，一发孰能遏。<div id='poem_sentence_8_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_66622'>挥毫不停缀，盈卷无点抹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_66622'>汉廷执戟郎，环顾皆错莫。<div id='poem_sentence_10_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_66622'>纵横五千字，字字医国药。<div id='poem_sentence_11_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_66622'>期于必伐病，非徒事迂阔。<div id='poem_sentence_12_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_66622'>怪言一惊众，士论叹且愕。<div id='poem_sentence_13_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_66622'>皆云布衣流，志在縻好爵。<div id='poem_sentence_14_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_66622'>乃尔张危言，身谋胡太错。<div id='poem_sentence_15_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_66622'>当时群宗匠，其间多龌龊。<div id='poem_sentence_16_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_66622'>指言为沽直，欲使趋鼎镬。<div id='poem_sentence_17_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_66622'>堂堂春官臣，主张独何确。<div id='poem_sentence_18_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_66622'>谠议既冰释，众口不能铄。<div id='poem_sentence_19_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_66622'>乙科忽大阐，秋天一雕鹗。<div id='poem_sentence_20_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_66622'>传诵争取先，纸价为翔跃。<div id='poem_sentence_21_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_66622'>声华顿辉赫，蔼然暨南朔。<div id='poem_sentence_22_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_66622'>忆昔客东都，猥厕英游数。<div id='poem_sentence_23_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_66622'>每于谈笑间，论议闻謇谔。<div id='poem_sentence_24_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_66622'>诵语非沽名，生平真所乐。<div id='poem_sentence_25_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_66622'>乖离三四载，遣我情怀恶。<div id='poem_sentence_26_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_66622'>间者见眉宇，飒然意气豁。<div id='poem_sentence_27_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_66622'>亟使罗酒浆，沈沈动清酌。<div id='poem_sentence_28_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_66622'>秉烛夜相对，谈词恣嘲谑。<div id='poem_sentence_29_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_66622'>公卿颇历诋，治乱亦商略。<div id='poem_sentence_30_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_66622'>间出新诗篇，清制皆洒落。<div id='poem_sentence_31_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_66622'>祇怀苍生忧，肯为穷愁作。<div id='poem_sentence_32_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_66622'>少陵不忘主，气味若相若。<div id='poem_sentence_33_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_66622'>倘使任言责，必有裨帷幄。<div id='poem_sentence_34_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_66622'>奈何谏诤姿，久矣滞丘壑。<div id='poem_sentence_35_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_66622'>似闻庙堂上，知己被新渥。<div id='poem_sentence_36_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_66622'>一公丞乌台，一公相黄阁。<div id='poem_sentence_37_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_66622'>吾君皆<span class='inlineComment2'>（文津本作望）</span>太平，二公繄深托。<div id='poem_sentence_38_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_66622'>荐贤乃报国，看子翔寥廓。<div id='poem_sentence_39_66622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_66622'></div><div id='poem_sentence_40_66622_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　居襄阳谷城，为避襄阳乱，西走汉中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　在谷城。除父丧，仍困居家乡。始识綦崇礼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　困居家乡谷城。范宗尹罢相归乡，与之成患难之交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　困居家乡谷城。已有长子镛。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c9ecbd23d6a74f1785130e3b19ee0f5b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c9ecbd23d6a74f1785130e3b19ee0f5b");'><span id='c9ecbd23d6a74f1785130e3b19ee0f5b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1126')">1123-1126年</a>，20-23岁</div><div id='c9ecbd23d6a74f1785130e3b19ee0f5b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1124')">1123-1124年</a>　在汴京，游于太学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　在汴京，自都城开封至河南封丘省欧阳氏姊，途中有诗寄范宗尹。作品：乙巳四月自都下省欧阳氏姊于封丘时河朔流移满道即事有作寄范觉民。<div id='poem_66472' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_66472' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/66472?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乙巳四月自都下省欧阳氏姊于封丘时河朔流移满道即事有作寄范觉民</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_66472")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_66472_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_66472'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_66472'>北出都门道，红尘污客襟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_66472_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_66472'>号蝉如有意，高柳自成阴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_66472_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_66472'>辙乱思良马，林幽慕逸禽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_66472_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_66472'>据鞍回首处，愈觉帝阍深。<div id='poem_sentence_3_66472_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_66472'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_66472_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　曾与乃父至南阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　在汴京，秋试。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
温州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cc01d1b6e5b54ee4b3cd655b95e1563b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cc01d1b6e5b54ee4b3cd655b95e1563b");'><span id='cc01d1b6e5b54ee4b3cd655b95e1563b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>，29岁</div><div id='cc01d1b6e5b54ee4b3cd655b95e1563b' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>至东瓯。居东瓯期间，闻讯姊已死三年，痛骇而作祭文。作品：祭宜州欧阳氏姊文。<div id='poem_1243597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭宜州欧阳氏姊文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243597")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243597'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243597'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243597_comment'></div>我生不辰，幼遭悯凶，七岁失母，踰冠而孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243597_comment'></div>同产之爱，荐遇兵祸，死生契阔，今馀一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243597_comment'></div>姊先南来，意必无恙，云何不淑，亦遽夭伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243597_comment'></div>荼毒苍天，痛酷苍天！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243597_comment'></div>惟姊为人，天资明哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243597_comment'></div>既归华族，内外咸宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243597_comment'></div>克育奇儿，聪敏是似，谓成伟器，光我外家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243597_comment'></div>岂期母子，相继沦谢，一岁之内，逝者四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243597_comment'></div>身既零落，爰及苗裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243597_comment'></div>王氏之出，绝于高门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243597_comment'></div>何辜于天，祸至此酷！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243597_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243597_comment'></div>姊于兄弟，我爱尤厚，鞠我字我，恩勤备至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243597_comment'></div>自姊之别，无日不思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243597_comment'></div>襄汉大乱，骨肉凋丧，数口避地，西走汉中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243597_comment'></div>念姊在南，乃心悬悬，涉险万里，惟姊之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243597_comment'></div>我困东瓯，姊在南越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243597_comment'></div>虽间岭海，会有见期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243597_comment'></div>姊家书来，踊跃以喜，谓承吉问，以慰远怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243597_comment'></div>发函中读，忽睹凶报，惊惶痛骇，号叫失声，泣血拊膺，五情割裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243597_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243597_comment'></div>姊殁三岁，我始获知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243597_comment'></div>哀信未来，犹谓姊在，日日以冀，庶几见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243597_comment'></div>自今以往，此怀绝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243597_comment'></div>昔与姊别，我尚未婚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243597_comment'></div>今妇惟张，有子惟镛，愿一见姊，俾其识姑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243597_comment'></div>噫其永已，夫复何言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243597_comment'></div>万里闻丧，奔赴无及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243597_comment'></div>远寓一奠，魂驰形留，南望长号，绝而复活。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1243597_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在东瓯，上书綦崇礼，为生计而求官。作品：上綦侍郎书。<div id='poem_1243399' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243399' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243399?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上綦侍郎书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243399")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243399_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243399'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243399'>某闻南山之阿有异木焉，萌蘖以生，才数寸尔，已有郁然挠云之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243399_comment'></div>不幸压于土石，拳蹙不遂，将失其性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243399_comment'></div>又遭时之旱暵，泉乾土裂，孤根熬熬，焦然且死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243399_comment'></div>俄而有泰山之云，蒸布太虚，将遍雨乎天下，百谷草木毕仰其泽，而是木也尤汲汲焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243399_comment'></div>夫云之降时雨以润物，固其职也，非有私乎惠物也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243399_comment'></div>物之仰雨以生，亦其宜也，非有私乎求雨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243399_comment'></div>然是木也于众草中独汲汲焉，欲亟蒙其泽者，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243399_comment'></div>盖困于积年之压，重以三伏之旱，抑屈枯悴，非他草木比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243399_comment'></div>一日二日不雨，殆将死矣，则其情岂不急而可怜哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243399_comment'></div>今有人不幸而类此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243399_comment'></div>其生于世二十有九年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243399_comment'></div>其立身行己，积学著文，虽不敢妄意古人，亦不肯自后时辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243399_comment'></div>弱冠游太学，屡以不腆之语，滥处上游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243399_comment'></div>丙午试于秋闱，亦在异等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243399_comment'></div>此顾何足道，然倘一得献技于礼部，待问于天庭，虽不足以争步英豪，追踪晁、董，至如韩退之所谓「循次而进，亦不失万一于甲科」者，诚不自揆，妄以为庶几焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243399_comment'></div>奈何遭时不祥，仍以家难，流离忧苦，不得试其艺者已七年于兹，是以在此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243399_comment'></div>若乃讥评时政，诋诃公卿，出位而谋，居下讪上，以侥倖万一，则又某之所不忍为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243399_comment'></div>以此饥寒困穷，为当世失职者之最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243399_comment'></div>今者迫于门户之寄，衣食之奉，摧折素志，欲因世禄而苟一官，悼心失图，自愧平昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243399_comment'></div>是岂异夫木之拳蹙不遂，失其本性，遭旱而将死者邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243399_comment'></div>伏遇阁下以贰卿之重，独总天官，自二千石而下皆铨次于阁下之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243399_comment'></div>士大夫之望之，若百谷之仰膏雨也，而某事之去留亦在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243399_comment'></div>于众士大夫中，独更汲汲有望乎阁下者，其意非有求乎其私之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243399_comment'></div>盖以流落之久，资用不足以供桂玉，而羁穷之馀，钱财不足以贿胥吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243399_comment'></div>自非阁下特达而哀怜之，则旦暮之间且饿而死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243399_comment'></div>此所以祈公之尤切，而望公之尤深也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243399_comment'></div>伏惟阁下云行雨施，利泽万物之馀，赐之以涓滴，则枯茎朽枝不崇朝而遂有生意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243399_comment'></div>虽绵弱之质，何以酬造化之施？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243399_comment'></div>然假以岁时，俾其成材，岁寒之资，或有可观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243399_comment'></div>夫叩人急者人必疑，无因而至前者人莫我知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243399_comment'></div>今某实犯二忌以进，故敢献其区区之说，欲阁下一知而不疑耳，激昂自荐，市道所羞，冒昧自陈，出于穷迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243399_comment'></div>惟察其肺肝，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1243399_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d01c889398cf408caa2fac1a6f8a63ec_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d01c889398cf408caa2fac1a6f8a63ec");'><span id='d01c889398cf408caa2fac1a6f8a63ec_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>，66岁</div><div id='d01c889398cf408caa2fac1a6f8a63ec' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　年初，到温州任。有谒诸庙文。作品：永嘉到任谒诸庙文。<div id='poem_1243620' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243620' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243620?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永嘉到任谒诸庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243620")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243620_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243620'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243620'>吏以命綍，假守是邦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243620_comment'></div>神以典祀，森卫此境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243620_comment'></div>惟神与吏皆食于民，厥职交修，是为无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243620_comment'></div>某谨以视事之始，祗祓进见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243620_comment'></div>所冀雨旸时若，时和岁丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243620_comment'></div>匪吏所能，繄神阴相。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1243620_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月</a>　在温州，因温州遭水灾，不即闻奏，王之望特降一官。后因捕海贼许大有功而免予追究。上谢表。作品：谢水灾免降官表。<div id='poem_1243300' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243300' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243300?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢水灾免降官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243300")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243300_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243300'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243300'>告灾敢缓，宜从必罚之科；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243300_comment'></div>宥过以宽，特反惟行之令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243300_comment'></div>拜章自劾，画旨报闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243300_comment'></div>惧剧履冰，感深漏网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243300_comment'></div>伏念臣性尤疏戆，老益眊昏，尚承乏于海邦，实虚糜于廪食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243300_comment'></div>顷者风潮之变，稍为秋稼之伤，曾弗预言，殊乖共理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243300_comment'></div>数马以策而迟其对，所以严事上之恭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243300_comment'></div>画蛇为足而败于成，盖欲条惠民之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243300_comment'></div>既素体忧勤之意，乃或稽疾苦之陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243300_comment'></div>顾镌秩以犹轻，何计功而幸免？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243300_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下仁同天覆，德与春温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243300_comment'></div>乐善无厌，虽微劳而必录；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243300_comment'></div>使臣以礼，非大故而不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243300_comment'></div>致令旷职之孤踪，得逭黜幽之重谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243300_comment'></div>臣敢不捐躯效报，没齿衔恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243300_comment'></div>罪不逃刑，当益励古人之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243300_comment'></div>退思补过，庶不贻明主之羞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1243300_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月</a>　在温州，因水灾上表自劾。作品：温州水灾放罪自劾奏札。<div id='poem_1243356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>温州水灾放罪自劾奏劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243356")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243356_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243356'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243356'>臣今月十九日准尚书省劄子，勘会已降指挥，温、台州近被水灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243356_comment'></div>逐州守臣王某、陈岩肖各不即闻奏，陈岩肖仍赈恤迟缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243356_comment'></div>王某特降一官，陈岩肖落职放罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243356_comment'></div>近台州申，获海贼首领毛大等五十七人，温州申获次首领许大等九十六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243356_comment'></div>十月十一日三省同奉圣旨，王某、陈岩肖各有捕贼之劳，以功赎过，特与放罪，前降指挥更不施行，内陈岩肖与宫观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243356_comment'></div>臣伏读训敕，感激涕流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243356_comment'></div>臣误蒙圣恩，畀以便郡，政事乖剌，荐至天灾，不能即以上闻，罪在不赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243356_comment'></div>况臣尝侍帷幄，深识圣主勤恤民隐，亟欲知四方疾苦之心，宜与它郡守不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243356_comment'></div>而老病之馀，悖眊如此，陛下何赖焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243356_comment'></div>考实论情，合加重谴，乃从末减，恐未足以压服公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243356_comment'></div>若以捕获海贼，功过相除，自是明见千里之外，创置水寨及将士用命所致，臣何力之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243356_comment'></div>正使建明其事，偶出于官，亦守臣常职，恶足以赎蔽灾之大过？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243356_comment'></div>黜官一秩，已为轻典，更加贷宥，何以示刑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243356_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特赐处分，将臣降官指挥依旧施行，仍从罢免，以为付委不效之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243356_comment'></div>其于陛下信赏必罚，综核名实之政，岂小补哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243356_comment'></div>臣无任惭惧战慄俯伏待罪之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243356_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1243356_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月</a>　在温州，又奏灾后措置事宜。作品：条奏温州水灾后措置事件奏议。<div id='poem_1243357' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243357' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243357?labeling=true' target='_blank'>条奏温州水灾后措置事件奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243357")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243357_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243357'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243357'>臣近睹邸报，臣僚劄子，自夏至秋，浙东一路濒海之郡三遭风水甚至，民间以木筏搬载，湍急之处庐舍飘荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243357_comment'></div>禾稼不以早晚，或秀而未实，或实而未收，浸淫损害，所馀亡几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243357_comment'></div>在法，水伤去处差官检视，蠲减田租以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243357_comment'></div>州县之吏恐为己累，懵不加恤，惟惧朝廷之得闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243357_comment'></div>欲望先委浙东监司及诸郡守臣，询问著实被水去处，分差清强官检视，定其高下，减免租税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243357_comment'></div>并行下诸路监司郡守觉察，或有灾伤，先期从实奏上，庶几不敢欺隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243357_comment'></div>奉圣旨依奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243357_comment'></div>续于今月十四日转运副使刘敏士到州，布宣德音，体访委曲，过于优恤，惠利有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243357_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下忧民救灾之诚，至深至厚，恩泽所施，孰不鼓舞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243357_comment'></div>然浙东七郡，其四濒海，被灾轻重各有等差，不皆如臣僚劄子所言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243357_comment'></div>臣先呼集诸县知县赴州，亲加审问，皆云损伤不多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243357_comment'></div>其人素皆爱民，非喜为掊剋者，所言可信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243357_comment'></div>又戒更切询究，不得抑遏人户状词，各皆遵禀而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243357_comment'></div>既是损伤不多，则检踏蠲放合依条限，难以前期张皇申奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243357_comment'></div>至于讲求荒政，固已预为堤备，大抵于成法之外，更务宽假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243357_comment'></div>此皆守臣职分之常，其所设施，何敢一一溷渎朝听？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243357_comment'></div>陛下抚养黎庶，视之如子，每闻疾苦，宵旰轸怀，临遣漕臣，躬行按视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243357_comment'></div>此尧舜之用心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243357_comment'></div>臣岂容隐默，略无陈述？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243357_comment'></div>谨具本州风水后措置事件，编成一册，缮写投进以闻，庶几上宽宸虑，少副综核之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243357_comment'></div>伏乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1243357_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月</a>　在温州。十月下旬，上火灾降黜奏议。作品：温州遗火乞赐降黜奏札。<div id='poem_1243355' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243355' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243355?labeling=true' target='_blank'>温州遗火乞赐降黜奏劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243355")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243355_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243355'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243355'>臣契勘本州自今月十七日西北风大起，遂预作准备，点检防火之具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243355_comment'></div>十九日风甚，巳时新河南界居民叶八家火发，烟焰所冲，六处并起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243355_comment'></div>臣与通判赵不流躬诣火势猛处救应，分遣诸头项军兵百姓并力向前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243355_comment'></div>至未时扑灭，烧过民居三百七十一家，茅瓦屋相间约计六百二十馀间，并岑山尼院一所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243355_comment'></div>是夜二更后，城外南乡居民遗火，亦即时救灭，烧一十五家，计二十间，并系茅屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243355_comment'></div>臣等朝夕巡警，浇泼馀烬，不敢少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243355_comment'></div>翌日风势依前猛急，至未时市东界杜秀家火发，五处俱作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243355_comment'></div>臣等又如昨日极力救护，至酉时扑灭，烧过民居六百七十三家，茅瓦屋相间约计一千一百七十馀间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243355_comment'></div>龙兴宫、开元观、嘉福院，并当风头，不容拆救，内龙兴宫有市舶务一所，并皆焚毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243355_comment'></div>飞火出城南，烧却民居七十家，及造船营一所五十六家，计草屋一百四十二间，打造未成粮船四只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243355_comment'></div>除此之外，两日所烧别不曾延及仓场、库务、官司屋宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243355_comment'></div>臣守郡无政，天降之灾，大火继作，祸及民庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243355_comment'></div>按绍兴敕：「诸在州失火，都监即时救扑，通判监督，违者杖八十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243355_comment'></div>虽即救扑监督，而延烧官私舍宅二百间以上<span class='inlineComment2'>（芦竹版屋三间比一间。）</span>，都监、通判杖六十，仍奏裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243355_comment'></div>三百间以上，知州准此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243355_comment'></div>臣身忝守臣，无所逃责，见行待罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243355_comment'></div>伏望圣慈重赐降黜，以为州郡不职，致灾之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243355_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243355_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1243355'>〔小签〕臣契勘本州居民约计万数千家，寺观四十所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243355_comment'></div>今两日所烧，共一千一百八十五家，茅屋相间计一千九百五十馀间，寺观四所，大抵几灾及十分之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243355_comment'></div>而官司廨宇与仓库务、军兵营垒，除市舶务与造船营外，并皆无虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243355_comment'></div>寻常州郡被火，缘于敕有奏裁之文，往往减削人户间架以避责罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243355_comment'></div>臣今不敢隐漏，尽行供具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243355_comment'></div>计其延烧之数，罪戾非轻，然通判而下皆极力救护，故虽风势猛盛，一两时间便得熄火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243355_comment'></div>伏望圣慈但将守臣重作行遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243355_comment'></div>臣甘从谴戮，不敢有词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243355_comment'></div>伏候敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243355_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1243355'>臣契勘本州从来多有火灾，每数年间辄一作，动焚数千百家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243355_comment'></div>盖缘并海多西北风，而屋邑繁隘，茅瓦相间，以致易为延烧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243355_comment'></div>臣自到官，常以为虑，而习俗滋久，难与虑患，若先事更革，必以为扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243355_comment'></div>今遭此一爇，遂得大为之防，以修火政，庶为后日之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243355_comment'></div>伏乞睿照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243355_comment'></div>臣自本州遭火之后，即刷贫乏被火人户，计口给粮赈济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243355_comment'></div>又为措置材瓦之类，彻茅蓬舍宇，增置救火器具，及部勒官军，预为区处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243355_comment'></div>不敢一一条上，伏乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1243355_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年11月15日</a>　在温州，言者论王之望坐视火灾，被放罢。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
台州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f19f3b84ba2a42258e25f084ccb3f34e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f19f3b84ba2a42258e25f084ccb3f34e");'><span id='f19f3b84ba2a42258e25f084ccb3f34e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1137')">1132-1137年</a>，29-34岁</div><div id='f19f3b84ba2a42258e25f084ccb3f34e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　居台州。在台州荫补为官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　监台州盐仓，安家与台州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年1月5日</a>　居台州，有感作《留穷文》<div id='poem_1243624' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243624' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243624?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留穷文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年1月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243624")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243624_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243624'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243624'>癸丑之孟春五日壬子，晨起，倦而假寐，见五怪物歘然俱至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243624_comment'></div>衣裳蓝缕，容色枯悴，耸肩拳脊，反耳昂鼻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243624_comment'></div>行步伛偻，仅有声气，咿嘤而言，意若忿戾，曰：「我乃子之穷鬼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243624_comment'></div>吾与子游，今三十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243624_comment'></div>子在孩提，我矜我怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243624_comment'></div>及子稍长，戏游蹁跹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243624_comment'></div>子能读书，佐子精研。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243624_comment'></div>艰难辛苦，不尔弃捐，望尔有成，报我周旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243624_comment'></div>事乃大谬，百无一然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243624_comment'></div>子年日长，子穷日炽，流离困阨，无复生意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243624_comment'></div>半生应举，无所识拔，易耨深耕，种而不刈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243624_comment'></div>偶得一官，日望其禄，不才无庸，所向墙谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243624_comment'></div>缨冠束发，号称曰儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243624_comment'></div>不获其利，苟得有馀，人皆为之，尔独不屑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243624_comment'></div>朝不及夕，期彼岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243624_comment'></div>尔子尔妻，仰尔以丰，吟饥呻寒，我耳为聋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243624_comment'></div>人皆愉愉，尔独闷闷，使我见子，无疾而病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243624_comment'></div>凡子之穷，不可殚论，有目未睹，有耳未闻：酿酒成醯，炊饭成糜，投鼠中器，误刀断机，卖浆遇寒，曝麦逢雨，渡水覆舟，执爨焚宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243624_comment'></div>不惟自穷，而更及旁，逢子者困，见子者殃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243624_comment'></div>洞庭之波，淼㳽无垠，子渴欲饮，九渊生尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243624_comment'></div>太仓之粟，川停岳峙，子饥取食，百万扫地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243624_comment'></div>我以穷故，依人而行，子穷若此，我何赖焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243624_comment'></div>逝将去汝，岂无他人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243624_comment'></div>结侣贪魃，缔交钱神，肉食锦衣，以终馀龄，安能百年，与子长勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243624_comment'></div>念子久游，不忍无言，一告而别，子其勉旃」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243624_comment'></div>王子于是骇然莫测，默然内愧，徐抽其端，缓颊以对：「吾读韩子，久闻尔名，谓子有知，庶几神灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243624_comment'></div>子则不然，憎贫弃旧，我不尔驱，尔顾我咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243624_comment'></div>凡人之生，各有定分，贵贱穷达，造物所命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243624_comment'></div>天生我穷，令与子俦，命实为之，汝安归尤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243624_comment'></div>物极必反，否泰相缪，吾穷久矣，庶其有瘳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243624_comment'></div>子姑少安，岂无报酬？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243624_comment'></div>何遽戚戚，于我而不留也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243624_comment'></div>富者则慕，贫者则去，被此名也，人谁汝顾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243624_comment'></div>子其改图，毋苦仓遽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243624_comment'></div>穷鬼闻此，顾嗟流涕，且悲且惭，释憾相谓：「人皆送我，尔独不屑，命也奈何，况此厚意，永为金石，有死无替」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1243624_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　居台州，始识吴芾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　居台州。吕颐浩罢相归临海，王之望上书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>　居台州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　寓台州期间，为台州普安禅寺重修作记。作品：台州重修普安禅寺记。<div id='poem_1243586' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243586' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243586?labeling=true' target='_blank'>台州重修普安禅寺记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243586")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243586_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243586'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243586'>出临海郡治之西四十五里曰宝藏岩，众山环合，一峰特秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243586_comment'></div>有古招提，相传权舆于萧梁之世，旧为安众院，治平中改赐今额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243586_comment'></div>其为十方，以长老住持久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243586_comment'></div>睦寇之乱，焚圮赤地，历数代十有馀年，颇复兴葺，而院小力薄，当往来之交，日不暇给，趣过目前，讫无前功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243586_comment'></div>绍兴阏逢摄提格之岁，故丞相高平范公过之，慨然以语郡守睢阳刘公棐曰：「物之废兴系其人，公盍择所授，庶可复乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243586_comment'></div>于是选于丛林，以保宁玑之子彦筠主之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243586_comment'></div>筠游方罢参，众推耆宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243586_comment'></div>至则因残就窘，左支右补，俾住者安居，游者饱食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243586_comment'></div>然后斥其赢馀，助以檀施，次第建立，不亟不徐，饰故创新，以底于大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243586_comment'></div>库有司，众有寮，爨有厨，浴有室，安僧说法各有堂宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243586_comment'></div>而佛殿岿然居中，三门两庑，旁带前揖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243586_comment'></div>荒基替址复为宝坊，斋钟粥鱼铿隐林壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243586_comment'></div>师曰：「吾院具矣，然山号宝藏，而经龛梵庋阙焉不设，名实不相副」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243586_comment'></div>乃书抵泸南帅冯公楫，得经五千四十八卷，规为转轮大藏，中栖千函，外覆大屋，学者恣取观之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243586_comment'></div>裒其施入，用佐供馈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243586_comment'></div>一日，其徒来告曰：「师之为勤矣，劳身苦思，垂二十年乃克成，而未有纪述，惜其远且无传，敢以为请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243586_comment'></div>予旧与筠游，其始来兹山，谓予曰：「刹无大小，顾为之如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243586_comment'></div>古人住山，披茨棘，蹈虎虺，孤坐岩谷，依草木而食其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243586_comment'></div>徒属从之，赘聚其旁，苫盖茅草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243586_comment'></div>及道孚而化行，来者益多，则稍稍栋宇，以渐至于华大，后人安享之，谓是固然，而不知厥初之艰勤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243586_comment'></div>夫利人之资而享其逸，孰则不能？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243586_comment'></div>今吾刹虽隳敝之馀，不犹愈乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243586_comment'></div>姑置吾力焉，奚忧弗集」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243586_comment'></div>予疑其落落难合，及今而信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243586_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243586_comment'></div>筠可谓克践其言者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243586_comment'></div>予乐其志之有成，又喜其不予欺也，故书俾刻之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1243586_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年8月</a>　范宗尹卒，王之望为文悼之。作品：祭范丞相文。<div id='poem_1243595' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243595' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243595?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭范相文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243595")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243595_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243595'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243595'>凤凰麒麟，千载一出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243595_comment'></div>卿云呈霄，俄顷灭没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243595_comment'></div>猗嗟我公，希世之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243595_comment'></div>命之不延，天啬其龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243595_comment'></div>惟公少时，豪气凌云，射策丹陛，名高刘蕡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243595_comment'></div>及在台谏，大体则争，不屑细碎，言重阳城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243595_comment'></div>靖康之末，天降祸灾，馀分窃位，代邸未来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243595_comment'></div>公勤濡足，起振其颓，首发大义，群言莫回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243595_comment'></div>复政长乐，大义克谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243595_comment'></div>功在生灵，口不自媒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243595_comment'></div>谤书虽入，金縢自开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243595_comment'></div>起公江湖，置公宪府，亟参大政，遂相明主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243595_comment'></div>独运庙堂，折冲樽俎，如山不动，内镇外御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243595_comment'></div>军书交驰，羽檄旁午，公居其间，从容笑语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243595_comment'></div>盗遍海内，敌临江浒，公相一年，天下安堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243595_comment'></div>一言不合，公遂勇退，帝岂不怀，公方壮岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243595_comment'></div>期公百年，社稷永赖，方壮而殒，出于意外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243595_comment'></div>寿少马周，年减如晦，人之云亡，邦国殄瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243595_comment'></div>惟我小子，早辱公知，爱等兄弟，恩均父师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243595_comment'></div>悲欢离合，二纪于兹，我困蜀汉，公罢鼎司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243595_comment'></div>携孥跃屩，万里来归，贫贱之交，弗渝故时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243595_comment'></div>口借其誉，心恤其私，饥食公食，寒衣公衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243595_comment'></div>脱我沟壑，繄公不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243595_comment'></div>谓当久久，从公以嬉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243595_comment'></div>云胡不淑，哲人其萎，山倾海竭，鱼鸟何依？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243595_comment'></div>西州路绝，东阁人稀，醴酒不设，繐帐空垂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243595_comment'></div>今其已矣，尚忍言之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243595_comment'></div>殽羞既陈，清酒盈卮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243595_comment'></div>想公平生，恍如在斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243595_comment'></div>音容不接，泣涕涟洏，抚棺一恸，终天永辞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1243595_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='5325c55ebf944849b9839a473d0c1a5b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5325c55ebf944849b9839a473d0c1a5b");'><span id='5325c55ebf944849b9839a473d0c1a5b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>，46岁</div><div id='5325c55ebf944849b9839a473d0c1a5b' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在台州。与台州通判石延庆游。有词。延庆满秩去官，王之望送之。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在台州，作石延庆墓志铭。作品：故左朝请郎石君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1243592' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243592' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243592?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故左朝请郎石君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十九年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243592")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243592_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243592'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243592'>绍兴十九年夏六月庚申，通判台州石君满秩去官，郡之士大夫与四方之寄寓者燕饯阅月，祖送倾城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243592_comment'></div>予与送君西郊，慷慨言别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243592_comment'></div>后二十馀日，闻君病，未几讣至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243592_comment'></div>凡前之送客，相与惊悼流涕，且忧其贫，无以举大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243592_comment'></div>既数月，其孤纯臣以书与行状来，曰：「葬谨具，惟志诸葬者未有其词，丈人其为之铭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243592_comment'></div>予惟君之旧与其孤之志，悲且怜之，义不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243592_comment'></div>按卫康叔七世孙靖伯食采于石，后以为氏，碏书《春秋》，汉万石君以孝谨显，厥宗遂大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243592_comment'></div>永嘉之乱，曰举南渡，为建安太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243592_comment'></div>子孙散处吴越，或家于会稽之新昌，枝叶蕃盛，为东南望族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243592_comment'></div>君曾大父讳象之，官至太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243592_comment'></div>盛年挂冠，自丞相潞国文公而下皆有诗送行，优游丘园四十馀年以卒，其潜德懿行见于清献赵公之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243592_comment'></div>大父讳景勋，隐逸不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243592_comment'></div>父讳师圣，有声场屋，赠右朝奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243592_comment'></div>母韦氏，赠宜人，左朝议大夫、知明州、累赠特进骧之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243592_comment'></div>君讳延庆，字光锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243592_comment'></div>六岁而孤，自知力学，颖悟绝人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243592_comment'></div>既长，遂工文词，应乡举第一，登绍兴二年进士第，授左迪功郎、容州司户参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243592_comment'></div>未赴，试中教官，改明州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243592_comment'></div>又中博学宏词科，授左修职郎，终更授左从政郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243592_comment'></div>入为详定一司敕令所删定官，改左宣教郎，充诸王宫大小学教授，兼亲贤宅讲书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243592_comment'></div>宗祀明堂，辟提点事务司干办官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243592_comment'></div>永祐因山，总护使辟掌笺表，寻除国子监丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243592_comment'></div>言者论其常见执政私第，叱其典谒，出，添差通判台州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243592_comment'></div>以赏典年劳，累官至左朝请郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243592_comment'></div>去台感末疾，请致仕，未报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243592_comment'></div>秋七月辛巳卒于新昌，享年四十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243592_comment'></div>远近来赴，哭之皆哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243592_comment'></div>冬十二月庚申葬于嵊县剡山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243592_comment'></div>君伉爽磊落，襟抱夷旷，嗜酒爱客，雅有风味，杯觞流行，沈酣笑歌，怡然放怀，不屑缰锁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243592_comment'></div>见之者无不心开意豁，忘戚戚拘窘之态，以故人多喜其为人，识与不识皆字之曰光锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243592_comment'></div>尤乐赒人之急，仓卒扣门，未尝以有无为解，吉凶不能振者辄身任之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243592_comment'></div>舅寿卿官会稽，举郡厉疫死者相枕藉，莫敢过门，君躬自调护，宿食其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243592_comment'></div>人或止之，笑曰死生命也，一无嫌惮之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243592_comment'></div>其所为类如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243592_comment'></div>四明更兵火后，学宫不葺，君请而新之，泮宫之制始备，生徒沓来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243592_comment'></div>遂举乡饮之礼，明酬酢降登揖拜之节，考订甚详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243592_comment'></div>后朝廷取其法颁之天下，三岁一行，以为定式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243592_comment'></div>岁在癸亥，始建郊丘临安，君因面对，乞备五辂以严禋祀，从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243592_comment'></div>自翠华南巡，仪物草创，大驾卤簿至是赫然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243592_comment'></div>君平时脱略细谨，咸以为不羁之才，及论议设施，皆大典礼，人始知其不可量也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243592_comment'></div>素不历州县，而临海之政详练敏达，辅以儒雅，士民安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243592_comment'></div>与其兄嗣庆笃相友爱，兄守江阴，卒于官，奔哭护丧，奉祀极力，事嫠抚孤，甚有恩惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243592_comment'></div>当世英俊多与之游，俸稍所得，索于宾客，身后无儋石之储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243592_comment'></div>浙东诸司俱治会稽，协力经纪其家，养生送死，始赖以济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1243592_comment'></div>君之素行由是愈彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1243592_comment'></div>君之旧名袭庆，集英唱第，改赐今名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1243592_comment'></div>娶同郡郑氏，封安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1243592_comment'></div>三男，曰纯臣、纯孝、纯行，皆传父业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1243592_comment'></div>女二人尚处，长许嫁右迪功郎处州青田尉陈达善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1243592_comment'></div>自中兴以来，连取三科者惟君一人，人物秀一时，声名藉藉，众望且大显，虽君亦自负，而止于此，庶几裕其后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1243592_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_1243592'>石宗渡江，蕃于新昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1243592_comment'></div>厥材如林，杞梓豫章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1243592_comment'></div>猗欤光锡，实惟其良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1243592_comment'></div>连掇三科，英声洋洋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1243592_comment'></div>兴举坠典，礼文有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1243592_comment'></div>青冥铩翮，厥飞不扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1243592_comment'></div>以位准才，十未一偿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1243592_comment'></div>呜呼弗延，惟命之伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1243592_comment'></div>琢铭坚石，永閟幽藏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1243592_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f83892140b94401c9adad7b36257c2e8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f83892140b94401c9adad7b36257c2e8");'><span id='f83892140b94401c9adad7b36257c2e8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1171')">1170-1171年</a>，67-68岁</div><div id='f83892140b94401c9adad7b36257c2e8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　在台州。冬，疾作。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年2月10日</a>　在台州，卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年4月</a>　在台州，赠左宣奉大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年12月6日</a>　在台州，葬于临海县。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='407820a5e3744eb1a5aadd8b8942badd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("407820a5e3744eb1a5aadd8b8942badd");'><span id='407820a5e3744eb1a5aadd8b8942badd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1141')">1138-1141年</a>，35-38岁</div><div id='407820a5e3744eb1a5aadd8b8942badd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　在临安。进士及第。上谢启。作品：谢及第启。<div id='poem_1243432' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243432' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243432?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢及第启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243432")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243432_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243432'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243432'>阶任子之恩，已更贱役；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243432_comment'></div>应兴贤之诏，复忝巍科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243432_comment'></div>循鄙分以非宜，抚疏才而自愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243432_comment'></div>窃以国家惟百年之计，留意人才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243432_comment'></div>学者以一日之长，致身科目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243432_comment'></div>凡彼公卿之蹊径，悉由文字以权舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243432_comment'></div>始类浮文，终收实用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243432_comment'></div>遂使清朝笃意，谓糊名较艺之足凭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243432_comment'></div>后进希声，以射策决科为可贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243432_comment'></div>故此艰难之际，亦严搜选之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243432_comment'></div>神州尚隔于一隅，江表自称为多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243432_comment'></div>虽未复限淮之地，亦不虚造榜之天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243432_comment'></div>方三祀之亮阴，肃九重而恭默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243432_comment'></div>龙池辍试，将权衡于近侍之臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243432_comment'></div>雁塔书名，等甲乙于春官之考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243432_comment'></div>训辞甚切，圣意有加，精求赋日之才，博采济时之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243432_comment'></div>谨其声律，盖将观组织之工；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243432_comment'></div>访以古今，所以考经纶之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243432_comment'></div>自非词兼众体，才擅数长，则何以副浚哲之旁求，处英贤之上列？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243432_comment'></div>如某者衣冠寒族，庠序晚生，无博观广览之资，有孤陋寡闻之累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243432_comment'></div>专心弱岁，功书剑以徒劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243432_comment'></div>刻意前修，佩韦弦而自饬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243432_comment'></div>妄起功名之意，早游教化之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243432_comment'></div>博士一经，生徒数载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243432_comment'></div>月程文艺，屡收得隽之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243432_comment'></div>秋试贤能，亦在先鸣之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243432_comment'></div>自诡穿杨之审，不知拾芥之难，龙门未跃于西河，鲸鬣遂掀于东海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243432_comment'></div>合繻以出，弹铗而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243432_comment'></div>继缠风树之悲，无复星槎之兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243432_comment'></div>十年兵火，脱盗贼于中原；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243432_comment'></div>万里风波，从衣冠而南渡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243432_comment'></div>讲道于绝粮之际，谈经于弛担之馀，素患难以安行，尝艰险而已备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243432_comment'></div>偶缘世赏，获厕官联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243432_comment'></div>铁消铸砚之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243432_comment'></div>金负满籯之训，绝意冥鸿之寥廓，甘心斥鴳之翱翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243432_comment'></div>然素业传家，惧弓冶箕裘之堕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243432_comment'></div>青衫入仕，有尘埃箠楚之羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243432_comment'></div>痛自激昂，载加勉励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243432_comment'></div>家无文史，重兴五厄之嗟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243432_comment'></div>官有簿书，更苦三馀之窘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243432_comment'></div>心耗于囊中之句，目昏于檠下之书，过时已觉于难成，中道几思于自画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243432_comment'></div>向用朝廷之事比，许还首善之荐名，来求礼部之选抡，偶犯有司之程度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243432_comment'></div>霜蹄遂蹶，剑气空呈，复垂翅于回溪，独倚辀于虞阪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243432_comment'></div>功同猿臂，疑骨相之难封；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1243432_comment'></div>命肖龙章，恨神仙之多障。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1243432_comment'></div>有求弗获，欲罢不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1243432_comment'></div>属诏綍之肆颁，励辞锋而再鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1243432_comment'></div>既与漕台之计，复观王国之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1243432_comment'></div>朋来集四海之英，颖出尽一时之秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1243432_comment'></div>时方用赋，皆升堂入室之流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1243432_comment'></div>士必通经，多专门名家之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1243432_comment'></div>玉有荆山之韫，珠无沧海之遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1243432_comment'></div>可谓盛哉，吁足畏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1243432_comment'></div>方锱铢之必较，忽糠秕以居前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1243432_comment'></div>然而求剑刻舟，守旧方而甚滞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1243432_comment'></div>好竽鼓瑟，追时尚以尤疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1243432_comment'></div>文或病其雕虫，技几成于画虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1243432_comment'></div>既瑕瑜之不掩，宜葑菲之俱遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1243432_comment'></div>何图骫骳之词，犹玷公明之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1243432_comment'></div>人非东晋，莫与刘琰之流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1243432_comment'></div>赋异《阿房》，终居杜牧之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1243432_comment'></div>尚次甲科之后，获尘乙夜之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1243432_comment'></div>自揣奇穷，已为侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1243432_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官才高人杰，道契天民，以兼资文武之才，膺注意安危之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1243432_comment'></div>计存庙社，威名独重于朝端；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1243432_comment'></div>位冠臣邻，风采想闻于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1243432_comment'></div>久持魁柄，力运化枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1243432_comment'></div>折遐冲于敌人窥伺之秋，镇雅俗于国势危疑之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1243432_comment'></div>临大事而不乱，盖胸中之气有馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1243432_comment'></div>推至公而必行，故宇内之心自服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1243432_comment'></div>国有中兴之渐，士无先识之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1243432_comment'></div>致此庸虚，有兹叨冒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1243432_comment'></div>某敢不益崇儒行，勉服官箴，随所遇于他时，期粗伸于素志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1243432_comment'></div>被君相作人之泽，虽匪成才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1243432_comment'></div>师圣贤行己之方，则为报德。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1243432_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　在临安。进士及第。上谢宰相书。作品：上宰相书（某闻唐虞之道）<div id='poem_1243401' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243401' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243401?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上宰相书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243401")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243401_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243401'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243401'>某闻唐虞之道、孔孟之学、皋夔稷契之事业，初非二物，如冶金锡以为器用，烹羊豕以为膳羞，本末虽殊，其实一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243401_comment'></div>《书》称尧、舜、禹、皋陶之为人，皆曰「稽古」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243401_comment'></div>伊尹乐道畎亩，起而相汤，格于皇天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243401_comment'></div>后世不知道为何物，不知学为何事，稽古之烈、格天之勋，判为二涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243401_comment'></div>其间亦有豪杰之士因时乘变，能成就其功名者，然考之圣贤之事业，终无黼黻宫商之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243401_comment'></div>《易》曰「一阴一阳之谓道」，推而至于富有之大业，日新之盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243401_comment'></div>又曰「形而上者谓之道，形而下者谓之器」，继之以化而裁之之变、推而行之之通、举而措之之事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243401_comment'></div>阴阳者物所由生，形器者事所从出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243401_comment'></div>道兼阴阳，冒形器则凡天下之事物幽明巨细，动静出入，变化云为，万殊不齐，孰有能外此者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243401_comment'></div>浚其源而流自清，挈其本而末自举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243401_comment'></div>故业大而富有，德盛而日新，变通至于不穷，而事业著乎天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243401_comment'></div>此圣人经纶之极致，非浮虚无用之空言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243401_comment'></div>《乾》之九二以利见之资处人臣之至，盛德博而化天下文明，孔子翼之曰「学以聚之，问以辨之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243401_comment'></div>聚者聚此者也，辨者辨此者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243401_comment'></div>傅说之诲高宗亦曰：「王人求多闻，时惟建事，学于古训，乃有获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243401_comment'></div>允怀于兹道，积于厥躬」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243401_comment'></div>由是言之，经世者必以道，致道者必由学，所得有浅深，则所发有大小，顾其渊源为何如耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243401_comment'></div>恭惟某官道为王佐，学为帝师，所以治其心、养其性、齐家治国者，粹然一出于六经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243401_comment'></div>蓄而为德，则刚健笃实，极乎辉光之盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243401_comment'></div>发而为文，则纯正简古，合乎典谟之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243401_comment'></div>曾参之忠恕、孟轲之刚大、子思之中庸，贯为一条，诚明白而自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243401_comment'></div>虽功盖一世，贵穷人爵，于书无所不通，于理无所不阅，而机政之外犹皇皇焉如不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243401_comment'></div>其终始典于学，自周公而来，未见其比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243401_comment'></div>故能智先著龟，节冠古今，信行蛮貊，勇过贲育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243401_comment'></div>赴危难而不慑，历困厄而不挫，临机会而不疑，入纷纠而不乱，享天下之富贵而不淫，极天下之功名而不骄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243401_comment'></div>始焉以天下非之，漠然如无闻于耳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243401_comment'></div>少焉以天下誉之，泛然若无介于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243401_comment'></div>此无他，有道于此，足以制事物于冥冥之中，而不为事物之所制焉故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243401_comment'></div>然则天下之事业有尽，而相公之学术无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243401_comment'></div>其功德之已陈于天下者，特因事而应之者耳，事之未来、应之未出者，天下恶足而知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243401_comment'></div>譬之泰山出云，人见其氤氲变化，合散万端，不崇朝而遍雨天下，以为至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243401_comment'></div>而不知精华亭毒之气蓄于中而未出者，多于见乎其外者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243401_comment'></div>某襄汉之鄙人，幼志于学，行年四十，未闻大道，何足以仰窥盛德之万一？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243401_comment'></div>抑闻达巷党人以里巷之流一见仲尼，喟然叹曰：「大哉孔子！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243401_comment'></div>博学而无所成名」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243401_comment'></div>著于《论语》，天下至今诵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243401_comment'></div>某虽不肖，托于钧播有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243401_comment'></div>岁在戊午，初忝科第，两蒙呼召，获顾盼于稠人之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243401_comment'></div>今兹改官，又承借重诸公，猥赐收录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243401_comment'></div>比之孔门，虽不足与高弟齿，至自附于达巷之党人，则称夫子之大不为过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243401_comment'></div>虽然，董仲舒以达巷党人为不学而自知，盖资质之美有绝人者，使留受业于门，则其于高弟亦庶几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243401_comment'></div>惜乎不知出此一言之外，后世无传焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243401_comment'></div>若某者，资质不及，而好学之心自谓过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243401_comment'></div>诚得朝夕门墙之下，益闻见其所未尝，则他日所得于相公之道，必又有深于此者，不止于一言而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1243401_comment'></div>不识相公果能收之否乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1243401_comment'></div>小子不敢自幸，谨献所为文一编，辱赐览观，或有可采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1243401_comment'></div>冒渎钧严，战慄无地。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1243401_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　在临安。有诗投递座主张致远。作品：投座主张子猷给事。<div id='poem_66600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_66600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/66600?labeling=true' target='_blank'>投座主张子猷给事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_66600")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_66600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_66600'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_66600'>东风入雕槛，百卉无不花。<div id='poem_sentence_0_66600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_66600'>一经造化手，各若矜春华。<div id='poem_sentence_1_66600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_66600'>主人最好事，护养从萌芽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_66600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_66600'>浇灌与封植，恩光无等差。<div id='poem_sentence_3_66600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_66600'>其间一本尤所喜，欲售千金贵无比。<div id='poem_sentence_4_66600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_66600'>君不见洛阳好事丞相家，曾剪姚黄贡天子。<div id='poem_sentence_5_66600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_66600'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_66600_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　在临安。有诗投递魏侍郎。作品：登第后投魏侍郎。<div id='poem_66619' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_66619' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/66619?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登第后投魏侍郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_66619")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_66619_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_66619'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_66619'>空山学仙子，旧识安期生。<div id='poem_sentence_0_66619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_66619'>青霄许相接，凡骨难为轻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_66619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_66619'>一朝行业满，九转丹砂成。<div id='poem_sentence_2_66619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_66619'>安期忽东来，从帝游玉京。<div id='poem_sentence_3_66619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_66619'>下视一笑莞，依然有馀情。<div id='poem_sentence_4_66619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_66619'>借我白云车，导以虹蜺旌。<div id='poem_sentence_5_66619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_66619'>摄身出尘土，随君凌紫清。<div id='poem_sentence_6_66619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_66619'>机会倘一失，千载何由丁。<div id='poem_sentence_7_66619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_66619'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_66619_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年10月</a>　在临安。上书孙近。作品：上孙承旨启。<div id='poem_1243433' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243433' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243433?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上孙承旨启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243433")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243433_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243433'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243433'>光奉制书，复登翰苑，承中禁几微之旨，冠内朝清切之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243433_comment'></div>传闻四遐，耸动群听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243433_comment'></div>窃以北门待诏，专取文章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243433_comment'></div>东阁别居，必推年德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243433_comment'></div>将相相望于前世，官资不计于同僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243433_comment'></div>在中朝熙洽之时，特为荣遇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243433_comment'></div>逮南渡艰难之后，无复常员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243433_comment'></div>自非大用之资，曷副久虚之选？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243433_comment'></div>恭惟某官斯文哲匠，当代耆英，疏通既禀于天资，练达尤深于世务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243433_comment'></div>清涂扬历，阅岁月于三朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243433_comment'></div>绝域征行，冒风霜于万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243433_comment'></div>夷险不渝于一节，身名由是以俱荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243433_comment'></div>入掌丝纶，出专斧钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243433_comment'></div>诏令继两京之作，威权侔二陕之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243433_comment'></div>属睿哲之求贤，思老成而共政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243433_comment'></div>锋车驰召，屡趣舍人之装；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243433_comment'></div>黼座对扬，遂前天子之席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243433_comment'></div>方今台阶未备，政路多虚，济时实藉于真才，注意允归于旧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243433_comment'></div>名书案上，闻宸翰之亲题；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243433_comment'></div>礼绝座中，有禁林之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243433_comment'></div>某叨蒙慰荐，粗识依归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243433_comment'></div>峻比龙门，已滥登于贱迹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243433_comment'></div>成同燕厦，惟窃贺于私心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1243433_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年11月</a>　在汴京。有启贺孙近除参知政事。作品：贺孙参政启。<div id='poem_1243434' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243434' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243434?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺孙参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243434")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243434_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243434'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243434'>进用真儒，入参大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243434_comment'></div>纶言诞布，隐然国势之隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243434_comment'></div>舆论佥谐，赫尔民瞻之峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243434_comment'></div>庇庥所及，庆抃交深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243434_comment'></div>窃观前世之兴衰，皆系大臣之能否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243434_comment'></div>诚得贤辅，必收隽功，未有用无奇之人，而可办非常之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243434_comment'></div>又况圣哲驰骛之日，非如国家閒暇之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243434_comment'></div>宗庙社稷之安危，动关举措；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243434_comment'></div>钱谷甲兵之繁冗，密备咨询。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243434_comment'></div>自非希世之才，曷展经邦之略？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243434_comment'></div>天厌祸乱，国登俊良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243434_comment'></div>恭惟某官道备弛张，学穷治忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243434_comment'></div>发为华藻，蔚乎两汉之文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243434_comment'></div>养以渊源，粹矣六经之蕴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243434_comment'></div>法律淹通于三尺，宪章练达于累朝，得其一长，已足名世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243434_comment'></div>至于大节，则又绝人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243434_comment'></div>曩勍敌之始通，择迩臣而往聘，敌心不测，物议交疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243434_comment'></div>方众人相视，莫敢请行之间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243434_comment'></div>独匹马徂征，出不反顾之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243434_comment'></div>信义行乎殊俗，忠勤简于清衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243434_comment'></div>位貌浸隆，宠灵甚渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243434_comment'></div>雍容玉帐，两专方岳之权；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243434_comment'></div>出入金銮，三奉禁林之直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243434_comment'></div>比载膺于图任，遂亟被于登庸，以将降大任之资，迪绍开中兴之烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243434_comment'></div>君臣同德，协际会于风云；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243434_comment'></div>中外倾心，望升平于期月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243434_comment'></div>某受知特达，闻命欣愉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243434_comment'></div>颂圣主之得贤臣，愧无妙语；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243434_comment'></div>以儒宗而居相位，更俟嘉音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243434_comment'></div>寒律方严，恩光尚远，期精加于调护，用宏济于艰难。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1243434_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　在临安。蒙恩赐第，改授左官。有启谢孙近举荐之力。作品：谢孙参政举改官启。<div id='poem_1243439' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243439' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243439?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢孙参政举改官启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243439")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243439_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243439'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243439'>辟铸颜之冶，久荷私恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243439_comment'></div>飞荐祢之章，复尘公举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243439_comment'></div>愚衷积感，弱质增荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243439_comment'></div>窃以辅政之臣，安危所系；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243439_comment'></div>举贤之任，出处惟均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243439_comment'></div>在朝则委以官人，去国而犹令进士，靡论中外，皆得荐扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243439_comment'></div>非如监司郡守之有拘，故所沾者广；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243439_comment'></div>加以祠官散员之许授，故欲得者多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243439_comment'></div>自非俊杰之材，不在题评之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243439_comment'></div>如某者禀资最陋，赋命多奇，祈柳巧而莫酬，驱韩穷而不去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243439_comment'></div>小不能披坚执锐，奋身行阵之前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243439_comment'></div>大不能排难解纷，效力功名之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243439_comment'></div>徒耽末学，分作迂儒，陆沉一世之间，雌伏百僚之底。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243439_comment'></div>偶缘科第，滥处胶庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243439_comment'></div>坐客无毡，举家食粥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243439_comment'></div>诲诸生于馆下，每虞讥笑之兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243439_comment'></div>集三鳣于堂前，岂有升迁之望？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243439_comment'></div>敢期侥倖，忽被甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243439_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官盛德格天，嘉猷济世，欲大恢于相业，故广揽于人材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243439_comment'></div>粉泽帝图，有咸熙之庶绩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243439_comment'></div>镕陶士类，无不获之一夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243439_comment'></div>致使寒微，亦膺记录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243439_comment'></div>某敢不激昂气节，淬砺猷为！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243439_comment'></div>虽功名富贵以难期，庶用舍行藏之无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243439_comment'></div>鸡鸣狗盗，已叨下座之收；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243439_comment'></div>虫臂鼠肝，更赖大钧之播。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1243439_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　在临安。改授左官后，有祭父母文。作品：登第告考妣文。<div id='poem_1243602' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243602' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243602?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登第告考妣文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243602")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243602_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243602'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243602'>某爰自孤露，荐历艰苦，每遵先训，不敢废学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243602_comment'></div>乃今年旅试省闱，叨在第六，蒙恩赐第，改授左官，且有师儒之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243602_comment'></div>此皆先考妣积善馀庆，流于后人，故不肖之孤，克继绪业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243602_comment'></div>永惟罪逆，致身迟暮，虽窃一第，不及拜亲，感慕悲哀，痛贯心骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243602_comment'></div>但当谨奉遗体，恪守义方，思所以立身扬名，显我父母者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243602_comment'></div>恭陈薄荐，以告庙筵。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1243602_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年3月</a>　在临安。有启贺楼炤除签书枢密院事。作品：贺楼枢密启。<div id='poem_1243437' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243437' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243437?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺楼枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243437")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243437_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243437'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243437'>光膺宠綍，越执洪枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243437_comment'></div>居政府之严，隐如敌国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243437_comment'></div>使朝廷之势，安若泰山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243437_comment'></div>将士交欣，缙绅胥庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243437_comment'></div>窃以先王之制，兵刑出于一原；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243437_comment'></div>有国之经，文武号为二柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243437_comment'></div>掌其政令，宜在庙堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243437_comment'></div>逮军民之既分，致将相以异任，典戎事者罔陪于国论，代天工者弗与于兵权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243437_comment'></div>注意既殊，全功曷责？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243437_comment'></div>国家开重熙之景运，仍五季之旧章，爰建辅臣，以司兵本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243437_comment'></div>稽于古，实六卿司马之职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243437_comment'></div>考其官，盖三事大夫之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243437_comment'></div>地亚钧衡，谋专帷幄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243437_comment'></div>必得腹心之佐，始膺体貌之隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243437_comment'></div>矧今大难已平，中兴伊始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243437_comment'></div>虽干戈倒载，永无征战之虞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243437_comment'></div>而樽俎折冲，允藉威怀之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243437_comment'></div>自非上哲，曷副旁求？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243437_comment'></div>恭惟某官资粹诚明，学穷治忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243437_comment'></div>沈深大度，量莫见于津涯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243437_comment'></div>厚重寡言，色不形于喜愠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243437_comment'></div>凛凛万夫之望，堂堂千载之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243437_comment'></div>出入三朝，险夷一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243437_comment'></div>曩缘对境，许缔和盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243437_comment'></div>方善意之未孚，致群情之大扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243437_comment'></div>独奋蓍龟之见，赞成金石之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243437_comment'></div>朝陈悟主之一言，夕获和戎之五利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243437_comment'></div>宣帝纳呼韩之款，赖萧傅之通经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243437_comment'></div>太宗用房乔之谋，资杜公之善断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243437_comment'></div>俄跻近弼，出抚全秦，王侯咸授于指踪，封拜得专于承制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243437_comment'></div>释俘归敌，黠羌得其欢心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243437_comment'></div>罚罪赏功，诸将输于死力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243437_comment'></div>名闻草木，功在鼎钟，暨零雨以言旋，将作霖而是命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243437_comment'></div>俄轸劬劳之痛，稍稽考慎之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243437_comment'></div>甫免私艰，亟分阃寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243437_comment'></div>轻裘缓带，拥油幕以临藩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243437_comment'></div>淑旂绥章，趣锋车而入觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243437_comment'></div>嘉猷既告，睿眷弥隆，一开日月之明，再契风云之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243437_comment'></div>对贾谊于宣室，不问鬼神；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243437_comment'></div>留姚崇于渭滨，非由驰逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243437_comment'></div>遂复青毡之旧，进陪黄阁之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243437_comment'></div>硕德既升，太平可必。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243437_comment'></div>基命宥密，方摅庙算之奇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243437_comment'></div>畴咨登庸，行正台阶之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1243437_comment'></div>某夙希附骥，近获登龙，谬承特达之知，许借吹嘘之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1243437_comment'></div>扫门已晚，尚及曹参之在齐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1243437_comment'></div>结绶有因，喜见贡公之辅汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1243437_comment'></div>岂止系当时之轻重，盖尤关小民之戚休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1243437_comment'></div>望舟楫于江干，日迟行色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1243437_comment'></div>伺丝纶于毂下，侧听除音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1243437_comment'></div>成命忽传，欢悰曷既？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1243437_comment'></div>剡书荐墨，虽未腾北海之章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1243437_comment'></div>羁旅穷愁，宁久索东方之米！</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1243437_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在临安。有谢楼炤启。作品：谢楼枢密举改官启。<div id='poem_1243440' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243440' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243440?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢楼枢密举改官启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243440")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243440_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243440'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243440'>泮水育材，苟幸旷瘝之免；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243440_comment'></div>铨曹考课，冒膺秩序之更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243440_comment'></div>受命知惭，抚躬曷称？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243440_comment'></div>窃以黜陟幽明之典废，士始惰功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243440_comment'></div>综核名实之政衰，人斯滥进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243440_comment'></div>惟吏部改官之制，推本朝立法之严，积以锱铢，较以毫发，一言不应，累善无容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243440_comment'></div>倘小节之弗完，亦前功之尽废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243440_comment'></div>虽圣世于焉而得士，然奸胥或得以舞文，视赂贿之重轻，为行移之淹速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243440_comment'></div>故难于应格，喻同进士之登科；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243440_comment'></div>而计所输赀，至比富人之入粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243440_comment'></div>与于此者，不亦难哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243440_comment'></div>如某者太学陈人，中原冷族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243440_comment'></div>专心弱岁，绝尼父之韦编；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243440_comment'></div>刻意前修，纫屈平之兰佩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243440_comment'></div>早尘世赏，旋窃文科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243440_comment'></div>免从州县之游，猥玷师儒之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243440_comment'></div>董帷常下，马帐空悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243440_comment'></div>媚学有徒，冠履漫同于聚蚋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243440_comment'></div>好书成癖，简编殆类于蠹鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243440_comment'></div>玩华丹于法度之言，振鼓吹于京师之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243440_comment'></div>饭蔬饮水，乐亦在中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243440_comment'></div>乘马从徒，兹非其幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243440_comment'></div>博士虚縻于廪粟，广文何有于才名？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243440_comment'></div>逮此终更，敢希平进，忽因公举，得厕京联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243440_comment'></div>资品叙升，始正有官之号；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243440_comment'></div>岁时驯致，式阶通籍之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243440_comment'></div>侥倖若兹，夤缘有自。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243440_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官至诚乐善，伟度包荒，观其广揽于英才，盖欲大恢于贤业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243440_comment'></div>吹嘘不倦，无非有味之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243440_comment'></div>謦欬所加，便作知名之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243440_comment'></div>推毂每先于寒远，登门不间于故新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243440_comment'></div>虽云无用之资，亦借曲成之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243440_comment'></div>重念某与时龃龉，赋性疏庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243440_comment'></div>久处穷涂，分无长物，知匪蘋蘩之可荐，自甘桃李之无言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243440_comment'></div>比黉舍之三年，偶剡章之四上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243440_comment'></div>方浮图之尖未合，恐濩落之瓠无容，续正赖于鸾胶，弃有同于鸡肋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243440_comment'></div>辄输肺腑，用丐齿牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243440_comment'></div>不待先容，亟蒙重诺，箭俄飞于燕将，璧遂假于许田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243440_comment'></div>大厦将颠，功独资于一木；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243440_comment'></div>中流获济，赐何啻于千金？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243440_comment'></div>成此叨逾，悉由特达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243440_comment'></div>某敢不钦承至意，铭著乃心！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243440_comment'></div>儒有古人与稽，愿坚操履；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243440_comment'></div>士为知己者死，誓报恩私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1243440_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在临安。有启给楼炤。作品：通楼枢密启（扬清激浊）通楼枢密启（去公府之潭潭）<div id='poem_1243438' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243438' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243438?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通楼枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a
