href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243438")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243438_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243438'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243438'>扬清激浊，诚先达之高风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243438_comment'></div>出幽迁乔，亦后生之雅志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243438_comment'></div>欲赴功名之会，必由上下之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243438_comment'></div>若矜其位而矜其能，孰为之先而为之后？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243438_comment'></div>是固交相求而一致，岂容化于道而两忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243438_comment'></div>声气苟同，卑高曷间？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243438_comment'></div>所以附翼攀鳞之喻，著自圣门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243438_comment'></div>弹冠结绶之谈，誇乎信史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243438_comment'></div>绝足继腾于王路，清芬蔼著于遗编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243438_comment'></div>逮五交之衅既萌，致三适之功无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243438_comment'></div>上之人偷安富贵，弗忧英俊之沉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243438_comment'></div>下之人自负才猷，耻藉王侯之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243438_comment'></div>方圆不合，胡越相悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243438_comment'></div>魁奇卓荦者灭迹而无闻，谗谄阿谀者乘时而得肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243438_comment'></div>比周无愧，势利相先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243438_comment'></div>曲意取容，不但奴颜而婢膝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243438_comment'></div>抵巇竞进，有同人面而兽心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243438_comment'></div>贤才之路用堙，市道之风滋扇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243438_comment'></div>克敦薄俗，必属伟人，幸公道之有归，披鄙诚而自列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243438_comment'></div>伏念某衣冠寒族，庠序晚生，蹉跎踰不惑之年，连蹇抱数奇之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243438_comment'></div>贤关肄业，半生白首之经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243438_comment'></div>仕路抗颜，一纪红尘之吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243438_comment'></div>曩策名于桂籍，因滥吹于芹宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243438_comment'></div>坐客无毡，举家食粥，瘦马空存于六印，沈舟坐阅于千帆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243438_comment'></div>齿发摧颓，老先期而骤至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243438_comment'></div>声光湮没，世与我而相违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243438_comment'></div>安寂寞于冷官，分栖迟于选调，既异蘋蘩之可荐，甘同桃李之无言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243438_comment'></div>曷尝低欲就之头，未省摇乞怜之尾，耻嗟来而得食，肯诡遇以获禽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243438_comment'></div>然而乐善公卿，久要故旧，或加力于收拾，或阴借于吹嘘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243438_comment'></div>岁律再更，剡章四上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243438_comment'></div>惟浮图之未合，恐濩落以无容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243438_comment'></div>譬如为山九仞，尚亏于一篑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243438_comment'></div>宛在中沚一壶，何啻于千金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243438_comment'></div>敢于轩槛之前，辄效顽金之跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243438_comment'></div>恭惟某官术优王佐，学擅儒宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243438_comment'></div>九德在躬，表臣邻之冠冕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243438_comment'></div>群书满腹，粹师友之渊源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243438_comment'></div>昔居韦布之间，已负经纶之气，暨逢兴运，骤阅华涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243438_comment'></div>西掖代言，高掩常杨之誉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243438_comment'></div>北扉视草，密参颇牧之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243438_comment'></div>允兼文武之资，果注安危之意，枢柄既登于二府，使星复耀于三秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243438_comment'></div>遣邓禹于关中，威名响振；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243438_comment'></div>分召公于陕右，德化流行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243438_comment'></div>幕府言旋，介圭入觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1243438_comment'></div>方鼎梅之欲命，忽风树以缠悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1243438_comment'></div>甫终祥禫之期，遂受蕃宣之寄，升隆名于秘殿，委重镇于陪都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1243438_comment'></div>细柳兵閒，甘棠讼简，修山阴兰亭之故事，题镜湖秦望之新诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1243438_comment'></div>顾惟良弼之求，方资帝赉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1243438_comment'></div>第恐衮衣之咏，难缓公归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1243438_comment'></div>伫凤诏以出纶，催鹿车而当轴，阿衡一世，陶冶群材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1243438_comment'></div>盖事君以仁者，众夙仰于宏猷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1243438_comment'></div>而荐贤报国者，时正宜于今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1243438_comment'></div>方将掩东海以取垂天之翼，决西江而迎涸辙之鱼，使《菁莪》歌乐育之仁，而《棫朴》颂能官之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1243438_comment'></div>缙绅属望，岩穴倾心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1243438_comment'></div>至于疏逖之踪，尤切依归之素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1243438_comment'></div>拟作韩门之弟子，未窥孔氏之宫墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1243438_comment'></div>非不能连草三书，漫怀一刺，请窦长公之介绍，假郭有道之题评，因舍人而见曹参，为门客而干延寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1243438_comment'></div>高山流水，固可觊于知音；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1243438_comment'></div>明月夜光，惧或逢于按剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1243438_comment'></div>今者涂经大府，谒入高门，瞻周公几几之仪，惊汉相堂堂之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1243438_comment'></div>谦冲下逮，顾盼生光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1243438_comment'></div>季路初来，已有升堂之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1243438_comment'></div>曹交受业，思为假馆之留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1243438_comment'></div>时在可言，义难自弃，用忘固陋，仰冀甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1243438_comment'></div>盖得其所归，燕雀犹知于贺厦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1243438_comment'></div>翔而后集，鹪鹩岂妄于巢林？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1243438_comment'></div>士虽居穷约之中，身亦择栖投之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1243438_comment'></div>若非盛德，敢借馀光？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1243438_comment'></div>素微半面之知，且乏游谈之助，辄输肝胆，便丐齿牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1243438_comment'></div>视古人之进退以无嫌，在今世为狂愚而可笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1243438_comment'></div>处己如此，期公谓何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1243438_comment'></div>或明附骥之心，愿借连鳌之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1243438_comment'></div>鸡鸣狗盗，既下客以兼收；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1243438_comment'></div>虫臂鼠肝，庶大钧之永托。</div><div id='poem_sentence_73_1243438_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1243450' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243450' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243450?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通楼枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243450")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243450_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243450'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243450'>去公府之潭潭，荐更岁月；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243450_comment'></div>仰台符之两两，杳对云天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243450_comment'></div>久尘庠序之官，每负简书之畏，名姓用疏于记室，精神徒结于门墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243450_comment'></div>惟时辅弼之良，夙茂经纶之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243450_comment'></div>祠庭偃息，方益耸于具瞻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243450_comment'></div>神物扶持，宜厚膺于纯嘏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243450_comment'></div>恭惟某官才高人杰，道契天民，独兼文武之资，早注安危之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243450_comment'></div>玉堂诏令，追《尔雅》于二京；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243450_comment'></div>油幕韬钤，折遐冲于四国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243450_comment'></div>一攀鳞翼，再秉枢衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243450_comment'></div>屹然柱石之擎，炳若蓍龟之断，允当大任，果济中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243450_comment'></div>佐佑成王，君奭协周公之化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243450_comment'></div>谋谟贞观，房乔推如晦之筹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243450_comment'></div>旋抗封章，恳辞机政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243450_comment'></div>体恤特深于睿眷，股肱稍逸于贤劳，游绿野以娱神，侣赤松而访道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243450_comment'></div>属四海作霖之望，争睹十行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243450_comment'></div>副九重审象之求，伫臻三入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243450_comment'></div>某儒流晚进，钧播微生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243450_comment'></div>曩腾光范之书，获厕翘材之馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243450_comment'></div>轮囷见器，初无蟠木之容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243450_comment'></div>踊跃自言，遽入洪炉之铸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243450_comment'></div>遂脱身于选调，继列职于行都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243450_comment'></div>静言卵翼之私，遂自齿牙之借。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243450_comment'></div>知己之深恩未报，古人之大节奚论，克谨操修，恐辜提奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243450_comment'></div>比在渊源之地，属经寒暑之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243450_comment'></div>司训诂以非才，日虞官谤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243450_comment'></div>念松楸而自请，叨假军麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243450_comment'></div>尚飘萍寄之踪，未及瓜期之代，窘饥寒之方急，执洒扫以无阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243450_comment'></div>菅蒯至微，永托卿云之荫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243450_comment'></div>潢污虽远，终期沧海之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243450_comment'></div>兹炎赫之在辰，宜保绥之加意，亟被赐环之召，式隆调鼎之功。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1243450_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1141')">1140-1141年</a>　在临安任左官。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ba13bc00f09b4a928502e10ad60c814d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ba13bc00f09b4a928502e10ad60c814d");'><span id='ba13bc00f09b4a928502e10ad60c814d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1148')">1144-1148年</a>，41-45岁</div><div id='ba13bc00f09b4a928502e10ad60c814d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年5月</a>　在开封，除太学录，有谢宰相启。作品：除太学录谢宰相启。<div id='poem_1243436' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243436' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243436?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除太学录谢宰相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243436")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243436_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243436'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243436'>脱选调之尘埃，初更禄秩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243436_comment'></div>录成均之考法，忽冒除书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243436_comment'></div>揣己何堪，就官有腼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243436_comment'></div>我国家观人文而化天下，度绝前闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243436_comment'></div>建首善而自京师，实由内始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243436_comment'></div>逮华戎之多故，痛庠序之久隳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243436_comment'></div>天之未丧斯文，俄臻偃革；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243436_comment'></div>物不可以终否，复观迓衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243436_comment'></div>圣贤相逢而治具张，财力有馀而颂声作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243436_comment'></div>乃依行所，肇辟贤关，规模还列圣之容，警跸来九天之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243436_comment'></div>誉髦云集，声教飙驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243436_comment'></div>爰遴简于师儒，俾讲明于经术，仍分正录，用纠生徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243436_comment'></div>虽取法先王，本诗书礼乐以造士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243436_comment'></div>然更资大器，执规矩准绳而治人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243436_comment'></div>宜得名流，以谐清议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243436_comment'></div>如某者禀才至薄，涉世尤疏，谬传箕裘弓冶之馀，无复师友渊源之自。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243436_comment'></div>策名第一，嗟壮岁之已过；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243436_comment'></div>随牒四方，怅谫能之无补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243436_comment'></div>一行泮水，三变周星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243436_comment'></div>仕有时为贫，本作升斗之计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243436_comment'></div>教然后知困，惭无尺寸之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243436_comment'></div>比及终更，偶容善去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243436_comment'></div>顾无德而富贵，早已灰心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243436_comment'></div>惟有道之贱贫，未能雪耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243436_comment'></div>勉从铨课，遂忝京僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243436_comment'></div>方徒劳州县之间，甘为俗吏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243436_comment'></div>何乐育人材之地，遂并英游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243436_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官仁济含生，功超振古，耻尧、舜之不及，至周、召而乃留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243436_comment'></div>保乂王家，克端命于上帝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243436_comment'></div>会绍乃辟，用追孝于前人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243436_comment'></div>致万物以得宜，无一夫之不获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243436_comment'></div>至如孱陋，尤困奇穷，貌丑心妍，利居众后，发髡齿豁，不见已知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243436_comment'></div>与其掉乞怜之尾，而侥倖于他人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243436_comment'></div>曷若由中正之涂，而投诚于吾相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243436_comment'></div>式下灵鳌之钓，靡资蟠木之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243436_comment'></div>草光范之书，无烦三献；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243436_comment'></div>开翘材之馆，亟纳孤踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243436_comment'></div>轸其从官之清贫，授以为文之要体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243436_comment'></div>大钧所播，至鉴难逃，蒙厚德以如斯，殒微躯而何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243436_comment'></div>某敢不恪共尔位，终始其躬！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243436_comment'></div>当任贤使能之朝，既尘公举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243436_comment'></div>坚仗节死义之守，必报私恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1243436_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　在开封，除太学博士，有谢宰相启。作品：除博士谢宰相启。<div id='poem_1243442' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243442' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243442?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除博士谢宰相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243442")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243442_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243442'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243442'>纠教法于贤关，蔑闻善状；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243442_comment'></div>正官联于讲席，忽奉恩纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243442_comment'></div>就列无堪，循名有腼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243442_comment'></div>窃以四海渊源之自，盖本成均；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243442_comment'></div>六经训诂之传，实由博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243442_comment'></div>明人伦而在是，列天象以昭然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243442_comment'></div>平时固号于才难，文治尤严于德举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243442_comment'></div>得见君子斯可矣，否则学者无述焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243442_comment'></div>如某者业谢师承，体非儒雅，只缘幸会，偶误甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243442_comment'></div>属当首善之兴，遂造群英之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243442_comment'></div>典司规矩，岂谐宽猛之宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243442_comment'></div>校阅艺文，莫赞公明之考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243442_comment'></div>继下帷而摄事，每非座以怀惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243442_comment'></div>敢期寡闻无约之资，乃冒久假不归之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243442_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官至明烛隐，大度包荒，修礼乐于小雅尽废之馀，洪基图于炎政中微之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243442_comment'></div>雷破山而风振海，壮矣帡幪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243442_comment'></div>鸢戾天而鱼跃渊，妙哉橐籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243442_comment'></div>故虽绵薄，亦被生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243442_comment'></div>惟辞章视一世以污隆，而国学为四方之楷式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243442_comment'></div>变齐鲁以至道，欣盛化之已纯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243442_comment'></div>逃杨墨而归儒，恨斯文之未副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243442_comment'></div>既公去取，必绝爱憎，恃直道之方行，冀狂澜之可复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243442_comment'></div>某敢不勉思博约，确守靖共！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243442_comment'></div>譬彼铸金，德难酬于大冶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243442_comment'></div>用诸攻玉，质徒愧于它山。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1243442_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　在开封太学，每值谈经，同僚避席。王十朋等争求指教。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　在开封。杨朴献《礼部韵括遗》，王之望奏其类实繁。作品：看详杨朴《礼部韵括遗》状。<div id='poem_1243309' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243309' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243309?labeling=true' target='_blank'>看详杨朴礼部韵括遗状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243309")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243309_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243309'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243309'>近承朝廷降下杨朴所进《礼部韵括遗》，令监学官看详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243309_comment'></div>契勘礼部韵止为场屋程文而设，非如《广韵》、《集韵》，普收奇字，务为该洽，故谓之「韵略」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243309_comment'></div>元祐间博士孙谔等申明，谓经传所用之字，《礼部韵略》所不载，只取举人常用者，附入数十字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243309_comment'></div>今杨朴所进，分为五门，采摭之功，颇为详悉，博涉经史，足有可嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243309_comment'></div>其可收者，欲依所乞附韵，或注云「一作」，或别出一字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243309_comment'></div>内字非常用，如「庐」之为「卢」、「泜」之为「𣹑」之类；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243309_comment'></div>或别无经见，如「辂」之为「迓」、「愉」之为「偷」之类；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243309_comment'></div>或非韵所押，如「单」之音「善」、「众」之音「终」之类，于科举之文无所轻重，恐疑学者，并乞不收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243309_comment'></div>其音不必改一项，既关先儒义训，不当以私意改更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243309_comment'></div>兼释文自出音，或诸家已有别说，近时学者自不改读，徒立异同，何裨损益？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243309_comment'></div>其字不必附一项，如「旦明」之为「神明」、「缮怒」之为「劲怒」之类，率多假借，或出谬误，《礼部韵略》元所不收，广示搜罗，几于芜赘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243309_comment'></div>然其间如「术」之为「遂」、「遍」之为「辩」，「肉好」之「肉」读为救切，音释明白，《韵略》所无，既欲增添，却宜收附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243309_comment'></div>至于「埶」之为「势」，「食」之为「饮」，「揄」之音「由」，「焉」之音「嫣」，「荼」之音「舒」，《韵略》已收，难以重出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243309_comment'></div>杨朴又谓「箛篍皆已入韵」，以此为例，其类实繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243309_comment'></div>前人所收，不无冗长，今之所附，岂可效尤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243309_comment'></div>今各于逐字下开具奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1243309_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　在开封，有启给楼炤。作品：通楼枢密启。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年1月24日</a>　在开封，充点检试卷官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年闰11月</a>　在开封，面对，乞印群经。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>　在开封，有跋。作品：跋赵祖文七进图。<div id='poem_1243545' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243545' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243545?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋赵祖文七进图</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243545")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243545_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243545'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243545'>先君宣和中在京师与竹隐公游，喜称诵其词章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243545_comment'></div>后公出帅南阳，过博望，题诗传舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243545_comment'></div>自序少时娶田氏于襄阳，携家往来，今三十年过之，当时之人独身在耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243545_comment'></div>因感退之《始兴江口》诗，和之云：「邯郸枕上人何在，华表声中鹤仅存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243545_comment'></div>世事悲欢三百载，此怀欲与退之论」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243545_comment'></div>乙巳岁，先君经行是驿，见壁间粉牌，曰：「此赵承之诗也，小子识之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243545_comment'></div>时公已殁，后二年而先君不幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243545_comment'></div>又十八年，见公从子祖文于武林，出所画《七进图》示余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243545_comment'></div>观其跋云：「图中所存，今惟二人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243545_comment'></div>因追记博望之诗，则当时目前相逐者又零落如此，而余亦孤苦流落，行且老矣，感叹之馀，为之出涕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243545_comment'></div>此图文甚雅丽，画又妙绝，所谓虽无老成人，尚有典刑者也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1243545_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　在开封，论《三坟书》为伪作。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年6月16日</a>　在开封。面对，论举人程文。作品：乞禁约举人文体奏议。<div id='poem_1243308' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243308' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243308?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞禁约举人文体奏议<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十三年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年6月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243308")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243308_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243308'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243308'>臣伏睹国家贡举之制，专试艺文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243308_comment'></div>有司考校之科，皆有程度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243308_comment'></div>中间累举，属在艰难，场屋取人，犹多阔略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243308_comment'></div>陛下聿兴大业，垂意斯文，恢辟胶庠，遍于中外，布韦之士，皆得专讲习于其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243308_comment'></div>彬彬之风，寖复承平之旧矣，则选取之法固宜益加详密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243308_comment'></div>且如连用本朝文集十句，在熙宁、元丰、崇宁、大观法，皆黜落不考；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243308_comment'></div>元祐法与建炎所修，虽降从轻，尚为一抹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243308_comment'></div>而今举人殊不知避，一篇之内或纯用数百言，主司不以为非，更谓该洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243308_comment'></div>又如试文内作歌颂，及用佛书全句十字以上，大观法亦系不考，而建炎删去不收，以致举人尤多犯者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243308_comment'></div>若此之类，未易悉举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243308_comment'></div>秋试在近，其可不革乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243308_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特赐睿旨，检举见行条法，申严行下，令考官遵守、举子通知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243308_comment'></div>其遗漏未尽者，更照前后格式量加参定，庶几去取之际，不至疑惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243308_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1243308_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年8月</a>　在开封，充点检试卷官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>　在开封，上宰相秦桧书，乞迁一官。作品：上宰相书（某闻下之事）<div id='poem_1243402' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243402' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243402?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上宰相书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243402")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243402_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243402'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243402'>某闻下之事上，莫贵于用情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243402_comment'></div>情之所在，求之而不为贪，辞之而不为矫，趣舍之际无适不宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243402_comment'></div>昔孔门弟子或欲干禄，或不愿仕，吾夫子因而遂之，进退无讥焉，诚知其心无所隐于我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243402_comment'></div>后世之士忠信不足，妄诞有馀，阳为名高，阴趣势利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243402_comment'></div>范汪志干时用，托省儿坟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243402_comment'></div>杜淹欲得美官，反效隐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243402_comment'></div>心迹相反，以伪钓奇，真治世之罪人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243402_comment'></div>独唐韩愈以古道自信，不恤时议，上书宰相，以布衣求官，其言曰：「可举而举焉，不必逊于自举也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243402_comment'></div>可进而进焉，不必廉于自进也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243402_comment'></div>既斥潮州，作表哀谢，称己之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243402_comment'></div>其自处于君相之间，诚可谓较然不欺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243402_comment'></div>然为国子博士三年不迁，既不能恬于进取，默尔无言，又不能吐露肺肝，卓然自结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243402_comment'></div>其作《进学解》委曲以致其意，虽当路怜之，自此稍进，亦不得谓之诚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243402_comment'></div>岂愈信道不笃，为流俗之所移邪，抑当时执政者不足以诚告之也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243402_comment'></div>某诵之久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243402_comment'></div>向自下士来，不因绍介，负其不腆之文，仰干典谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243402_comment'></div>相公收之于泥涂穷悴之中，使教育天下之英材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243402_comment'></div>自惟疏贱无能，滥被器使，夙夜磨砺，思有以自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243402_comment'></div>当官行己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243402_comment'></div>如相公之身临而目瞰之，立见于前，乘见于衡，盖五年于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243402_comment'></div>上自朝士，下至诸生，无一人亲戚乡闾之援，惟恃恩纪，以逭谴诃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243402_comment'></div>安全卵翼之恩，一毫未报，岂宜侥倖茍得，更有所干请哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243402_comment'></div>但以渊源之地，风波易动，指目为多，不才之人久此叨据，尝恐不免于戾，上玷陶镕，欲布腹心，未敢率尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243402_comment'></div>不谓相公特轸钧念，俾得自言，尚可默默畏避，怀不尽之意乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243402_comment'></div>如某之寒，相公知之旧矣，居官得禄，犹不能自给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243402_comment'></div>今终更在迩，故乡不可归，挟数百指之累，将安之邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243402_comment'></div>又一寡居表姊，近携孤女远来，任其嫁遣之责，其势尤迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243402_comment'></div>若于此时不能一鸣其情，是蹈韩愈之失，而不以吾夫子待其门人者望吾相也，而可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243402_comment'></div>伏惟察其区区之诚，终始矜怜，畀以一官，免待远次，则啼饥号寒之属，庶不殒于沟壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243402_comment'></div>其恩德之小大轻重，某宜知何报也！</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1243402_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年闰8月23日</a>　知荆门军，以葬亲有请也。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c045f0975bbc491b945dbe863b6f6155_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c045f0975bbc491b945dbe863b6f6155");'><span id='c045f0975bbc491b945dbe863b6f6155_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>，50岁</div><div id='c045f0975bbc491b945dbe863b6f6155' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>　任左承议郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年8月</a>　充点检试卷官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年9月1日</a>　提举荆湖南路常平茶盐公事。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2b78113361f343a9b18dfce9d7191ce6_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>，57岁</div><div id='2b78113361f343a9b18dfce9d7191ce6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年8月5日</a>　在临安府。召赴行在，除太府少卿，总领四川财赋军马钱粮。上谢表。作品：谢授太府卿表。<div id='poem_1243280' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243280' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243280?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢授太府卿表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年8月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243280")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243280_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243280'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243280'>主计坤维，苟逭旷官之责；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243280_comment'></div>升华月寺，忽惊增秩之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243280_comment'></div>更膺修举之褒，愈切叨尘之愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243280_comment'></div>伏念臣早专儒学，初乏吏能，于财赋以何资，尤性资之所短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243280_comment'></div>矧当调饷，乃误使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243280_comment'></div>宿重戍于三边，开新疆于两路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243280_comment'></div>转输粗给，皆朝廷申画之明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243280_comment'></div>凯捷屡腾，实将帅驱驰之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243280_comment'></div>夫何绵薄，猥冒恩光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243280_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下仁孝独隆，德刑并举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243280_comment'></div>聪明睿智而不杀，伟略无前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243280_comment'></div>是非赏罚之已明，微劳必录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243280_comment'></div>故虽疏远，亦被甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243280_comment'></div>然臣衰病日侵，事功难彊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243280_comment'></div>投闲置散，已屡贡于忱诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243280_comment'></div>治剧济烦，恐终辜于寄委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243280_comment'></div>愿回明鉴，俯照丹衷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1243280_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='068e039c4cc449acba965ab9da962aeb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("068e039c4cc449acba965ab9da962aeb");'><span id='068e039c4cc449acba965ab9da962aeb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>，60岁</div><div id='068e039c4cc449acba965ab9da962aeb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年10月</a>　在临安。还朝，以版曹参赞都督府。上谢表。作品：谢吏部侍郎表。<div id='poem_1243290' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243290' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243290?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢吏部侍郎表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243290")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243290_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243290'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243290'>再贰计曹，初无补报，亟升选部，益愧叨逾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243290_comment'></div>仰戴恩私，伏深震悸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243290_comment'></div>伏念臣比缘抱疾，亦既投閒，旋召复于故官，仍外参于督府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243290_comment'></div>洎蒙赐对，遂俾留中，继寓直于禁林，俄出将于使聘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243290_comment'></div>未决辞荣之请，益怀避事之心，期仗节以还归，即丐祠而引去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243290_comment'></div>岂图侥倖，更冒宠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243290_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下唐帝聪明，汉皇溪达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243290_comment'></div>贤才是急，形梦想于精神；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243290_comment'></div>赏罚靡轻，严笑颦于劝沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243290_comment'></div>致兹冗职，亦误褒迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243290_comment'></div>臣敢不戒在瘝官，审于量己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243290_comment'></div>不能者止，况堪衰病之侵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243290_comment'></div>有欲必从，终冀生成之造。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1243290_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　在临安。还朝，以版曹参赞都督府。上辞免奏札。作品：再辞免奏札。<div id='poem_1243339' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243339' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243339?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再辞免奏劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243339")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243339_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243339'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243339'>臣昨具奏劄，辞免淮西宣谕使恩命，奉圣旨依已降指挥，不得再有陈请，仍日下条具合行事件申尚书省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243339_comment'></div>臣冒渎天威，仰勤圣主再三戒敕，九殒莫赎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243339_comment'></div>臣欲求对，则腰膝缓弱，不能久立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243339_comment'></div>陛下不信臣病，试令内殿引见，察其形神，可见不妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243339_comment'></div>臣平生所历，未尝辞难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243339_comment'></div>前为四川总领之日，正值军兴，臣以一身横抗三面，得免疏阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243339_comment'></div>后蒙就除川陕宣谕，守御蜀门，臣与吴璘驻于河池，经画边防，慰抚将士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243339_comment'></div>虽德顺失利，而蜀竟无他。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243339_comment'></div>既而得请奉祠，旋被召命，水行八千馀里，冲冒三峡涨潦之险，偶幸生存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243339_comment'></div>到阙两旬，便差奉使大金，臣更不敢辞，赖陛下保持，复还阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243339_comment'></div>今兹淮西之事，闻朝廷自有处画，比前三者未至甚难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243339_comment'></div>臣所以力辞者，盖衰病所婴，筋力甚惫，心气积损，思虑不周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243339_comment'></div>一面事宜，利害甚重，深恐有误国计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243339_comment'></div>况臣十八日上殿已有文字丐祠，数日之间劄目三上，则非闻命而避事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243339_comment'></div>今中外侍从才智不少，岂无一人可当任使，乃必欲令疲惫老病之人冒死而行？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243339_comment'></div>窃意陛下宽仁睿智，知臣下之勤劳，必不忍独于微臣逼抑如此，盖未审其实病耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243339_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特赐矜察，检会累劄，改授一宫观差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243339_comment'></div>臣屡拒诏旨，罪合诛夷，惟陛下哀怜，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1243339_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　在临安，初见孝宗，有奏疏，言人主论兵与臣下不同。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年11月12日</a>　在临安，权户部侍郎兼权直院。上辞免札。作品：辞免兼权直学士院奏札。<div id='poem_1243332' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243332' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243332?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免兼权直学士院奏劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年11月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243332")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243332_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243332'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243332'>臣今月十二日准尚书省劄子，备奉圣旨，差臣兼权直学士院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243332_comment'></div>臣闻命之际，感惧交并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243332_comment'></div>窃以禁林寓直，实资润色之才，是虽时暂兼权，不当辞避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243332_comment'></div>缘臣久更烦使，旧学荒疏，衰病之馀，志思凋落，岂可承乏内制？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243332_comment'></div>若或冒处，必致失职，以取颠隮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243332_comment'></div>矧今侍从之间，居多文学先进之士，使当此任，无不具宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243332_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特回误渥，改受英俊，以穆师言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243332_comment'></div>所有前件恩命，未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243332_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1243332_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年11月</a>　在临安，除吏部侍郎。上谢表。作品：谢吏部侍郎表。<div id='poem_1243290' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243290' class='poemTitle class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243333?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论集议通和惟求其当奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243333")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243333_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243333'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243333'>臣窃惟金人通和，在今日事体最重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243333_comment'></div>陛下既欲集议，以收群策而示至公，此诚谋及卿士之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243333_comment'></div>凡与议者，固当展尽底蕴，用副圣主虚心广览之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243333_comment'></div>然人心不同，有如其面，各言尔志，不可责以雷同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243333_comment'></div>武王伐商，誓于牧野，其诗曰：「上帝临汝，无贰尔心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243333_comment'></div>臣愿陛下诏群臣务尽实情，以对越天地，其或私意观望其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243333_comment'></div>诏台谏勿以同异为喜怒，诏宰执勿以喜怒为用舍，而陛下采纳之际，勿以多寡为从违，惟求其当，以济国事，天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1243333_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d44a4369f08a45e9b5055404338fc368_label'><a href='javascript: showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243336?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上殿再乞宫观劄子<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243336")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243336_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243336'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243336'>臣顷朝辞面对，尝以奏劄，沥具危恳，仰渎宸聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243336_comment'></div>缘连年抱疾，精力凋耗，出疆事重，不敢辞难，自合糜捐，以身徇国，乞使事回日，改授一在外宫观差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243336_comment'></div>臣到盱眙，一病四十馀日，虽幸生存，而支离愈甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243336_comment'></div>脏腑滑泄，胸膈喘懑，表虚多汗，呼吸冷气，极畏风寒，尤惮晨起，心气积损，恍惚健忘，稍涉思虑，终日怔忪，两目昏花，不能细字，腰膝缓弱，跪立艰难，微有动作，便加困殆，委是勉强不前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243336_comment'></div>陛下若责以事功，则必辜委任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243336_comment'></div>若许其尸素，则自愧平生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243336_comment'></div>臣反覆自量，去就甚审，非敢上欺君父，有邀求规避之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243336_comment'></div>伏望圣慈检会前劄，早赐矜允，使就安养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243336_comment'></div>庶几少宽忧畏，可引残年，得免颠隮，以全晚节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243336_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣不胜祈哀俟命、惶惧迫切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243336_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1243336_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年3月</a>　在临安。回朝后，三上奏札乞宫观。作品：上殿再乞宫观札子（臣比再具奏札）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年3月25日</a>　在临安，为淮西宣谕使。上辞免奏札。作品：辞免淮西宣谕使奏札。<div id='poem_1243338' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243338' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243338?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免淮西宣谕使奏劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年3月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243338")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243338_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243338'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243338'>臣二十五日夜准三省枢密院劄子，奉圣旨差充淮西宣谕使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243338_comment'></div>闻命忧惶，泣涕终夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243338_comment'></div>臣之疾疢，国信使一行尽皆见之，朝廷上下尽皆知之，独不蒙陛下悯恻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243338_comment'></div>顷三具奏劄，恳求宫观，刳心沥血，无一语欺诞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243338_comment'></div>既未回天意，而今所差委愈更重难，岂不酷哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243338_comment'></div>且淮西事宜最今日安危所系，既非臣乡土，又不经游宦，官吏将帅全不相识，人情地利，一切不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243338_comment'></div>使臣强健之时，亦不能办，况衰病如此邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243338_comment'></div>臣精神昏眊，筋力凋残，畏恶风寒，如避锋刃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243338_comment'></div>若使奔走边塞，颠覆何疑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243338_comment'></div>虽臣之一死，朝廷视犹蝼蚁，在所不恤，其于疆埸之事，岂不有误经度？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243338_comment'></div>伏望圣慈略赐矜察，以此重任，改授能臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243338_comment'></div>臣虽窜戮，不敢奉诏，与其误国，宁获违命之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243338_comment'></div>但恐臣死之后，奉公尽瘁之人皆以臣为戒耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243338_comment'></div>惟陛下天地父母，哀而怜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243338_comment'></div>干犯天威，无所逃罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243338_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1243338_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年3月28日</a>　在临安，奏乞以亲王为江淮元帅。月底，再奏。作品：乞以亲王为江淮元帅奏议。<div id='poem_1243340' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243340' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243340?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞以亲王为江淮元帅奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年3月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243340")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243340_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243340'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243340'>臣契勘宣谕之职，所以宣布德意，以谕其所部经度事宜，所当图上方略，听命于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243340_comment'></div>至于阃外之制，则非其所当专也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243340_comment'></div>方无事时，采访申画，禀令于上，且容承乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243340_comment'></div>若缓急用兵，岂比都督、视宣抚，可责以成败之任？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243340_comment'></div>见今将帅犹以王人会议之，故可同措置，将来防秋，朝廷遣殿司马步三衙之兵出戍于江北，与宣谕不相统摄，其肯听其号令乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243340_comment'></div>或曰：「敌若犯塞，朝廷自别有处置」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243340_comment'></div>臣应之曰：经画边事，须是敌人未动之前，既动之后，亦何所及？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243340_comment'></div>临时误事，必云前遣宣谕失于经度，则误国之罪，专在宣谕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243340_comment'></div>宣谕获罪，固不足恤，独不知误国之祸于宗庙社稷如何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243340_comment'></div>唐使九节度围安庆绪于相州，以李光弼、郭子仪皆元功，不置都帅，而以鱼朝恩为观军容使，事权不一，遂大溃其师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243340_comment'></div>宪宗伐蔡，使裴度督战，时韩弘为都统，乃以度为宣慰使，然度方为宰相，虽以都统推弘而实专帅事，故能有济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243340_comment'></div>迩来北边探报不一，皆云金人签兵聚粮，蓄力大举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243340_comment'></div>敌不动则已，若其敢来，必鉴逆亮之失，别有贼计，亦可谓大敌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243340_comment'></div>而独倚二宣谕以当之，不亦难乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243340_comment'></div>臣有愚计，望陛下以亲王为江淮元帅，而于见任宰执中择一人为之副，以办防秋之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243340_comment'></div>将帅士卒知陛下以圣子贤王出总大柄，必皆欢呼奋励，人人愿效，气当百倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243340_comment'></div>今方贻书北敌，欲议和好，彼闻吾此举必当震怖，和事愈益易集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243340_comment'></div>或者必谓如此，则当犒设诸军，创置官属，有所费用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243340_comment'></div>臣谓亲王不必临边，只开府于阙下，军兵自不须犒设，而使其副驻于建康、镇江之间，足增重事权，张皇军威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243340_comment'></div>阙下开府，则亦不须多置僚属，何费之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243340_comment'></div>臣非惮宣谕之行，设此以自脱，盖自视才力不足独当重责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243340_comment'></div>若果如臣所请，将来幕府僚寀或乏使令，臣不敢以不肖为辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243340_comment'></div>陛下勿以和议为必成，遂弛边备，臣谓正宜立武以壮国体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243340_comment'></div>此安危大计，愿陛下断自宸衷，速发大号，天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1243340_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年4月2日</a>　在临安，未行，又拜左谏议大夫。上奏议。作品：初除左谏议大夫上殿奏议。<div id='poem_1243350' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243350' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243350?labeling=true' target='_blank'>初除左谏议大夫上殿奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年4月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243350")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243350_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243350'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243350'>臣愚不肖，陛下过听，擢长谏垣，臣未知所以称塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243350_comment'></div>窃闻唐魏郑公以谏诤为心，耻君不及尧舜，平居歆慕，以为人臣如斯，可以无愧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243350_comment'></div>然贤人君子立人之朝，孰不欲尧舜其君？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243350_comment'></div>至于得行其志者，宰相之外，独谏官耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243350_comment'></div>臣今缪当其职，敢不以郑公之心为心乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243350_comment'></div>或者以尧舜为不可及，欲致君尧舜者谓之责难于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243350_comment'></div>臣以为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243350_comment'></div>尧舜之道甚大而易行，尧舜之政甚简而易为，顾后世不之察耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243350_comment'></div>尧舜之道，行于其躬者惟孝，施于其下者惟仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243350_comment'></div>陛下既允蹈之，一无所难，信乎甚大而易行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243350_comment'></div>尧舜之政则在于官人，而官人之道在于敷奏以言、明试以功而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243350_comment'></div>尧告舜曰「询事考言，乃言底可绩」，禹于皋陶亦云，此所谓敷奏以言者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243350_comment'></div>舜命禹作司空曰「汝平水土，成允成功」，称皋陶曰「汝作士，明刑弼，教民协于中，时乃功」，此明试以功者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243350_comment'></div>陛下于群臣中敷奏之以言欤，言发于前而底绩于后者何人也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243350_comment'></div>明试之以功欤，功作于始而克成于末者何事也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243350_comment'></div>以此察之，则虚名不足以惑众听，横议不敢以摇至公，奸欺不容，真伪判矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243350_comment'></div>共工静言庸违、象恭滔天，而驩兜乃叹美其「方鸠僝功」，欲尧之用之，而尧竟不从，此言之不验者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243350_comment'></div>四岳荐鲧治水，尧曰「咈哉，方命圮族，九载绩用弗成」，此功之不效者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243350_comment'></div>舜既承尧，首正四凶之罪，天下咸服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243350_comment'></div>尧舜之政，岂不甚简而易为乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243350_comment'></div>陛下以聪明睿智之资，承光尧付托之重，属时多事，未尝一日以位为乐，忧勤庶政，三年于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243350_comment'></div>宜其治效崇成，未有云获者，非道之不弘，政未举耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243350_comment'></div>臣伏见今朝廷之上，妨功固位之习未殄，背公死党之论日闻，以妄诞为才能，以凶悖为坚正，执偏见而不求天下之通论，各私所主而不恤公家之大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243350_comment'></div>大抵图国甚拙，而为其身谋则工；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243350_comment'></div>爱君不专，而附其交党则力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243350_comment'></div>孔子曰：「鄙夫不可与事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243350_comment'></div>未得之，患不得之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243350_comment'></div>既得之，患失之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243350_comment'></div>茍患失，无所不至」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243350_comment'></div>此风不革，陛下虽欲彊兵富国为治安之计，臣固知有所不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243350_comment'></div>伏愿陛下明诏在廷，各励节操，平其心于论议之际，端其趣于背向之间，使廉耻兴行，风俗丕变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243350_comment'></div>访之以言者必要其验，试之以功者必覈其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243350_comment'></div>若附下罔上，造为弗靖，怙终而不变，则虞舜四凶之罪，在陛下其得已乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243350_comment'></div>如是，则朋比自破，功罪不诬，而天下可运于掌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243350_comment'></div>此帝王致治之要术、御世之至权也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243350_comment'></div>惟陛下留神，宗社幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1243350_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年5月3日</a>　在临安，劾刘光时。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年5月17日</a>　在临安，劾邵宏渊。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年6月4日</a>　在临安，上奏论两淮镇戍要害，同诸将分定把截关隘、战守、屯泊去处。诏从之。作品：论两淮镇戍要害奏议。<div id='poem_1243347' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243347' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243347?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论两淮镇戍要害奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年6月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243347")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243347_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243347'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243347'>臣伏准三省枢密院劄子备钱端礼奏内称：昨来敌人累次侵犯，皆自西路入寇，盖濠、寿之地径捷，而粮船多自清河以入滁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243347_comment'></div>今西路部分要害已得其宜，若严切固守，无致侵犯东路滁州一带最为上策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243347_comment'></div>设若透漏奔冲，则郭振全军与西路军马夹击，甚为利便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243347_comment'></div>及令刘宝、郭振互相照应，临机制胜，遇有两路连接事机，星火关报，协力一心，无致差误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243347_comment'></div>奉圣旨，劄与淮西宣谕司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243347_comment'></div>臣观钱端礼所陈，甚合事宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243347_comment'></div>契勘两淮屏蔽大江，利害一体，尤不可以东、西分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243347_comment'></div>朝廷既差两宣谕，遂有界限，势使然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243347_comment'></div>且如以前宣抚都督通管两路，则如何分得东、西？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243347_comment'></div>淮南形势，淮水殊不足恃，而大江狭处最是采石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243347_comment'></div>敌人每来由巢县、和州一带，径至江上，最为要害，其次方到六合、扬州，盖江道阔而路稍背也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243347_comment'></div>今西路措置，修石湖亭、昭关等处关隘，使贼不得至采石，则是两淮最要害处，西路已独当之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243347_comment'></div>其馀光、黄、桐城等处，孔道甚多，皆须堤备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243347_comment'></div>六合虽隶淮东，而地邻西路，臣所以欲两路相关措置，设有缓急，自合两路相应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243347_comment'></div>此事臣与钱端礼所言一同，乃今日措置两淮之上策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243347_comment'></div>若要固守濠、寿等州，使敌不犯滁州一带，则必无是理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243347_comment'></div>臣前奏庐、寿、光州决不可守，濠州若敌大入，亦须保横涧山，而两路中间接近去处，即合相关措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243347_comment'></div>盖缓急分东西不得，敌奔冲东路六合，必须西路夹击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243347_comment'></div>若欲固守濠、寿，使不犯东路滁州，则西路亦岂能独任其责？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243347_comment'></div>滁州不可守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243347_comment'></div>滁州之不可守而守六合，而寿、濠之地其可责西路之保守，使贼不透漏乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243347_comment'></div>今东路刘宝一军把遏水道外，殿前一军人数甚众，将来屯在扬州，郭振军在六合，所备此一带平阔，然不过一二百里之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243347_comment'></div>而西路疆界阔远，边面千里，地平如掌，又无城池之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243347_comment'></div>若不据险，不知用几人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243347_comment'></div>虽有大众，终不足以当敌人之骑兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243347_comment'></div>见今张守忠军屯巢县，与时俊保石湖岭，王彦屯和州保旷口、昭关，戚方屯桐城保北峡诸关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243347_comment'></div>敌兵不犯去处，方可抽那应援，今敌人分兵，一犯西路昭关，一犯东路六合州，则各处仅能自保而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243347_comment'></div>此所以备御之不可不严也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243347_comment'></div>故臣曰西路当据诸山之险，以控其兵锋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243347_comment'></div>东路当扼清河之口，以断其粮道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243347_comment'></div>淮西若不扼诸山之险，而守濠、寿以蔽障滁州，此乃刘锜、王权辈前车之覆辙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243347_comment'></div>若西路败于濠、寿之间，则将何兵马与东路夹击于六合乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243347_comment'></div>西路既败，非徒无可以应援东路，而东路六合、扬州之众，亦恐不复能枝梧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243347_comment'></div>若吾据关守险，非徒可以自保其处，敌知吾有备，亦未必便敢深入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243347_comment'></div>使其送死，则吾以逸待劳，以饱待饥，正堕吾计中，可以得志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243347_comment'></div>故臣以为今日措置两淮之上策，无以加此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243347_comment'></div>臣与钱端礼所论，大抵相同，只恐淮东指准淮西固守濠、寿，欲其不犯滁州，将来却成相误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243347_comment'></div>臣愚欲望圣慈预戒两路诸帅，遇有侵犯两路相近要害去处，互相策应，不得坐观成败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243347_comment'></div>临时朝廷更严赐指挥，盖此非两宣谕之力所能独办也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243347_comment'></div>仍乞降臣此劄，行下照会，庶几不致疑误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243347_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1243347_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年6月23日</a>　在临安，劾韩元吉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年7月7日</a>　在临安，上救弊之策。作品：论恩榜任子革弊奏议。<div id='poem_1243351' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243351' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243351?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论恩榜任子革弊奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年7月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243351")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243351_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243351'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243351'>臣今月初七日准御封降下御劄文字付台谏官，谓：「朕自临御以来，躬率俭抑，每念官冗恩滥，思革积久之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243351_comment'></div>将来任子、贡举，若停三年之限，必胥动以浮言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243351_comment'></div>今欲遇郊祀之恩，已经奏补者并权免荫补一次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243351_comment'></div>开贤良方正之科，许令中外普荐真材，其免解该恩榜人，且权住罢赴试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243351_comment'></div>卿等各宜公协乃心，参酌所宜，条具上来，朕审处而行之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243351_comment'></div>臣猥以庸虚，备数谏省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243351_comment'></div>伏睹陛下天资英睿，济以果断，厉精求治，约己救时，近古帝王盖所未有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243351_comment'></div>即位以来，慨然愤积弊之久，欲一切惩革，以大有为于天下，斯千载之一时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243351_comment'></div>臣不肖，待罪谏省，得奉咨询，何其幸欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243351_comment'></div>然臣闻更化者不欲骇俗，而除弊者不可循常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243351_comment'></div>人情安于侥倖，茍且历数，百年乃欲，一旦革而正之，势必至于纷纷而不靖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243351_comment'></div>将遂行而不恤欤，则必失天下之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243351_comment'></div>将中道而复止欤，则后日无以为政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243351_comment'></div>是不可以不审也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243351_comment'></div>若曰「更化除弊，难恤流俗之议」，亦须在我者词直而有名，犹当反覆调伏，使无所发其忿怼不逞之心，始可以无悔，况其未然乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243351_comment'></div>汉文帝时诸侯彊大，僭上不轨，景帝愤之，峻加裁削，于是七国俱反，汉几失山东，此乃循常骇俗之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243351_comment'></div>其后武帝用主父偃之策，各使封及支庶，诸侯不削而自弱，盖处之得其道耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243351_comment'></div>任子恩科，祖宗时有之，遽停三年，必不免浮言之胥动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243351_comment'></div>庆历中仁宗开天章阁，命辅臣陈当世急务，范仲淹、富弼辈条上数事，减任子其一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243351_comment'></div>未几谤讟大兴，一时名臣皆狼狈而去，所言卒废格不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243351_comment'></div>神宗熙宁中减进士状头恩数，而苏轼亦极言其非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243351_comment'></div>大抵更化除弊为至难，在祖宗时已然，况风俗久坏，纲纪未振，如今日之甚者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243351_comment'></div>且名位有高卑，子侄有多寡，若已经奏补者并免荫补一次，则贵贱不分，而人有幸不幸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243351_comment'></div>特奏名之人，举数有多少，年齿有老壮，若并权住罢，则举多者受屈，而年老者无聊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243351_comment'></div>至于开贤良之科，广中外之荐，自是国家求才，与任子、恩榜非所以相乘除也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243351_comment'></div>自靖康以后兴复此科，十有馀举，竟无一人应诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243351_comment'></div>虽令普荐，亦恐虚名而无实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243351_comment'></div>陛下欲大有为于天下，每事不可求速，宜为之以渐，使侥倖之俗日减月脧，愈久愈效而无后悔，则善矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243351_comment'></div>以陛下之英睿果断，厉精求治，十年之后，何事不立？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243351_comment'></div>今即位未久，虽勤俭仁孝之德孚于天下，而恩泽之沾渍者尚未深也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243351_comment'></div>如此二事，关于士大夫者甚众，愿陛下姑少宽之，以为后图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243351_comment'></div>必欲稍救其弊，则亦有说矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243351_comment'></div>夫人之情笃于爱其子以及其孙，其次则兄弟若侄若甥，以至于疏属，于其至亲则利害之心切，其馀亦泛泛而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243351_comment'></div>先王因其亲疏之别，制为五服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243351_comment'></div>此人情之杀，天理之自然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243351_comment'></div>今文臣自带职朝奉郎以上隔郊奏荐，中散大夫以上每郊奏荐，太中大夫以上虽致仕遇郊亦得奏荐，其子孙近亲皆已官矣，又及其疏属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243351_comment'></div>每荐一人，有纳贿至数千缗者，其寿考之人有荐至数人者，甚无谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243351_comment'></div>今若立制：自某官以下，子孙之外不许奏期亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243351_comment'></div>某官以下，不许奏大小功亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243351_comment'></div>某官以下，不许奏缌麻亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243351_comment'></div>其许奏者，差其官品，立定员数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243351_comment'></div>以郊恩、致仕、遗表通计，数已足矣，虽有恩泽，不得奏补，只许回授与已有官人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243351_comment'></div>仍不得名他子孙为己子孙，以冒荫补，无子息者许养一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243351_comment'></div>如此，则一郊所省，文武不下数百员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1243351_comment'></div>然于其人之利害，初亦不甚切也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1243351_comment'></div>此救任子之说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1243351_comment'></div>方今科举之弊，莫甚于转运司之牒试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1243351_comment'></div>祖宗时无若是之滥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1243351_comment'></div>有避一人亲而牒三四十人者，而所谓亲未必亲也，所谓门客而未必门客也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1243351_comment'></div>每三岁诏下，士人奔走，竞求牒试，富者行贿赂，巧者干请托，改换乡井，诡冒宗支，败坏礼俗，莫此为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1243351_comment'></div>就试者十人解一人，到省则十四人取一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1243351_comment'></div>若牒一百四十人，是暗添一员省额矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1243351_comment'></div>天下每举，诸路转运司所解不下数百人，则省额安得不滥乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1243351_comment'></div>十四人之中令举一人，而馀十三人者，十七八年之后皆免解进士也，则恩榜安得而不多乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1243351_comment'></div>免解就试之人众，非徒恩榜众多，而正奏名省额亦自暗增，盖以十四人则额当取其一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1243351_comment'></div>今若将中外官门客牒邻州服属疏者免牒试，试院帘内、帘外官别作措置，仍申严保官批书之法，务在必行，则转运司试人绝少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1243351_comment'></div>每举正奏名，可减数十人，而将来免解之数又不知其几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1243351_comment'></div>此救科举之说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1243351_comment'></div>凡为此者，所以修法度、重名器、柅奸倖、覈诈欺，而于祖宗之制非有所戾也，不亦辞直而有名乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1243351_comment'></div>虽有纷纷，亦不能为患矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1243351_comment'></div>此其大略，其馀纤悉，当命有司条具以闻，而陛下审处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1243351_comment'></div>臣素怀愤世之心，最疾冒滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1243351_comment'></div>今在得言之地，遇非常之主，非不欲将顺隆旨，以一扫宿蠹，顾事有不可以骤语者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1243351_comment'></div>臣区区之愚，惟欲吾君政法流行而名誉光美，不愿求欲速之效，使兴讹造讪者得以窃议于其间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1243351_comment'></div>伏惟圣慈留神采择，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1243351_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_65_1243351_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
丽水
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　春夏间，在处州任教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年8月</a>　在处州，有代祭徽宗梓宫文。作品：代处州路祭徽宗梓宫文。<div id='poem_1243610' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243610' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243610?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代处州路祭徽宗梓宫文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243610")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243610_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243610'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243610'>功就因山，礼成启殡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243610_comment'></div>极骏奔于同轨，悉孺慕于遗黎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243610_comment'></div>汾水神游，不返唐尧之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243610_comment'></div>稽山土下，永安夏禹之藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243610_comment'></div>怀旧德以沦心，感馀民而洒血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243610_comment'></div>龙輴所届，想笳鼓以如闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243610_comment'></div>仙驭已赊，痛衣冠之永閟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243610_comment'></div>臣远分符竹，阻造园陵，式修馈奠之诚，恭致攀号之恋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1243610_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年2月9日</a>　在处州，增修处州州学，作记。作品：增修处州学记。<div id='poem_1243581' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243581' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243581?labeling=true' target='_blank'>增修处州学记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十三年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年2月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243581")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243581_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243581'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243581'>处居闽浙之郊，地偏而土瘠，视他郡为陋，前世闻人鲜焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243581_comment'></div>百年以来，衣冠盛于东南，名儒钜公磊磊相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243581_comment'></div>三岁诏下，以进士试有司者无虑数千人，取甲乙、走声名于时，踵相接也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243581_comment'></div>虽其溪山秀绝，精华磅礴之气实钟乎人物，然閟于古而发于今，岂适然也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243581_comment'></div>殆由近世承流宣化，时得其人，克敦学校之风，以作成而劝励之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243581_comment'></div>唐以前尚矣，自邺侯李繁新夫子庙养士其中，韩文公文之于碑，杜牧之书其碑阴，处州之学闻天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243581_comment'></div>历代割据，废彻扫地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243581_comment'></div>宋兴，至康定中孙威敏公首请于朝，创立黉舍，在邺侯故址之东南一里而近，其制加侈焉，士始喟然兴于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243581_comment'></div>其后或因或革，不可概考，要以一时二千石之贤否而为其盛衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243581_comment'></div>宣和中盗起睦州，隳于兵火，故侍御史黄公葆光乘残剽掇拾之馀，更造今学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243581_comment'></div>殿堂环庑，斋庖翼外，总为屋九十间有奇，而缺其三分之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243581_comment'></div>后来者欲有所加，顾力不给，则熟视罢去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243581_comment'></div>历二十年，当绍兴壬戌，天子垂意儒术，诏诸郡葺学宫，而华阳王公禔属守是州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243581_comment'></div>公达于政理，以良能称当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243581_comment'></div>其为郡如津人之操舟，纵横曲折，心谙手习，弗遽弗留，暇而必济，故承上之命敏有馀力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243581_comment'></div>通守陈公大节君子儒也，实佐佑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243581_comment'></div>越来相视，孰弊宜理，孰阙宜增，条其所宜用，下之六邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243581_comment'></div>六邑之长皆善士，乐闻其役而劝趣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243581_comment'></div>秋九月丁未丽水至，起教授厅于讲堂之东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243581_comment'></div>辛丑缙云、青田至，起执事位中门之左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243581_comment'></div>己酉松阳、遂昌至，起斋于殿廊之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243581_comment'></div>斤筑云集，耻陋矜先，于新既成，亦旧是饬，端倾除腐，暗昧载彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243581_comment'></div>周邦向风，多士滋至，乃增弟子员，益本钱百万，出廪米以赡给之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243581_comment'></div>生徒欣绘公像而祠焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243581_comment'></div>俄解印绶去，而毗陵徐公汲实来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243581_comment'></div>公老于儒学，早以德行经术为后学师表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243581_comment'></div>其治民如圃者之艺木，根深本邃，养以风雨，勿震勿挠，用观其天，庶几于教化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243581_comment'></div>视事之始，即诣泮宫，周览舍宇，问兴造之本末，曰：「七尺之躯，风骨之贵贱视其面目；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243581_comment'></div>千里之地，人材之盛衰占乎庠序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243581_comment'></div>今学之门绝居西偏，面势不端，襟抱亏缺，恐不利乎学者，盍从而新之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243581_comment'></div>诸生合辞而进，曰：「噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243581_comment'></div>前人病此久矣，而其地旧错民居，营求百方，靳不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243581_comment'></div>王公易而获之，方迁是图，去弗及举，用有遗恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243581_comment'></div>留钱二十万，以备其费，曰后有贤者成吾志焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243581_comment'></div>其有待于公也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243581_comment'></div>于是龙泉之材适至，乃规屋七楹为南北向，属之两庑，辟三门其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243581_comment'></div>所须而未具者，一瓦、一钉、一椽，市以其直，无扰于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243581_comment'></div>经始于十月之乙酉，而成于季冬之甲申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243581_comment'></div>宏正显敞，里外轩新，栋联宇匝，其气弗漏，山迎水赴，天置神设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243581_comment'></div>他日，车马从人靡限降登，旁径殿门，中贯讲舍，喧鬨杂蹂，人用弗严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243581_comment'></div>及门成，始有阃阈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243581_comment'></div>明年元日，公率僚吏谒拜圣师，下车鞠躬，屏骑从于大门外，俨俨秩秩，至者肃然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243581_comment'></div>父老嗟叹，谓自有此学，门庭几更而气象可观，莫与今比，吾邦殆其兴乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243581_comment'></div>请书其事，俾后人知所从来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1243581_comment'></div>尝闻古之诸侯，天子命之教，然后为学，直患不得为耳，曷尝得为而不为也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1243581_comment'></div>后世师帅不贤，则主德不宣、恩泽不流，虽有天子之命，鲜或能奉承之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1243581_comment'></div>幸此邦继有贤侯以克绍前烈，布宣上之德泽，惟恐弗逮，遂济厥功，可书也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1243581_comment'></div>书不书于二公何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1243581_comment'></div>虽然，使天下郡守皆如二公之贤，则圣主之德可以覃乎无外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1243581_comment'></div>使此邦之后来者能继二公之迹，则国家之泽可以垂于无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1243581_comment'></div>诚不可使无传也，于是乎书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1243581_comment'></div>绍兴十三年二月九日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1243581_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　在处州，为文祭綦崇礼。作品：祭綦内翰文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（綦崇礼《北海集》附录中卷亦载此文，即《王教授祭内翰先生文》）</span><div id='poem_1243596' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243596' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243596?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭綦内翰文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243596")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243596_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243596'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243596'>古今所难，莫如文词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243596_comment'></div>文词之中，体重而施远者，又莫难乎书命之为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243596_comment'></div>使世当承平，优游翰墨，则中人可以任职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243596_comment'></div>及乎艰难之际，呼吸变故，而发为号令，以宣道上意，则皆欲切中于事机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243596_comment'></div>如三镇诏书，使奸雄不敢顾望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243596_comment'></div>奉天赦令，虽武夫悍卒亦流涕而嗟咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243596_comment'></div>是皆系成败、关盛衰，非高世之材不能善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243596_comment'></div>故代王言者，尤难乎多事之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243596_comment'></div>国家南渡之初，倾侧扰攘，而文德广被，与武功而并驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243596_comment'></div>当是时也，公以高文大笔，振英声于翰苑者，凡历几年于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243596_comment'></div>其深厚尔雅，浑浑噩噩，以鼓动乎一世者，固无愧乎两汉之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243596_comment'></div>而隐顺体势，参揣轻重，锱铢必较，曾一字之莫移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243596_comment'></div>制诏之出，海内传诵，人皆以为得体，虽呫呫然好动其喙者，亦莫得而瑕疵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243596_comment'></div>至今北扉东阁之间，天下称以为真学士者，皆曰非我公而其谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243596_comment'></div>其学问之富，上探六经之渊奥，旁猎子史之浩博，而近尤熟于国朝一代之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243596_comment'></div>凡典章故实，与夫前辈出处之际，上下数百载间，若指诸掌而无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243596_comment'></div>此皆搢绅士大夫所共推服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243596_comment'></div>至于嘉谋硕画，密陈于中禁，而系天下之安危治乱者，则人不可得而周知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243596_comment'></div>盛德伟望，上方倚以为相，而民之无禄，忽一卧而长辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243596_comment'></div>世失名臣，文丧哲匠，所以识与不识，皆兴殄瘁之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243596_comment'></div>矧惟小子，出入门下，从容受教，盖一纪以抠衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243596_comment'></div>公不以为不肖，慰荐诱掖，矜怜抚翼之意，蒙最厚于等夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243596_comment'></div>讣音忽闻，惊涕失声，而縻于斗食，不得伸一恸于灵帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243596_comment'></div>馈奠之微，远寓千里，以致一哀而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243596_comment'></div>若乃感念旧德而怀想仪形，则不知其何日而忘之也！</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1243596_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　在处州，秦熺等成书《皇太后回銮本末》，王之望上贺表。作品：贺皇太后回銮成书表。<div id='poem_1243271' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243271' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243271?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺皇太后回銮成书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243271")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243271_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243271'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243271'>慈闱久服，大典初成，垂简策以增光，罄幅员而共庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243271_comment'></div>窃以郑开大隧，犹誇考叔之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243271_comment'></div>汉割鸿沟，乃逸侯公之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243271_comment'></div>传伤溢美，史恨阙文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243271_comment'></div>伟哉圣孝之隆，著此信书之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243271_comment'></div>恭维皇帝陛下乐天而保大，屈己以宁亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243271_comment'></div>亿万斯年，躬定太平之业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243271_comment'></div>五十而慕，日承长乐之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243271_comment'></div>冠百行以无前，作一经而诏后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243271_comment'></div>臣远将使指，阻造朝班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243271_comment'></div>编之诗书，喜铺张于伟绩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243271_comment'></div>老于文学，期歌诵于中兴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1243271_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　在处州，上书秦桧，自请其收为门徒。作品：上宰相书（某闻唐虞之世）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　在处州期间，有三贤画赞。作品：孙威敏处州郡庠三贤画赞。<div id='poem_1243589' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243589' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243589?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙威敏处州郡庠三贤画赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243589")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243589_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243589'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243589'>维威敏公，人中之龙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1243589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1243589'>谠言将略，声动华戎。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1243589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1243589'>瑰姿伟然，可想遗风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1243589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1243589'>兹维名臣，拜者肃恭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1243589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1243589'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1243589_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　在处州期间，有黄葆光画赞。作品：黄侍御葆光画赞。<div id='poem_1243588' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243588' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243588?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄侍御葆光画赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243588")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243588_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243588'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243588'>俨然正色，风宪之馀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1243588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1243588'>气恬以平，循吏之徒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1243588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1243588'>我询邦人，万口交誉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1243588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1243588'>不及见公，徵诸画图。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1243588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1243588'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1243588_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　在处州期间，有祭文。作品：处州同官祭王守阁政恭人。处州同官路祭王守恭人文。处州州学立孙威敏、黄侍御、吴冲和三贤堂祭文。处州州学上丁祭三贤文。<div id='poem_1243598' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243598' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243598?labeling=true' target='_blank'>处州同官祭王守閤政恭人文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243598")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243598_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243598'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243598'>惟夫人体钟纯懿，胄出高华，作配君子，弼成有家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243598_comment'></div>《易》称中馈，《礼》标内则，由始暨终，其仪不忒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243598_comment'></div>显显使君，四佩守符，循良之政，所至蔼如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243598_comment'></div>自家移官，厥由内辅，成此令名，夫人之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243598_comment'></div>积善之报，既寿而康，死生奄忽，理不可常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243598_comment'></div>煌煌雕轩，来未阅月，一卧不起，闻者忽咽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243598_comment'></div>凡我诸人，素仰德声，恭陈薄荐，用展哀诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1243598_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1243599' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243599' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243599?labeling=true' target='_blank'>处州同官路祭王守恭人文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243599")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243599_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243599'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243599'>夫人始来，时维孟春，鱼轩徐驱，风和日曛，鼓乐在前，迎者如云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243599_comment'></div>夫人今归，岁既暮秋，灵车遽发，云惨天愁，哀挽悽然，闻者涕流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243599_comment'></div>令德在躬，云胡不淑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243599_comment'></div>日月几何，来歌往哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243599_comment'></div>丹旐西飞，祖送倾城，道周一奠，鉴此悲诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1243599_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1243600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243600?labeling=true' target='_blank'>处州州学立孙威敏黄侍御吴冲和三贤祠堂祭文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243600")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243600'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243600'>昔蜀之儒，盛于汉时，推原其初，志则有词，曰：文翁倡其教，相如为之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243600_comment'></div>蜀人怀德，实用并祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243600_comment'></div>括苍之学，威敏始之，买田息钱，以经纪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243600_comment'></div>维时冲和，讲道于斯，风同齐鲁，冠屦委蛇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243600_comment'></div>兵火之馀，侍御改为，请书于朝，学者是资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243600_comment'></div>三贤之泽，于今不隳，相望百年，异轨同驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243600_comment'></div>侍御未远，有像巍巍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243600_comment'></div>威敏、冲和，以久见遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243600_comment'></div>我访于人，载写令仪，萃于一堂，以永厥思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243600_comment'></div>呜呼典刑，将在于兹。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1243600_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1243601' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243601' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243601?labeling=true' target='_blank'>处州州学上丁祭三贤文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243601")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243601_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243601'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243601'>猗欤三贤，泽流此邦，殁有馀思，用祠于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243601_comment'></div>仲春之月，有事上丁，敢以兹辰，并陈薄荐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1243601_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
湖北

<div class='label1' id='93129554b1924f97a7a71bceb49d3b1f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("93129554b1924f97a7a71bceb49d3b1f");'><span id='93129554b1924f97a7a71bceb49d3b1f_link'
