href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年10月</a>　到荆门军任，上到任谢表。作品：荆门军谢到任表。<div id='poem_1243272' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243272' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243272?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荆门军谢到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243272")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243272_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243272'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243272'>传经庠序，愧非重席之才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243272_comment'></div>假守湖山，更忝分符之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243272_comment'></div>肃趋官次，祗戴君恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243272_comment'></div>伏念臣穷苦寒生，羁单冷旅，始延世赏，旋策贤科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243272_comment'></div>逢圣代之崇儒，入贤关而讲艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243272_comment'></div>三年训诂，安朝暮之齑盐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243272_comment'></div>万里丘坟，感春秋之霜露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243272_comment'></div>维兹小垒，密接故乡，久深怀土之情，忽冒专城之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243272_comment'></div>田莱虽旷，已稍复于流逋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243272_comment'></div>风俗还淳，爰绝希于斗讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243272_comment'></div>获承人乏，实便己私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243272_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下功济群生，仁侔列圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243272_comment'></div>不泄迩，不忘远，允恢无外之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243272_comment'></div>在知人，在安民，犹谨维良之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243272_comment'></div>顾虽庸鄙，亦玷使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243272_comment'></div>臣敢不悉意颁宣，究心抚字！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243272_comment'></div>顾圣朝有劳来还定之政，可举而行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243272_comment'></div>使斯民无叹息愁恨之声，庶免于戾。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1243272_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　到荆门军任，上谢宰相启。作品：荆门军到任谢宰相启。<div id='poem_1243446' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243446' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243446?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荆门军到任谢宰相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243446")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243446_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243446'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243446'>分符出守，托异县以需才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243446_comment'></div>怀绶之官，入黄堂而视事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243446_comment'></div>自惟非据，深用靡遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243446_comment'></div>伏念某赋性迂疏，禀资驽下，幸逢圣世，获厕儒林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243446_comment'></div>朝暮盐齑，久享诗书之乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243446_comment'></div>春秋霜露，每怀松槚之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243446_comment'></div>惟此小邦，密邻故里，辄效一麾之请，遂成三径之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243446_comment'></div>上谷遗风，比乡闾而甚类；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243446_comment'></div>儿童尘迹，寻泉石以都迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243446_comment'></div>朋旧欢迎，妻孥交庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243446_comment'></div>服缌从事，方有改葬之图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243446_comment'></div>上冢申哀，允便过家之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243446_comment'></div>获从私愿，实出优恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243446_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官盛德格天，元勋济世，接下必期于自尽，包荒靡见于遐遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243446_comment'></div>悯兹流落之踪，惟深怀土；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243446_comment'></div>察见颛蒙之守，粗可牧民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243446_comment'></div>故于枌社之旁，畀以竹符之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243446_comment'></div>生成甚力，铭刻何言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243446_comment'></div>某敢不俯体眷怜，方图报效！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243446_comment'></div>养生送死而无憾，既曲遂于身谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243446_comment'></div>爱人利物之谓仁，当仰钧于德施。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1243446_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　到荆门军任后，谒诸庙，作谒诸庙文。作品：荆门到任谒诸庙文。<div id='poem_1243613' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243613' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243613?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荆门到任谒诸庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243613")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243613_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243613'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243613'>某猥以菲才，蒙恩出守，视事之始，恭见群祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243613_comment'></div>神以聪明正直，庙食此土，雨旸灾疠，实司其柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243613_comment'></div>惟阴相之，俾民蒙其福，则吏克有终，报事之诚，其敢有怠！</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1243613_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年11月</a>　在荆门，为王十朋母万氏夫人作墓志铭。作品：故万氏夫人墓志铭。<div id='poem_1243594' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243594' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243594?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故万氏夫人墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243594")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243594_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243594'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243594'>余为博士太学，有王生十朋者来学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243594_comment'></div>余得其程文，在百千人中卓然也，因置之异等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243594_comment'></div>其后学益邃，论议益纯，而文日益奇，月校岁考，屡先多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243594_comment'></div>绍兴十九年秋，遂试上舍为第一，诸儒厌服无异辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243594_comment'></div>俄而母夫人病，以九月某甲子卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243594_comment'></div>明年冬十有一月某甲子，与其父合葬于先茔之侧白岩之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243594_comment'></div>将葬，使其徒郑生逊志来致其辞，曰：「十朋罪逆，急一第为亲荣，鼓笥去家，而吾亲下世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243594_comment'></div>病不尝药饵，敛不视衣衾，星奔而归，阖棺在堂，叫号不闻，怀痛穷天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243594_comment'></div>已矣，虽万钟之养，亦无及矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243594_comment'></div>惟有图所以不朽者，敢丐铭先生，以掩诸幽，以赎其不孝，以慰吾兄弟之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243594_comment'></div>羸瘠馀骸，旦暮死灭，不能自致宇下，谨扶杖再拜，授书门人，惟先生哀之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243594_comment'></div>余发书流涕，时适有远役，以装遽辞，而请益勤，重伤孝子之心，乃为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243594_comment'></div>夫人姓万氏，温州乐清人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243594_comment'></div>曾祖讳文会，祖讳安，父讳勇，皆隐德不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243594_comment'></div>夫人未笄，归里人居士王君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243594_comment'></div>事舅姑以孝谨闻，姑没三十年，每春秋荐飨，哀慕如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243594_comment'></div>居士讳辅，字安民，贤而好学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243594_comment'></div>夫人习于见闻，亦知书史，能道其梗槩，每以古今篇咏口授儿辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243594_comment'></div>居家有法度，虽盛暑必正衣冠，无少长一遇以礼，见僮仆无惰容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243594_comment'></div>严于内外之分，族属非至亲不接也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243594_comment'></div>乡人春月妇人集僧舍观佛事，夫人曰：「妇人职处闺房，此何为者」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243594_comment'></div>终其身不游，宗族化之，游者为息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243594_comment'></div>居士好宾客，夫人常储馔以待，虽仓卒，办具未尝告乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243594_comment'></div>遇其子之客加厚，且能料其人，曰：「某也异日必达」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243594_comment'></div>已而果然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243594_comment'></div>居士知其才，任以家事，内外之务毕举，而尤笃于教子，爱而能严，有过者年虽长不少假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243594_comment'></div>初，居士每以学校中废为其子病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243594_comment'></div>卒之明年，太学兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243594_comment'></div>三子既除丧，夫人悉遣受业，泣送之曰：「吾割爱遣尔，岂不旦夕念哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243594_comment'></div>乃父之志不可废也，行矣勉之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243594_comment'></div>十朋文喜已出群，不蹈时俗，前此数不利场屋，夫人抚之曰：「得失有命，顾所学如何，吾不以是戚戚也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243594_comment'></div>其明达识道理类如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243594_comment'></div>十朋既知名于时，今为太学上舍生，而二弟寿朋、百朋亦以学行自立，称善士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243594_comment'></div>虽皆居士之教，而夫人之力为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243594_comment'></div>夫人享年六十有七，临终区处后事，了了不乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243594_comment'></div>三女皆淑慎，长适邑子孙彦诏，次适万世忠，能宜其家，次许嫁支鸿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243594_comment'></div>孙三人：孟甲、孟乙、孟丙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243594_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243594_comment'></div>世之贤材，多由母德，母之于子习而切，故其训易入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243594_comment'></div>如夫人贤，是宜有子哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243594_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_1243594'>妇无非仪，曷窥德美？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243594_comment'></div>欲知其人，视夫与子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243594_comment'></div>夫称善人，子腾令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243594_comment'></div>夫人之贤，厥有典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1243594_comment'></div>白岩之阡，伉俪同穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1243594_comment'></div>刻铭斯石，千载不灭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1243594_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　冬，游荆门蒙泉，作记。作品：蒙泉龙堂小记。<div id='poem_1243583' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243583' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243583?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蒙泉龙堂小记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十二年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243583")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243583_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243583'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243583'>荆门为邦，依泉而立，饮濯烹饪，咸仰以生，下流灌溉，功利尤博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243583_comment'></div>唐人题咏，目为蒙泉，而今所封实惠泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243583_comment'></div>或曰北为惠，南为蒙，蒙今微而惠特丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243583_comment'></div>惠泉故有亭给龙，扃鐍严閟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243583_comment'></div>兵火之后，结茅故基，久益隳陋，神弗顾歆，日就湮秽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243583_comment'></div>绍兴庚午冬，余始至官，览之慨然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243583_comment'></div>明年春，军城大火，载葺民居，以其工力之馀稍加疏汰，出其瓦甓榛壤，积如丘阜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243583_comment'></div>如鼻去窒，如眼去翳，源流益滋，池用净澈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243583_comment'></div>夏苦旱暵，筑坛其傍而祷焉，牲血未凝而雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243583_comment'></div>又明年春，起皇华之馆、正洗心之堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243583_comment'></div>于是部民甘懋请新泉上之亭，而甃治之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243583_comment'></div>夏四月戊子落成，坚壮雅洁，还承平之旧观，庶几九渊之灵有所凭依，以惠泽斯民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243583_comment'></div>秋复不雨，祷之又应，岁则荐稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243583_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243583_comment'></div>此邦之人戴善利侯之德，其可以怠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243583_comment'></div>十月望，军守襄阳王某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1243583_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年</a>　在荆门，有诗赋荆门皇华馆。作品：皇华馆以上巳落成因修禊事题诗纪之。<div id='poem_66540' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_66540' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/66540?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇华馆以上巳落成因修禊事题诗纪之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_66540")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_66540_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_66540'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_66540'>泉上新台紫翠环，暮春修禊俯潺湲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_66540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_66540'>汉<span class='inlineComment2'>（文津本作溪）</span>流尚带桃花水，云气初披杏子山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_66540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_66540'>柳絮轻飏晴日暖，竹光不动午阴閒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_66540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_66540'>时和岁稔游人乐，一醉聊开病守颜<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_66540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_66540'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_66540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_66540'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_66540_0'>⑴ 自注：杏子在军之西。天每欲雨则此山出云，收则雨止。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_66540_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年</a>　在荆门，有诗次韵吕愿中题皇华馆诗。作品：吕叔恭运使和题皇华馆诗复次韵。<div id='poem_66506' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_66506' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/66506?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吕叔恭运使和题皇华馆诗复次韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_66506")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_66506_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_66506'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_66506'>何处溪声响佩环，洗心堂下转潺湲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_66506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_66506'>数株古柳枯临水，百亩丛篁翠倚山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_66506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_66506'>岁久刊题多泯灭，时清景物自幽閒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_66506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_66506'>轺轩登览留佳句，顿觉林泉发妙颜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_66506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_66506'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_66506_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年</a>　在荆门，乞免除荆门军垦田税租。作品：乞展免耕垦闲田税租状。<div id='poem_1243311' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243311' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243311?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞展免耕垦閒田税租状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243311")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243311_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243311'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243311'>臣伏睹绍兴五年七月七日敕节文：诸路都督行府奏，勘会荆门军閒田甚多，召人耕垦，税租差科并免三年六料，奉圣旨依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243311_comment'></div>愚民无厌，转生奸弊，年限甫满，便辄迁徙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243311_comment'></div>臣愚欲乞将今后垦田所免税租差科三年六料展为六年，每年与免一料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243311_comment'></div>年岁既久，人亦重迁，兼每年止免一料，亦可补迁徙之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243311_comment'></div>其已免而料数未尽者，比类施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243311_comment'></div>如此，则不损朝廷宽恤之典，而民不容奸，各为长久之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243311_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1243311_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>　在荆门。春，有词寄齐尧佐。作品：丑儿奴·寄齐尧佐。<div id='poem_66627' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_66627' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/66627?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丑奴儿/采桑子<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>寄齐尧佐</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_66627")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_66627_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_66627'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_66627'>蒙泉秋色登临处，愁送将归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_66627_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_66627'>一梦经时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_66627_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_66627'>肠断佳人、犹唱渭城词。<div id='poem_sentence_2_66627_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_66627'>春来重醉分携地，人在天涯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_66627_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_66627'>别后应知。<div id='poem_sentence_4_66627_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_66627'>两鬓萧萧、多半已成丝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_66627_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年8月</a>　在荆门，代还入见，请命有司编集中兴以来宽恤诏令。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>　在荆门，有词。作品：念奴娇·荆门军宋签判陶教授许尉同坐。<div id='poem_66637' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_66637' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/66637?labeling=true' target='_blank'>念奴娇<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>荆门军宋签判、陶教授许尉同坐</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_66637")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_0_66637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_66637'>四者难并谁信道，草草幽欢能足。<div id='poem_sentence_1_66637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_66637'>美景良辰，赏心乐事，更有人如玉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_66637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_66637'>今宵此会，陋邦惊破衰俗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_66637_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_66637'>豪俊傅粉诸孙，几年分袂，一笑还相逐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_66637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_66637'>痛饮厌厌清夜永，那管更深催促。<div id='poem_sentence_5_66637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_66637'>宋玉词章，陶潜风概，况继前贤躅。<div id='poem_content_66563'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_66563'>西北峨峨叠嶂来，涛奔浪涌势难回。<div id='poem_sentence_0_66563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_66565' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/66565?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠元运使</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_66565")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_66565_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_66565'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_66565'>使节东来炯绣衣，蒙泉景色动旌旗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_66565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_66565'>官曹传檄清风肃，老稚随车淑气移。<div id='poem_sentence_1_66565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>　在荆门期间，有谢晴文。作品：荆门军谢晴文。<div id='poem_1243615' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243615' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243615?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荆门军谢晴文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1243615'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243615'>比以风雪过多，公私告病，辄输丹恳，仰叩洪私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243615_comment'></div>斋戒而云气渐开，祷祈而晴晖遂彻，精神所格，影响不愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243615_comment'></div>蒙感应以如斯，戴生成而愈笃，恭陈薄荐，用致微诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1243615_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: href='/Writing/1243614?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荆门修造祷诸庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1243614'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243614'>惟此军城，近遭回禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243614_comment'></div>悯民人之暴露，亟土木之修营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243614_comment'></div>力役既兴，工程有限，而窘兹风雨，病及公私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243614_comment'></div>用竭微诚，仰干灵祀，愿晴和之借气，俾旬月以收功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243614_comment'></div>当候落成，别图报谢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1243614_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
襄阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4c4d595dc177425c9118d76c9ebef2a2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4c4d595dc177425c9118d76c9ebef2a2");'><span id='4c4d595dc177425c9118d76c9ebef2a2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1153')">1152-1153年</a>，49-50岁</div><div id='4c4d595dc177425c9118d76c9ebef2a2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>　荆门军替回，上奏论公人无赖、不逞之徒散出乡村之害。作品：荆门军替回论禁约公人下乡奏议。<div id='poem_1243312' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243312' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243312?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荆门军替回论禁约公人下乡奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243312")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243312_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243312'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243312'>臣每伏睹朝廷所下诏令，陛下爱养元元之意可谓至矣，则四方万里民之利病，事无巨细，必欲周知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243312_comment'></div>方今郡县之间为民之害者，莫大于公人无赖不逞之徒散出乡村，乘威怙势，恐喝良善，小邀酒食，大索货财，秋取稻禾，夏求丝麦，稍不如意，鞭絷随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243312_comment'></div>民之畏怖，甚于盗贼，而郡守县令，不知禁戢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243312_comment'></div>又征税场务，私人猥多，皆鲜衣美食，肤体充盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243312_comment'></div>此辈非特丰其身以及其家，又有饮博游荡之费，何所从出？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243312_comment'></div>大抵商贾所输，官得其十之一二，以故岁课日以不登，而有司不察，犹以为征之未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243312_comment'></div>此皆公私之大蠹，而天下之所共疾者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243312_comment'></div>臣愚欲望圣慈诏诸路监司严督察州县，事非重大，不得差公人下乡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243312_comment'></div>而税场吏有定额，不得多置私人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243312_comment'></div>散出文榜，俾民通知，高立赏格，许诸色人陈告，必罚无赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243312_comment'></div>庶几农民安业，行旅通流，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243312_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1243312_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>　还家乡ang谷城。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>　在谷城。春，有诗次韵齐尧佐。作品：齐尧佐寄诗许予授代归谷城日相过次韵。<div id='poem_66516' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_66516' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_9_1243447_comment'></div>来承人乏，得便己私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243447_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官雅量镇时，英猷济物，耸缙绅之重望，膺君相之深知。<div class='inline' -----title
衡阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f233872fae62416a8947e93365842715_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f233872fae62416a8947e93365842715");'><span id='f233872fae62416a8947e93365842715_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1155')">1153-1155年</a>，50-52岁</div><div id='f233872fae62416a8947e93365842715' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年11月</a>　到任提举荆湖南路常平茶盐公事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　在衡阳，有祭家庙文。作品：衡阳祭家庙文。<div id='poem_1243606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衡州祭家庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1154年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243606")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243606'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243606'>某去岁暮春离乡造朝，九月初蒙恩假此使节，十一月末到官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243606_comment'></div>新妇、诸孙今年五月至自台州镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243606_comment'></div>去岁七月就亲于吴氏，今年三月新妇入门，与姑偕来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243606_comment'></div>踪迹不定，一年有半，祭祀旷废，夙夜不遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243606_comment'></div>惟大夫家岁时荐享，皆有仪法，是用略依古式，修三献之礼，自今已往，用以为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243606_comment'></div>古大宗小宗之制，各祀其先，绝者立后，祭不敢黩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243606_comment'></div>今十六叔有之先为之后，两房兄嫂更不置立，每遇时祭，列于从祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243606_comment'></div>五哥已葬，亦系长殇，今次于二兄之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243606_comment'></div>伏惟昭鉴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1243606_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年5月15日</a>　在衡阳，向朝廷申奏茶寇事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年9月1日</a>　在衡阳。盗贼横行，请留兵五百人戍衡、郴。朝廷从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　任职衡阳期间，有诗次韵吴芾。作品：吴明可寄诗次韵为答。<div id='poem_66518' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_66518' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/66518?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴明可寄诗次韵为答</a><span class='authorDate'>（1154年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_66518")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_66518_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_66518'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_66518'>两地相望百舍强，相思空结九回肠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_66518_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_66518'>君家沧海宾初日，我戍衡山俯夕阳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_66518_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_66518'>情话何当倾肺腑，倦游聊复信行藏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_66518_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_66518'>求田问舍真长策，捧檄荣亲道更光。<div id='poem_sentence_3_66518_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_66518'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_66518_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　在衡阳期间，有奏议论盗贼。作品：论衡阳郴州桂阳军贼盗札子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　在衡阳期间，有奏议。作品：乞分戍奏札。<div id='poem_1243314' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243314' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243314?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞分戍奏劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1154年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243314")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243314_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243314'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243314'>臣契勘武冈、全州猺贼，李道讨捕已及数分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243314_comment'></div>某询访熟溪峒事者，说杨再兴已老，诸子惟正修聚人最多，颇奸滑，正拱最凶悍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243314_comment'></div>今再兴与正拱兄弟皆得，惟正修并男杨小二、杨小三未擒，所宜必获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243314_comment'></div>然计其人众，五分无一，自不须全军在彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243314_comment'></div>若就行分拨，权屯衡、郴二州，以御盗贼，其所带潭州戍兵，亦令发还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243314_comment'></div>兼溪峒中无所用马，不若迁置平地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243314_comment'></div>武冈山路，漕运艰难，亦可少宽民力，委实便利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243314_comment'></div>乞赐详酌施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1243314_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　在衡阳期间，有奏议论差役。作品：湖南提举司论差役奏议。<div id='poem_1243315' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243315' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243315?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖南提举司论差役奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1154年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243315")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243315_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243315'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243315'>臣契勘保正差役，吏奸最多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243315_comment'></div>其所差人有未当差法者，有保正副陈诉差选不当者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243315_comment'></div>所属限一月与夺，应与夺而违限者徒一年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243315_comment'></div>绍兴十五年七月二十八日申明节文，差募之际，以籍为定，即行交替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243315_comment'></div>如有保伍内应差之人，以诈匿倖免，许被差保正长于充役以后指论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243315_comment'></div>如并计物力，委高于被差之人，轮次当差，即行改正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243315_comment'></div>然近经州郡，远经监司，文移往返，动涉时月，其承行人往往故作留滞，有所邀求，虽获改正，被差已久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243315_comment'></div>其未当差者，将来当役，又要别充二年，以此差选不当者多不能声诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243315_comment'></div>欲乞朝廷详酌，应今后保正副差选不当，后行改正者，其物力可差而轮次未到之人，候将来当差，计役过月日，通行二年交替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243315_comment'></div>其物低小，只合充大保者，候充大保，以役过月日比折，及三月以上者，与免催税一料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243315_comment'></div>其乡司人吏差选与夺，违戾情罪，自依见行条法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243315_comment'></div>如此，则设有不当，为患稍轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243315_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1243315_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　在衡阳期间，有奏议论河渡。作品：湖南提举司论河渡奏议。<div id='poem_1243316' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243316' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243316?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖南提举司论河渡奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1154年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243316")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243316_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243316'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243316'>臣到任，屡有民旅陈诉津度艰阻，多取渡钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243316_comment'></div>寻行勘会，盖缘州县榜卖河渡，实封投状之人多是过立高价以争必得，既给卖后，却以增添官钱为名，加倍收取渡钱，数年以来，此风特甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243316_comment'></div>今乡村小津渡空行人亦不下收钱一二十，担擎客旅可知，其广阔津渡又可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243316_comment'></div>农家米贱，艰于得钱，输纳税租，困于邀阻，买扑争夺，其势未已，增添之数，岂有限极？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243316_comment'></div>更一两界，行者不胜其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243316_comment'></div>然所增官钱却多拖欠，是官司得高价之虚名，而往来被邀阻之实害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243316_comment'></div>检准绍兴敕：「诸津渡堰闸无故留难人杖一百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243316_comment'></div>若非理邀求，仍就本处令众五日，兵级改差重役，馀人勒替」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243316_comment'></div>本司措置严行约束外，欲乞朝廷行下诸路，今后出卖河渡实封投状，添钱承买，价高当给之人，并从本州先次责状，不得增收渡钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243316_comment'></div>违者依非理邀求条法断罪，令众勒替，罚钱若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243316_comment'></div>关报所属县分，于渡头出榜晓示，许人陈告，以所罚钱充赏，庶得自此止绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243316_comment'></div>契勘河渡与坊场不同，坊场若增酒价，人得不沾，然酒于法有禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243316_comment'></div>河渡据往来必由之地，而擅增渡钱，尤为切害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243316_comment'></div>虽有非理邀求一条，未甚著明，若比附坊场立法，实为利便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243316_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1243316_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年4月18日</a>　为潼川府路转运判官。上谢宰相启。作品：潼川漕谢宰相启。<div id='poem_1243457' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243457' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243457?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潼川漕谢宰相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年4月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243457")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243457_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243457'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243457'>糜廪食于湘滨，已辜命节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243457_comment'></div>将转输于梓部，载误恩纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243457_comment'></div>揣分无堪，冒荣有腼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243457_comment'></div>窃以总利权于一道，外台推漕计之繁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243457_comment'></div>次地望于四川，左蜀号益都之亚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243457_comment'></div>分三铨而选吏，权万井以通商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243457_comment'></div>粤自军兴，仍多边费，四海既臻于康泰，一方未省于征求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243457_comment'></div>上轸顾忧，远加宽恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243457_comment'></div>虽事为之制，经讲画之已明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243457_comment'></div>然存乎其人，要推行之尽善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243457_comment'></div>必得异能之士，庶知协济之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243457_comment'></div>如某者赋性甚迂，理财素昧，比玷光华之选，日惟瘝旷之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243457_comment'></div>丰食货以裕民，曷裨良法；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243457_comment'></div>宣诏条而善俗，蔑布深仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243457_comment'></div>幸凭覆护之慈，未抵谴诃之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243457_comment'></div>忽惊申命，靡俟终更，专重寄于一司，补缺员于五稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243457_comment'></div>惟是久虚之选，宜升不次之才，敢谓疏愚，乃承空乏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243457_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官神功不测，元化难名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243457_comment'></div>有一德以享天心，允任大臣之重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243457_comment'></div>使万民而正王面，每勤肤使之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243457_comment'></div>致若孤踪，亦叨器使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243457_comment'></div>某敢不更殚夙夜，益守靖共！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243457_comment'></div>外竭力于一官，冀无大戾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243457_comment'></div>内矢心于九死，必报洪恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1243457_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
射洪
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='32993db4f03448b5b56b6666dd967d4a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("32993db4f03448b5b56b6666dd967d4a");'><span id='32993db4f03448b5b56b6666dd967d4a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>，52岁</div><div id='32993db4f03448b5b56b6666dd967d4a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>　赴任途中，谒射洪显惠庙，有文。作品：谒射洪显惠庙文。<div id='poem_1243618' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243618' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243618?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谒射洪显惠庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243618")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243618_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243618'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243618'>惟王生为良吏，没为明神，封爵既崇，嘉号累锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243618_comment'></div>能见物怪，出云雨，以利泽万物，威福一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243618_comment'></div>使两蜀之人，奔走祀事，可谓灵矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243618_comment'></div>某猥因行部，道出庙下，祗陈薄荐，用列微诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1243618_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
遂宁
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='41692e15bbb148c19883faa030c4a16a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("41692e15bbb148c19883faa030c4a16a");'><span id='41692e15bbb148c19883faa030c4a16a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>，52岁</div><div id='41692e15bbb148c19883faa030c4a16a' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>到任潼川府路转运判官，上谢表。作品：潼川运判到任谢表。<div id='poem_1243273' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243273' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243273?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潼川运判谢到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243273")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243273_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243273'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243273'>熊湘持节，方虞瘝旷之诛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243273_comment'></div>梓蜀观风，忽假转输之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243273_comment'></div>叨逾滋甚，感惕交深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243273_comment'></div>伏念臣儒业荒疏，吏能浅薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243273_comment'></div>比玷外台之寄，劫来南岳之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243273_comment'></div>道德意志虑于远民，虽殚夙夜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243273_comment'></div>行歛散阜通之良法，蔑效涓埃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243273_comment'></div>敢期申命之颁，曾靡终更之待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243273_comment'></div>矧潼江之一道，亚益部于四川；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243273_comment'></div>维将漕之攸司，久摄官而虚次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243273_comment'></div>俾承空乏，宜属贤能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243273_comment'></div>岂谓凡才，乃膺遴选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243273_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下躬汤一德，执舜两端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243273_comment'></div>王业载隆，久同符于治古；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243273_comment'></div>使华分遣，尤加意于遐方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243273_comment'></div>故虽绵弱之资，亦误使令之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243273_comment'></div>臣敢不悉心饷馈，毕力驰驱！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243273_comment'></div>谨留州送使之常务，一遵于宪度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243273_comment'></div>体足国裕民之制期，两便于公私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243273_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1243273_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在遂宁，论西路财计。时王之望生病。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在遂宁。生日，有词。作品：醉花阴。<div id='poem_66651' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_66651' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/66651?labeling=true' target='_blank'>醉花阴 生日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_66651")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_66651_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_66651'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_66651'>弧门此日犹能记。<div id='poem_sentence_0_66651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_66651'>叹居诸难系。<div id='poem_sentence_1_66651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_66651'>弹指片声中，不觉流年，五十还加二。<div id='poem_sentence_2_66651_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_66651'>儿童寿酒邀翁醉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_66651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_66651'>笑欣欣相戏。<div id='poem_sentence_4_66651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_66651'>休画老人星，白发苍髯，怎解如翁似。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_66651_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='381398e2c86144728fbe44ddfbe8c2fd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("381398e2c86144728fbe44ddfbe8c2fd");'><span id='381398e2c86144728fbe44ddfbe8c2fd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>，53岁</div><div id='381398e2c86144728fbe44ddfbe8c2fd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年9月13日</a>　在遂宁。朝廷降诏，重申王之望等措置四川裕民事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年9月29日</a>　在遂宁。应诏论经界利害，上奏议。作品：论潼川路措置经界奏议。<div id='poem_1243317' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243317' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243317?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论潼川路措置经界奏议<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十六年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年9月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243317")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243317_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243317'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243317'>臣契勘臣前在东南日，闻蜀中经界大为民害，豪富为奸，例获轻减，贫弱受弊，多致逃移，上户利之，而下户皆不愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243317_comment'></div>去年，臣蒙恩自湖南提举常平茶盐，除潼川府路转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243317_comment'></div>入本路境，首至广安军、渠州界，此两州尝行经界而复罢，百姓多遮道投牒乞行经界，与峡外所闻不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243317_comment'></div>深窃怪之，因问之曰：「尔等皆在上户乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243317_comment'></div>曰：「下户也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243317_comment'></div>诘其所以愿行经界之意，则曰：「人户诡名寄隐产业，有田者无户，有户者无田，而差某等充户长，催驱税赋，率皆代纳，以此破家者众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243317_comment'></div>若用经界，则户名有归，此弊可绝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243317_comment'></div>及入遂宁府境，系见行经界地分，百姓陈诉者益多，或以为便而愿行，或以为害而欲罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243317_comment'></div>因使数十朋自辩于庭下，各执偏说，互有得失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243317_comment'></div>乃知蜀中经界不论贫富，大抵税增者愿罢，税减者愿行，皆出一己之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243317_comment'></div>而形势户之不愿者为多，盖诡名挟户，非下户所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243317_comment'></div>蜀人之至东南者皆士大夫，不然则公使与富民尔，其贫弱之徒固不能远适，虽至峡外，亦无缘与士大夫接，故不愿者之说独闻，而其愿行者东南不得而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243317_comment'></div>六年之间，士人上书，百姓投状，言其不便者不知其几人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243317_comment'></div>上至朝廷省部，下至诸司郡邑，皆被烦紊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243317_comment'></div>陛下忧悯黎元，至诚无已，始也以赋税之不均而行之，终也以论诉之不息而疑之，累诏监司看详改正，有以见圣人无我，惟务便民，虽尧舜之心不能过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243317_comment'></div>然奸民观望，词讼滋繁，诸路监司累年讲究，终无为陛下别白而言之者，诚以事体至重，众口不同，利害可疑，不敢以偏辞断也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243317_comment'></div>臣初到官，适有诏旨坐知复州蜀人王骏乞罢经界劄子，委制置司与所属监司相度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243317_comment'></div>臣于部内询访甚详，而守令所陈同异相半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243317_comment'></div>臣以谓此田里间事，必尽见民情然后可决，虽有牒诉，皆一偏之论，不可凭用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243317_comment'></div>遂令州县取诸乡税名为鼠尾帐，家至户到，问其愿否，使各书其名下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243317_comment'></div>分乡编类，愿用旧税户若干，愿用经界户若干，于是究其两党之多少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243317_comment'></div>本路管一十五州，泸、叙州、长宁军以边郡不行经界，渠、果州、广安军既行而复罢，行经界者九州，凡三十七县，为税户三十三万三千七百有奇，除户绝逃移二十有四，愿行经界者一十七万七千五百馀户，愿用旧税者一十五万六千一百馀户，此其大略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243317_comment'></div>州别计之，则昌、荣、资州、怀安军四州之民愿者为多，潼川、遂宁、普州、富顺监之民愿者为少，而合州适得其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243317_comment'></div>县别计之，则愿行之多者一十有六，愿行之少者二十有一，盖由当时奉行之人有能否之不同故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243317_comment'></div>臣闻治道去太甚，虽尧舜之法不能人人皆利，要当以多者为正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243317_comment'></div>今之经界在视民愿否之多寡而损益之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243317_comment'></div>若州县之愿行者多，自不须复议，愿行者少，为之量行措置；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243317_comment'></div>人户之增减者轻，自不须复议，增减重者为之稍加裁正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243317_comment'></div>如此，则公私事省，不至甚扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243317_comment'></div>正使小有不均，亦可置而不问，何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243317_comment'></div>经界以釐正旧税，固当有所增减，减者既以为是，增者必以为非，或欲每人而悦之，是朝行夕改，无时而定也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243317_comment'></div>且蜀人之言其不便者，曰：「法行之始，验土色之高下，量顷亩之多少，奸弊百出，贿赂公行，故税之轻重不当，造帐画图为费甚广，追呼须索，不胜其扰」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243317_comment'></div>是则然矣，事在既往，虽改无及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243317_comment'></div>至于税之轻重，则新旧各有其弊，就二者而较之：经界之弊在于业多者税或轻，业少者税或重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243317_comment'></div>而旧税之弊则在于有田者或无税，有税者或无田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243317_comment'></div>要之，以轻为重、以重为轻，犹稍愈于以有为无、以无为有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243317_comment'></div>而蜀人之言其不便者，或过其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243317_comment'></div>若初行之扰则有之，而今日之弊不如是之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243317_comment'></div>臣置司遂宁，且以倚郭小溪一县论之，官户凡五百八十有四，而愿行经界者一百一十有七，不愿者四百六十有七，公吏为户二百二十有二，而愿用者一十有八，不愿者二百有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243317_comment'></div>它县大率皆然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243317_comment'></div>以此而观，则或者谓豪富之家皆获轻减而利之，岂不过哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243317_comment'></div>至于下户逃移，亦绝无仅有，或以时经旱潦，或以家自贫穷，未必皆经界所致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243317_comment'></div>传曰：「利不百，不变法」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243317_comment'></div>使经界元初不行，或行之未久而罢，固善；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1243317_comment'></div>今立为成法，已经历有年所，料旧税图籍悉多散略，中间买卖分析，户限改更，矧覈见隐寄之后，虚户尽去，创户甚多，承认供输已有定分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1243317_comment'></div>一旦举而变之，则升降纷然，侥倖复启，实户之创出者悉皆走失，虚户之诡立者不可推寻，吏肆其奸，又将有前日之扰，且终亦不得其平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1243317_comment'></div>而催科愈难，争诉益甚，军须督责，何以应期，为官吏者不亦难乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1243317_comment'></div>臣恐凋瘵之民无复宁岁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1243317_comment'></div>惟陛下少安圣虑，静以镇之，姑去其太甚者，则纷纷自息，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1243317_comment'></div>谨具错置画一下项：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1243317'>一、本路见行经界者九州三十七县，逐州人户以十分纽计，其愿用经界者，昌州得九分五釐，资州得八分九釐，怀安军得八分八釐，荣州得六分六釐，此四州民愿者多，乞且令仍旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1243317_comment'></div>普州得一分二釐，富顺监得二分五釐，遂宁府得三分四釐，潼川府得四分五釐，合州得五分一毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1243317_comment'></div>此五州民愿者少，乞量行裁正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1243317_comment'></div>臣愚欲望朝廷委监司一员，与所属守令委曲计议，各以逐处事宜从长措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1243317_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_1243317'>一、应经界县分，有所税溢于旧额者，乞令逐县取旧税额外之数，将大段增重人户通融均减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1243317_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_1243317'>一、新税不均，所合裁正者，谓元初打量顷亩、定验土色不当等户，若是未经界买卖田业，不曾推收及隐寄诡名之家，自当归并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1243317_comment'></div>即非因经界不均以至轻重如此者，不应受理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1243317_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_1243317'>一、前后经本司下状人户，有增税不及一二分而为奸猾上户驱扇，亦列名陈理，意在多将户数，皇惑官司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1243317_comment'></div>或是本户所增虽少，而诡立别名之户，当时作弊，不皆并合，却创立别户，故亦一例陈论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1243317_comment'></div>如此，则一户不愿，便是两户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1243317_comment'></div>今乞将人户经界新税比旧增减五七分以下者，更不增减，为裁正之限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1243317_comment'></div>增减数多，而非实行买卖及并合户名者，即就逐乡会集众户，如推排法，互相指决，以众證为定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1243317_comment'></div>不伏者再为界量，将量出田土没官断罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1243317_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_62_1243317'>一、乞令所委监司选差见任官五员，分诣诸县逐乡受接经界词状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1243317_comment'></div>又于本县令佐内选可委官一员通签，同共审量裁正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1243317_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_1243317'>一、所差官五员，若事毕日别无违戾，民讼稀少，乞许保明申奏朝廷，量行推赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1243317_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_1243317'>一、乞候农隙月分措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1243317_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_1243317'>右谨录奏闻，取进止。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_1243317'></div><div id='poem_sentence_66_1243317_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年9月</a>　在遂宁。上书论经界。作品：论部民诉经界书。<div id='poem_1243405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论部民诉经界书<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十八年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243405")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243405_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243405'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243405'>某契勘，四川经界惟潼川一路词讼最多，盖缘所部一十五州，有行者，有不行者，有既行而复罢者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243405_comment'></div>以此人无定志，各怀侥倖，一夫鼓扇，十百附和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243405_comment'></div>每县易一令，郡易一守，监司易一人，则境内纷然，牒诉丛委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243405_comment'></div>或讼初行之日，保正耆长因界量而受赃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243405_comment'></div>或讼既行之后，案吏乡司以走弄而取贿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243405_comment'></div>牵连枝蔓，必不可行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243405_comment'></div>所诉增重之数，多至十馀倍，少亦不下两倍，考其事实，皆未必然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243405_comment'></div>若监司守令姑务持循，则不过取会行移，受其烦紊而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243405_comment'></div>或者未详情伪，喜任更张，则信其偏词，便有损益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243405_comment'></div>县不禀州，州不告监司，监司不以闻于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243405_comment'></div>乡异邑殊，前行后止，贿赂狼藉，请托公行，失陷赋租，害及贫弱，使经常之赋无复定制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243405_comment'></div>如是者八九年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243405_comment'></div>某前备员转运判官，奉诏看详措置经界利害，因上便民事，内一项专论经界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243405_comment'></div>乞将本路不均甚处，委监司一员与所属守令委曲计议，各以事宜，从长措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243405_comment'></div>仍选见任官五员，农隙月分分诣诸县，逐乡受接人户词状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243405_comment'></div>其所诉元初打量步亩、定验土色不当，增减税数至五七分以上者，会集众户，如推排法互相指决，以众證为定，不伏者再为界量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243405_comment'></div>若是未经界买卖田业，不曾推收，及隐寄诡名之家，自当归并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243405_comment'></div>而非经界不均以致轻重者，更不受理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243405_comment'></div>逐县经界所税有溢于旧额者，以额外之数与增重人户通融均减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243405_comment'></div>既已奏闻，又具状劄缴申庙堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243405_comment'></div>伏蒙仆射相公特赐主张，取旨依申，如有人户论诉去处，照应前后指挥施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243405_comment'></div>某遵依前件圣旨，遂令逐县勒乡司先将未经界前一年并经界一年新旧税簿逐一较对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243405_comment'></div>取见新税比旧增减及五七分以上人户，具帐供申，不得追集人民，有所骚扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243405_comment'></div>其以前人户论诉多是虚词滥说，不可凭用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243405_comment'></div>遂修立状式，雕版印造，分送诸县，晓示百姓：如不愿裁正，更不须下状；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243405_comment'></div>若愿裁正，即请买状式具实书填，经所委官投押。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243405_comment'></div>若有指决，不得过三户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243405_comment'></div>再限一月，出限更不受状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243405_comment'></div>自绍兴二十七年十月后选差清彊官，分诣经界不均县分裁正，其词讼不多去处，只就本县委官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243405_comment'></div>缘本司所立状式关防周密，杜绝弊幸，无所容奸<span class='inlineComment2'>（状式已具册内。）</span>，其从来妄状鼓扇，烦紊官司之人，皆不复欺诞滥有披陈，以致词讼不烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243405_comment'></div>某又疑县道及所委官惮于裁正，抑遏百姓，不令声说，累次严行约束，及密切询访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243405_comment'></div>委是少有请买状式之人，亦有书填不行，既买复还者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243405_comment'></div>据所委官申，皆只就县受状，不曾下乡，不曾追集百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243405_comment'></div>多是以逐处溢额税数与偏重人户对减，民间亦少相指决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243405_comment'></div>虽间有被决增税之家，亦情愿承受，别无争执。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243405_comment'></div>以此田亩并不曾复行界量，吏民并无责罚，公私无毫发之扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243405_comment'></div>未结绝间，某蒙恩就除提点刑狱公事，遂申尚书省，乞就宪司结绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243405_comment'></div>于今年三月以前并已了毕，溢额税色纽计钱四千八百五十馀贯，庄租麦四石有奇，对减税重人户五千六百八十五户，用人户科决状推排减偏重税八十九户，增偏轻税一百六十六户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243405_comment'></div>已出榜晓示百姓，认定供输，自此永绝词讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243405_comment'></div>方推行之始，人见其事体浩大，皆谓争诉必多，收之为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243405_comment'></div>及状式一出，奸民往往引退，讼牒甚少，异论已息，然犹疑有所骚动，非一二年未易遽了。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243405_comment'></div>已而略无一事，数月而毕，皆翕然帖伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243405_comment'></div>自非仆射相公聪明远烛，洞见万里之外，兼收博采，不以人废其言，则一方宿弊，岂能尽去？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243405_comment'></div>今已具录奏及申尚书省，又缮写成册，投纳府第，以便省览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1243405_comment'></div>某自入蜀以来，日为经界词讼所扰，深疾奸弊，求所以安人息讼，可以经久之策甚详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1243405_comment'></div>每士大夫陈述、百姓诉理，人人与之论辨，参稽讲究，备见本末，踰年始敢上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1243405_comment'></div>既蒙朝廷听委，则说谕守令，选择官僚，审谨而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1243405_comment'></div>若今后官吏士民尚敢扇摇，欲复行旧税以疑误百姓者，乞从所属具事因申奏，重寘于法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1243405_comment'></div>庶几远民得安业一方，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1243405_comment'></div>其普州安岳一县不均最甚，措置裁正比它县尤为详悉，已别具劄子申呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1243405_comment'></div>并乞钧照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1243405_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年9月</a>　在遂宁。有状论安岳县经界。作品：改正安岳县经界状。<div id='poem_1243318' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243318' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243318?labeling=true' target='_blank'>改正安岳县经界状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243318")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243318_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243318'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243318'>臣契勘普州安岳县初行经界日，县令张宁大为奸弊，改移税额，轻重失平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243318_comment'></div>比及三年，亏官二十五万七千馀贯，依圣旨除放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243318_comment'></div>自绍兴二十四年至今，又亏一十二万四千馀贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243318_comment'></div>绍兴二十三年，县官以阙乏之故，分诣诸乡巡门驱歛，村民不堪其扰，结集山谷间，抗敌官吏，几致生事，至今土人谓之垛山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243318_comment'></div>垛山者，言山上之人其多如堆垛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243318_comment'></div>臣前在转运司，令诸县作鼠尾帐，家至户到，遍问百姓，愿用新税或旧税，各令亲书于名下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243318_comment'></div>独安岳一县愿用旧税者十分之九，公私俱病，民不聊生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243318_comment'></div>臣于去年冬，选委昌州推官左从事郎刘弇，同县令右从政郎张介受状、措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243318_comment'></div>凡三百六十馀状，指决干连者不下千五百家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243318_comment'></div>若只量行裁正，则无由去偏重不均之弊，若尽行覈实，则有追集丈量之扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243318_comment'></div>弇与守令皆谓欲救其弊，莫若顺民之情，复用旧税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243318_comment'></div>臣以本县经界所失虽多，亦不可尽废，遂令将新旧税簿互相参校，于所增减，取其酌中分数，通融裁正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243318_comment'></div>凡新税之增于旧税者，以所增十分为率，减其七分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243318_comment'></div>新税之减于旧税者，以所减十分为率，复其六分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243318_comment'></div>谓如某人户下元管旧税一百文，经界日增至二百文，即裁减七十文，作一百三十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243318_comment'></div>某人户下元管旧税二百文，经界日减至一百文，即却复六十文，作一百六十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243318_comment'></div>盖经界增者重，减者轻，故今所损益者有多少之差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243318_comment'></div>元申画指挥增减不及五七分，则不在裁正之限，今此一县其弊至深，不可以五七分为限，故自二分以上皆裁正之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243318_comment'></div>本县经界增税者四千五百七户，计增正税钱三十八贯八百一十二文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243318_comment'></div>今减其七分，为钱二十七贯一百六十有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243318_comment'></div>经界减税者六千一百二十二户，计减正钱四十贯七十五文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243318_comment'></div>今复其六分，为钱二十四贯四十有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243318_comment'></div>其增减不及二分者，新税簿籍脱漏户限为多，可见者计二千九百馀户，若一一纽算裁正，又恐太烦，若只用新税，则漏户不可复得，遂仍以旧税为正，计减却正税钱五贯五百有奇，却收漏户二千七百馀户，得正税钱八贯七百有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243318_comment'></div>又根括到失陷税钱，补足旧税外有溢额者四贯三百有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243318_comment'></div>以此数项衮同对补，裁减之数于租额尚有赢馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243318_comment'></div>又张宁经界之初，既失税额，恐岁计不敷，则擅增折变以补之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243318_comment'></div>每正税一钱，增米三合、麦二合，大率比旧加十分之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243318_comment'></div>今一切蠲除，悉依现例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243318_comment'></div>凡上件措置，皆委曲计议，务尽人情，轻重适中，更无不均之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243318_comment'></div>百姓租税各有归著，易于催理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243318_comment'></div>自此官赋无复失陷，委为经久之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243318_comment'></div>其裁正曲折，别编作一册奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1243318_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='1bcfebfad2ab4b18ba8465f927c12554_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1bcfebfad2ab4b18ba8465f927c12554");'><span id='1bcfebfad2ab4b18ba8465f927c12554_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1157')">1156-1157年</a>，53-54岁</div><div id='1bcfebfad2ab4b18ba8465f927c12554' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年10月27日</a>　在遂宁。上札子乞裁减四川赡军之费。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年1月24日</a>　在遂宁。奏减军中冗食浮费，复捐以裕民。高宗云王之望有爱民之志，但临事不审，率尔有请。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年3月24日</a>　在遂宁。用王之望等请，朝廷诏减三川对籴米。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年3月</a>　在遂宁。上奏论铜山县铜事。作品：论铜坑朝札。<div id='poem_1243375' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243375' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243375?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论铜坑朝劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243375")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243375_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243375'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243375'>某去年八月二十日准尚书省劄子，委措置铜山县铜事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243375_comment'></div>寻差知涪城县姜宿前去检踏，缘本官差充类试官，别选怀安军金水县丞赵纯、权遂宁府蓬溪县酒税胡宰，分诣逐处相度措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243375_comment'></div>某亦蒙制置司差充类试所考试官，至成都府界，以朝廷专委辞行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243375_comment'></div>九月初十日径到铜山县，躬亲相视，广行询访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243375_comment'></div>其新旧铜窟凡二百馀所，匠户近二百家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243375_comment'></div>与郪县出铜器地名于打铜村相去数十里，其于打铜村铸造之家亦百馀户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243375_comment'></div>初谓所产铜矿大段浩瀚，每岁欲且立万斤为额，而民户哀诉不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243375_comment'></div>某委曲说谕，诘以铜窟、铜匠、铸铜之家如此之多，岂得谓之无铜，且县号铜山，此名不应虚得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243375_comment'></div>今朝廷以铸钱阙铜，遍行搜括，知尔县所出不赀，专委漕臣措置，岂容尔辈尚专其利？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243375_comment'></div>可依实认额，毋取罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243375_comment'></div>其老宿等对曰：「此县铜矿有无不常，每遇一窟苗脉尽灭，即于旁近寻访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243375_comment'></div>窟之深者至数十百丈，若是坑苗丰盛，岂有弃旧图新？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243375_comment'></div>今新旧二百馀窟，见可采者只一十七处，后又添两窟，窟之多盖以铜之少也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243375_comment'></div>诸村匠户多以耕种为业，间遇农隙，一二十户相纠入窟，或有所赢，或至折阅，系其幸不幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243375_comment'></div>其间大半往别路州军铜坑盛处趁作工役，非专以铜为主，而取足于此土也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243375_comment'></div>其郪县于打铜村所铸器物，多是汉州及利州大安军等处客贩之铜，又四川贩铜悉集于此，故铜器为多，不皆出于本县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243375_comment'></div>县虽以铜得名，然非严道邓通所赐之铜山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243375_comment'></div>《图经》载唐《地理志》，贞观二十三年置铸钱官，至调露元年即罢，可见此县产铜自来不多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243375_comment'></div>数十年前有窟二十二处，每年人户认铜三百六十五斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243375_comment'></div>政和年中宪漕两司各遣官重行检踏，只七窟有苗，馀一十五处无可采取，止于七窟上量添铜二十一斤而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243375_comment'></div>非不欲多增，势不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243375_comment'></div>某等伏睹榜示，亦知朝廷搜括铜宝甚急，于使司赏罚非轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243375_comment'></div>本县山僻，无监司巡按数十年矣，今使者亲来宿留累日，岂敢以多为少，欺罔官司乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243375_comment'></div>乞从使司严行禁绝，如有藏匿铢两，衷私货卖，甘伏重罪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243375_comment'></div>某亦未以为然，遂籍匠户分窟取矿，置场拘收烹鍊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243375_comment'></div>以十月为头，仍差赵纯权铜山令，专主其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243375_comment'></div>至十一月末，兼中间有闰，凡三个月，每月趁办不及五百斤，甚费督责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243375_comment'></div>又民户陈诉不一，盖缘诸窟散在山乡山谷五七十里之间，难于拘籍，遂再委姜宿前去子细审量措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243375_comment'></div>凡阅两月，方得就绪，每月及五百斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243375_comment'></div>今每岁以六千斤为额，遇闰更加五百斤，已别具状画一申尚书省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243375_comment'></div>自十月至正月五个月，收到铜二千五百斤，见行起发，通先所起拘到器物铜，共计一万一百三十三斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243375_comment'></div>窃缘创行之初，事涉经久，非审见的确利害，未敢条上，以此稍稽月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243375_comment'></div>某不才，伏蒙廊庙曲加记录，特赐任使，实不敢不尽疲驽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243375_comment'></div>伏惟钧慈特赐照察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1243375_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

中江
