-----title
三台
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a700e48cabfd45d5834f17526099fe3b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a700e48cabfd45d5834f17526099fe3b");'><span id='a700e48cabfd45d5834f17526099fe3b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>，53岁</div><div id='a700e48cabfd45d5834f17526099fe3b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年9月</a>　在梓潼。以转运判官行部至梓州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d3bea64f0bf042b69ef244c800bb9750_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d3bea64f0bf042b69ef244c800bb9750");'><span id='d3bea64f0bf042b69ef244c800bb9750_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1158')">1157-1158年</a>，54-55岁</div><div id='d3bea64f0bf042b69ef244c800bb9750' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年6月4日</a>　改提点本路刑狱公事。上到任谢表。作品：潼川提刑谢到任表。<div id='poem_1243274' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243274' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243274?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潼川提刑谢到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年6月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243274")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243274_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243274'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243274'>久司飞挽之权，曾微善最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243274_comment'></div>就易平反之职，不改部封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243274_comment'></div>命节增华，汗颜有腼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243274_comment'></div>伏念臣早专朴学，晚窃贤科，顾朝廷渥泽之所加，何臣子涓埃之足道！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243274_comment'></div>祗安愚分，忽误明恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243274_comment'></div>维谏官御史之昌言，必大夫国人之公论，敢图列荐，滥采虚名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243274_comment'></div>遂烦圣造之曲成，斯实清时之盛美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243274_comment'></div>资联内阁，奉裕陵丕显之谟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243274_comment'></div>体重外台，光蜀道皇华之遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243274_comment'></div>静思疏逖，可谓超逾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243274_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下日月照临，乾坤覆育，申九歌于帝典，严八柄于天官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243274_comment'></div>信任臣邻，曾四目四聪之弗壅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243274_comment'></div>甄明爵赏，虽一嚬一笑以无私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243274_comment'></div>致若孤踪，亦膺异宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243274_comment'></div>臣敢不激昂晚暮，黾勉事功！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243274_comment'></div>云汉昭回，方问乘槎之上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243274_comment'></div>井参扪历，更输叱驭之忠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1243274_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年8月</a>　移节至潼川宪治。到任后，上谢宰相启。作品：潼川宪到任谢宰相启。<div id='poem_1243459' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243459' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243459?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潼川宪到任谢宰相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243459")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243459_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243459'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243459'>久叨饷馈之司，曾无政绩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243459_comment'></div>就易平反之任，不敢抚封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243459_comment'></div>命节增华，汗颜有腼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243459_comment'></div>伏念某早专朴学，晚抗尘容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243459_comment'></div>横经首善者始终五年，随牒外方者俛仰十稔，一纡守绂，三假使轺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243459_comment'></div>比将漕以充员，适励精之更化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243459_comment'></div>轻徭薄赋，务宣布于深恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243459_comment'></div>激浊扬清，式钦承于休德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243459_comment'></div>岂但转输之辄办，必期凋瘵以兼收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243459_comment'></div>使巴山万里之遥，如甸服一圻之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243459_comment'></div>至于刬除民蠹，禁戢吏奸，力虽倍以何功，心愈劳而更拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243459_comment'></div>徒依庥庇，未被谴诃，敢图瘝旷之馀，亦玷陶镕之末！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243459_comment'></div>飞刍挽米，既辞计事之烦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243459_comment'></div>揽辔登车，仍正职司之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243459_comment'></div>叨逾已甚，称塞维艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243459_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官道贯王猷，功熙帝载，名世乃圣人之遇，求贤真宰相之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243459_comment'></div>为桷为杗，校群材而并用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243459_comment'></div>采葑采菲，收片善以无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243459_comment'></div>顾若疏愚，误膺知奖，每自惭于谫薄，尤重费于生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243459_comment'></div>谓涪潼之间，固已粗谙于摩抚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243459_comment'></div>则刑罚之寄，或能上体于哀矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243459_comment'></div>因俾岁迁，实为侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243459_comment'></div>某敢不益殚夙夜，勉副使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243459_comment'></div>叱驭输忠，庶家风之未泯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243459_comment'></div>捐躯报效，岂国士之难追。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1243459_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年9月</a>　有启贺陈康伯除参知政事。作品：贺陈参政启。<div id='poem_1243521' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243521' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243521?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺陈参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243521")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243521_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243521'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243521'>光膺命綍，擢秉政机，四方耸闻，万口同庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243521_comment'></div>窃以聪明之主，或旷世莫值其臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243521_comment'></div>贤哲之人，有终身不获其位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243521_comment'></div>自昔所叹，相逢甚难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243521_comment'></div>当上圣之励精，操至权而御下，爰得风云之佐，仰符梦卜之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243521_comment'></div>事非偶然，功可立待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243521_comment'></div>恭惟某官气雄百辟，名重三朝，堂堂表特立之规，凛凛守后凋之操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243521_comment'></div>稽山啸傲，挹外监之高标；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243521_comment'></div>江左招徕，踵太常之旧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243521_comment'></div>粤升法从，益茂英猷，奋巨力以回天，竭孤忠而贯日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243521_comment'></div>刊修史牒，启沃经帏，遍仪禁路之华，妙极儒林之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243521_comment'></div>既论思之见效，宜倚注之弥深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243521_comment'></div>以三十年难进之资，应五百岁非常之运，遂膺图任，入预弼谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243521_comment'></div>人期致主之秋，帝恨用公之晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243521_comment'></div>必将讲明宪度，复列圣之宏规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243521_comment'></div>寝息兵刑，毕真儒之能事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243521_comment'></div>尽摅素志，以阐洪猷，茂凝钟鼎之勋，嗣正钧衡之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243521_comment'></div>某远将使指，窃听宸纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243521_comment'></div>大厦斯成，喜究梓人之用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243521_comment'></div>馀光可借，宁忧绩女之贫？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243521_comment'></div>寒律方严，台阶正邈，愿加调于鼎养，用下答于岩瞻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1243521_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年10月29日</a>　上奏状言放税。作品：潼川路放税利害状。<div id='poem_1243319' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243319' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243319?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潼川路放税利害状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年10月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243319")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243319_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243319'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243319'>臣准御宝封下尚书省劄子，坐奉圣旨指挥，将州县旱伤去处依条检放，仍支拨常平钱米措置赈济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243319_comment'></div>仰惟朝廷轸念远民，救灾恤穷之意可谓深至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243319_comment'></div>本司已即时行下诸州遵奉施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243319_comment'></div>据诸州申到，自夏及秋，限内不曾有人户陈诉，其田亩各改种了当，别无根查存在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243319_comment'></div>检准绍兴敕令节文：「诸官私田灾伤，夏苗以四月，秋苗以七月，水田以八月，听经陈诉，至月终止诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243319_comment'></div>在限外不得受理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243319_comment'></div>如未检覆而改种者，并量留根查，以备检视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243319_comment'></div>不愿作灾伤者听」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243319_comment'></div>今来圣旨指挥，系令依条检放，合遵上件条令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243319_comment'></div>缘所降指挥于十一月内被受，既限内无人户陈诉，又已改种，无根查可检，难以检放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243319_comment'></div>若复差官遍诣乡村，徒为纷扰，有力者得以计嘱，贫乏未必得免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243319_comment'></div>原灾伤所以放税，盖为人户不能输送。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243319_comment'></div>今年本路秋税已纳及八分以上，自无支还之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243319_comment'></div>若用对折来年税赋，倘遇丰熟，却反是丰年减放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243319_comment'></div>若不于来年对减，只据目今未纳之数蠲放，即是顽猾人户独得侥倖，而依时送纳善良之民反不蒙实惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243319_comment'></div>兼今未纳馀分，多是揽纳者已行结览，实启奸弊，官司空失岁计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243319_comment'></div>臣照得前者三司措置惠民画降圣旨，自今年秋科为头，尽除对籴米一项，比之旧额已减三分之一，宽恤不为不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243319_comment'></div>已行下一路，照会所有赈济一节，则于常平法旱伤去处失于披诉者，许放第四等已下阙食人户，自不相妨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243319_comment'></div>已关常平司施行外，谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1243319_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年10月29日</a>　上奏状言旱灾。作品：论赈济灾伤去处状。<div id='poem_1243320' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243320' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243320?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论赈济灾伤去处状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年10月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243320")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243320_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243320'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243320'>臣准御宝封下尚书省劄子，坐奉圣旨指挥，将州县旱伤去处依条检放，仍支拨常平钱米措置赈济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243320_comment'></div>本司已即时行下诸路遵奉施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243320_comment'></div>检准《绍兴重修常平免役令》：「诸灾伤计一县放税不及七分，或失于披诉，第四等已下阙食户，当职官保明，申提举司审度，依放税七分法赈给借贷讫奏本司」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243320_comment'></div>已遵上条，委本路州县当职官体量，自第四等以下阙食户，勒耆保尽实抄劄，支拨常平义仓米斛应副赈给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243320_comment'></div>如本州属县有阙常平米斛，系沿流县分，即自本州量度数目支拨，津载前去；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243320_comment'></div>如不系沿流去处，即行本处兑换税米支散，据用过数将在州常平义仓拨还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243320_comment'></div>若无合兑换税米，即行约度合用米数，估定在市实价，具数申本司，以凭通融一路之数移用，支本钱前去籴买应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243320_comment'></div>内遂宁府、果、普州见管义仓斛斗比诸州数多，亦行下量减价钱出籴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243320_comment'></div>见据遂州申，已行抄劄到本州县界实被旱伤去处孤老残疾不能自存阙食饥民人数，自十二月初六日以后赈给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243320_comment'></div>缘本路诸县地里相近，虑有两处重叠请给，已依条定日行下诸州，每月取二日、七日，五日一次，同日支散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243320_comment'></div>内饥民若系附郭近便人，即五日一支，若系三十里外人，即十日一支，庶免饥羸之人往来频并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243320_comment'></div>如有后到人数，即续行抄劄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243320_comment'></div>其馀不甚旱伤州县，亦已行下检举老疾贫乏不能自存及乞丐人，依条养济去处讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243320_comment'></div>见今本路诸州所管常平义仓钱米可以通融应副周足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243320_comment'></div>其旧抚司桩积钱更不敢取用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243320_comment'></div>如将来青黄未接，饥民大段数多，常平钱米或至有阙，即申报所属取拨施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243320_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1243320_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　冬，为遂宁冯耔作墓志铭。作品：遂宁冯耔君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1243593' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243593' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243593?labeling=true' target='_blank'>遂宁冯君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243593")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243593_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243593'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243593'>冯氏之先避唐末之乱，自秦入蜀，兄弟三人，散居遂、普、绵三州间，皆为著姓，而遂州之冯多隐君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243593_comment'></div>君遂之小溪人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243593_comment'></div>曾祖讳尧民，以经术操行高于蜀，闻于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243593_comment'></div>仁宗时再锡粟帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243593_comment'></div>熙宁初召试舍人院，不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243593_comment'></div>其生也，何公圣从论荐甚力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243593_comment'></div>殁则无尽张公以文表其墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243593_comment'></div>子孙世其风流，故居者重于出处，仕者轻于去就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243593_comment'></div>皇祖讳正雅，明经中第，元符间提举三门辇运，以上书言事免，与其弟正卿皆名刊党石，终朝奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243593_comment'></div>皇考讳芝，五试礼部不第，州举八行，辞不应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243593_comment'></div>乡人称为小隐君，以别于其大父云，赠右承事郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243593_comment'></div>二子，长曰耘，以祖任入官，锁其厅试，上舍登科，亦恬于进取，终左奉议郎、利州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243593_comment'></div>君其季也，讳耔，字与忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243593_comment'></div>力学多闻，居家孝友，与奉议公同居四十馀年，雍睦无间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243593_comment'></div>宗族之贫不能婚嫁者，君任其责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243593_comment'></div>绍兴初党禁解，大夫公始得致仕恩，补君将仕郎，非其志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243593_comment'></div>诸台数辟，置不就，乃择君所便，屈监荆井镇酒税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243593_comment'></div>荆井去家不百里，亲旧劝驾，君忻然从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243593_comment'></div>踰月即弃去，遂终身不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243593_comment'></div>浮沉里闾，日与宾客谈笑把酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243593_comment'></div>笃于风义，施穷周急，不计有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243593_comment'></div>四方游士至遂者皆主于君，馆之虽久，不厌益欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243593_comment'></div>一时名人，多与定交，或为文词以赞颂其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243593_comment'></div>君性乐易纯诚，不与物忤，而遇事分别是非，确然不可夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243593_comment'></div>乡党爱而畏之，咸取直焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243593_comment'></div>古所谓一乡之善士，其君之徒欤，年五十有九，以微疾终于家，实绍兴丁丑季冬之丁巳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243593_comment'></div>始娶潼川王氏，左通议大夫维之女；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243593_comment'></div>今夫人普慈王氏，左朝散郎深之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243593_comment'></div>男曰稷，左迪功郎、泸南沿边安抚司准备差使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243593_comment'></div>曰吴帅，早夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243593_comment'></div>女曰穆，嫁乡贡进士李朴而卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243593_comment'></div>曰稛，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243593_comment'></div>稷学行修整，敏秀而文，余使诸儿从授学焉，因得与君游，知君为详，是宜其有子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243593_comment'></div>累世隐德，其将发于斯乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243593_comment'></div>稷将以某年月日葬君某所，请铭，余不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243593_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1243593'>出处何常，惟其所适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243593_comment'></div>不违己以徇物，则超然于欣戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243593_comment'></div>君蕴不施，其志则逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243593_comment'></div>归安此丘，子孙逢吉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1243593_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年3月28日</a>　乞行下州县解决经界不均问题，遵守施行税法。从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　有状论赈济。作品：论赈济状。<div id='poem_1243321' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243321' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243321?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论赈济状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243321")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243321_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243321'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243321'>臣去年十一月伏准省劄，备奉圣旨，支拨常平钱米赈济实被旱伤去处，或支用不足，即于存留旧宣抚司桩积钱米取拨本司措置，行下州县，依条体量，自第四等以下阙食，以常平义仓米斛赈给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243321_comment'></div>如本州属县米斛有阙，系沿流县分，即自本州量度数目支拨前去；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243321_comment'></div>如不系沿流去处，即行下本处兑换税米支散，据用过数将在州常平义仓拨还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243321_comment'></div>若无合兑换税米，即约度合用米数，估定在市实价，具数申本司，以凭通融一路之数移用，支本钱前去籴买应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243321_comment'></div>遂宁府等州见管斛斗比诸州数多，即令减价出粜，据荣、叙、泸州、长宁军、富顺监申，不系旱伤州县，别无阙食饥流民外，潼川、遂宁、果、合、昌、普、资、渠州、怀安军申劄到阙食饥民人数，今自十二月初六日以后节次赈给，至今年三月终止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243321_comment'></div>共赈济过饥民一万八千六百六十人，斛斗一万一千四百八十二石二斗，出籴过斛斗五千七十石三斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243321_comment'></div>普州安居、乐至县钱米不足，于潼川府通融应副过钱引三千八十五道七百七十六文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243321_comment'></div>其旧宣抚司桩积钱米不曾取拨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243321_comment'></div>州县官吏推行有稍不如法者，亦惩治一二处，以此不敢违戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243321_comment'></div>朝廷实惠得以下及于民，一路之间并无流殍，利泽洋溢，歌颂蔼然，真盛德事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243321_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1243321_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年4月16日</a>　为成都府路转运副使。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
广汉
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='80f335e32b7e44b090de961c6b6420cd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("80f335e32b7e44b090de961c6b6420cd");'><span id='80f335e32b7e44b090de961c6b6420cd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>，55岁</div><div id='80f335e32b7e44b090de961c6b6420cd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　赴任途中，在汉州德阳县鹿头关有祭白马庙文。作品：祭鹿头关白马庙文。<div id='poem_1243607' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243607' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243607?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭鹿头关白马庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243607")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243607_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243607'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243607'>惟神声蔼凤雏，才标骥足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243607_comment'></div>蚤负济时之略，出依图霸之雄，倾侧荆湘，崎岖巴蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243607_comment'></div>方将与孔明而并骛，致昭烈于中兴，而逢辰不祥，当壮而殒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243607_comment'></div>气吞万斛，折辕轴于户庭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243607_comment'></div>志在九霄，摧羽毛于寻丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243607_comment'></div>凛英灵于千载，兹庙食于一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243607_comment'></div>某世乃襄人，神之邑子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243607_comment'></div>读《耆旧》、《先贤》之传，遐想高风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243607_comment'></div>游汉皋、岘首之间，每悲陈迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243607_comment'></div>今者将输益部，取道祠前，瞻古像以欷歔，吊孤坟而流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243607_comment'></div>时虽异代，义岂忘情？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243607_comment'></div>荐明信于一觞，感盛衰而三叹，庶几遗烈，俯鉴鄙诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1243607_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
成都
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='686a252aa8a84717bc6ae3f3d403a8c5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("686a252aa8a84717bc6ae3f3d403a8c5");'><span id='686a252aa8a84717bc6ae3f3d403a8c5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1160')">1158-1160年</a>，55-57岁</div><div id='686a252aa8a84717bc6ae3f3d403a8c5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　赴任途中，在成都县江渎王庙有谒庙文。作品：谒江渎王庙文。<div id='poem_1243616' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243616' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243616?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谒江渎王庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243616")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243616_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243616'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243616'>惟神发源灵长，经营于九州之半，浸溉利泽，殆与天地分功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243616_comment'></div>庙食蜀都，威神显赫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243616_comment'></div>某自幼至老，溯沿大江四十馀年，而无风波之虞者，实神之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243616_comment'></div>今以职事，实来是邦，其敢不拜祠下！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243616_comment'></div>区区之诚，惟神其鉴之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1243616_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　赴任途中，在成都县江渎王庙有奏科约文。作品：江渎庙奏科约文。<div id='poem_1243617' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243617' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243617?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江渎庙奏科约文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243617")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243617_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243617'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243617'>漕运之司，岁有科约，制一路财赋之出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243617_comment'></div>益部废而不讲，已更十年，州郡出纳，无以检束，奸弊百出，公私告病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243617_comment'></div>某承乏计事，复修旧籍，郡为一编，凡十有六帙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243617_comment'></div>念天地之间，幽有鬼神，明有官吏，公家之利病，民生之休戚，惟吏与神分掌其柄，故官法之所不及者，鬼得而诛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243617_comment'></div>惟神尊居四渎，功利半天下，而发源启庙，实在此都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243617_comment'></div>福善祸淫，神得司之，则于一路财赋经常之制，不可以无所稽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243617_comment'></div>是用焚献一部，以助神之威灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243617_comment'></div>若其蔑弃有司之籍，蠹耗邦财，以欺天而虐民者，神其鉴之！</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1243617_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　在成都有祭武侯庙文。<div id='poem_1243608' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243608' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243608?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭武侯庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243608")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243608_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243608'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243608'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243608_comment'></div>公才命世，王佐之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243608_comment'></div>若在唐虞，皋夔可希；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243608_comment'></div>使遇汤武，伊周庶几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243608_comment'></div>其治巴蜀，因蜀制宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243608_comment'></div>较其蕴蓄，十未一施；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243608_comment'></div>用于神州，岂止如斯？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243608_comment'></div>蜀政宽弛，萎弱不持，公检以法，上尊下卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243608_comment'></div>蜀兵脆怯，折北不支，公御以严，侮敌畏威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243608_comment'></div>蜀尚文雅，华实多违，公取有用，不主夸毗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243608_comment'></div>蜀喜侈靡，民无宿赀，公率以躬，明示轨仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243608_comment'></div>蜀风和易，各私所私，公莅以公，秋毫莫欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243608_comment'></div>有功必赏，虽仇弗遗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243608_comment'></div>有罪必罚，虽亲不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243608_comment'></div>法不尽用，惟仁是依，伏罪输诚，贷则有辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243608_comment'></div>蜀在三国，地小兵羸，如其不武，坐底陵夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243608_comment'></div>公用其众，振起衰微，以攻为守，屡耀其师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243608_comment'></div>南中六郡，懭悍莫羁，公服其心，听我抚绥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243608_comment'></div>三郡来降，进取迟迟，量力而动，不开祸机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243608_comment'></div>谋人之国，托受孤儿，宁容侥倖，或致颠危？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243608_comment'></div>公之相蜀，动癯道肥，驰驱至死，昭烈之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243608_comment'></div>公若在魏，未必逢时，虽或见用，焉尽猷为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243608_comment'></div>不幸之中，有幸于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243608_comment'></div>天不祚汉，置公一维，匪公之恤，惟世之咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243608_comment'></div>公殁千载，蜀有馀思，岂惟蜀人，古今共推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243608_comment'></div>名参管萧，公论莫移，德声衮衮，江汉同驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243608_comment'></div>求仁得仁，抑又何悲？</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1243608_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　抵达成都任所，上谢宰相启。作品：成都运使到任谢宰相启。<div id='poem_1243461' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243461' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243461?labeling=true' target='_blank'>成都运使到任谢宰相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243461")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243461_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243461'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243461'>石渠寓直，遽参英俊之游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243461_comment'></div>玉垒将输，复贰光华之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243461_comment'></div>宠荣重沓，感恩交并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243461_comment'></div>伏念某禀赋凡庸，见闻单浅，随牒今逾于二纪，乘轺遍历于诸台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243461_comment'></div>顷按刑书，未周岁籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243461_comment'></div>虽粗殚于夙夜，曾何取于涓埃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243461_comment'></div>敢期责实之朝，乃冒踰涯之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243461_comment'></div>怀铅抱椠，通仙籍于蓬山；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243461_comment'></div>挽粟飞刍，耀星芒于井络。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243461_comment'></div>漕权既重，地望弥高，矧择副以尤难，常空员而弗置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243461_comment'></div>膺兹优擢，必属异能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243461_comment'></div>忽并误于褒迁，实自惊于叨窃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243461_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官道遵皇极，学探帝谟，蕴大任之英姿，辅中兴之盛烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243461_comment'></div>贤才广览，已收多士之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243461_comment'></div>利泽远施，深轸四方之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243461_comment'></div>精求肤使，猥及迂儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243461_comment'></div>察其体国之诚，未尝沽虚名而乏调度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243461_comment'></div>知其爱民之意，不肯越经赋而横征求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243461_comment'></div>似于公私取予之间，稍识利害轻重之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243461_comment'></div>是以委之剧部，秩以清资，用伸劝励之规，以起衰颓之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243461_comment'></div>某敢不咨询民瘼，宣布君仁，期不负于使令，庶少逃于罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243461_comment'></div>然而盘根错节，众谓难图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243461_comment'></div>绵力薄才，岂能宏济？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243461_comment'></div>非大造曲加于假借，则孤踪必至于颠隮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243461_comment'></div>播以陶钧，既荷生成之赐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243461_comment'></div>缓其衔勒，更希覆护之慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243461_comment'></div>载厚德以无穷，陨微躯而何有。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1243461_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年5月5日</a>　在成都，申奏渠州科敷之事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年7月15日</a>　在成都，作记。作品：云山台记。<div id='poem_1243585' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243585' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243585?labeling=true' target='_blank'>云山台记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十八年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年7月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243585")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243585_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243585'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243585'>潼川宪治之正寝，卑庳湫闇，岁久滋敝，更癸酉大水之后，气益阴湿，居之多疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243585_comment'></div>绍兴丁丑秋八月，余自本路转运判官移节而来，易其旧而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243585_comment'></div>凡百所须，一不以烦吾民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243585_comment'></div>时郪有以淫鬼诳俗者，方鸠木为鬼庙，乃没而入之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243585_comment'></div>后圃有澄清堂，颇闳壮而不适用，亦命彻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243585_comment'></div>于是寝材始具，八十日而告成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243585_comment'></div>澄清既隳，故基岿然，因聚其土而崇之为台，其高二寻，广二丈二尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243585_comment'></div>冠小亭其上，翼以栏楯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243585_comment'></div>经始季冬，成于明年之孟夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243585_comment'></div>余与客升焉，问客曰：「杜子美有《梓州台上》诗，台安在哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243585_comment'></div>客曰：「台亡久矣，抑公为此，可以补此邦之阙矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243585_comment'></div>遂摘杜诗警句之二言，以名之曰「云山台」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243585_comment'></div>客曰：「昔楚子游兰台之宫，有风飒然，披襟而快之，宋玉赋雄风以讽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243585_comment'></div>今子居高明，处台榭，遗暑湿于云霄之上，进风凉于山谷之间，诚亦快矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243585_comment'></div>独不念薅耘畎亩者有泥涂暴露之勤乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243585_comment'></div>偪侧闾阎者有温暍烦冤之苦乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243585_comment'></div>郡县之狱有淹系于缧绁者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243585_comment'></div>村落之氓有追胥于道路者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243585_comment'></div>使民不时，有役于官而不释者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243585_comment'></div>听讼不决，有留于庭而不去者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243585_comment'></div>吾圣天子悯农功，宽力役，下疏决之诏，虽身居九重，未尝一日忘民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243585_comment'></div>子为部使者，逍遥台上，轶溽暑而延清风，若不能上宣主泽，下求民瘼，则登临之际，得无愧于骚人之所赋耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243585_comment'></div>余再拜谢客，曰：「是吾心也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243585_comment'></div>然则斯台之作，虽取名于杜陵之诗，而实寓意于兰台之赋以自警也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243585_comment'></div>后之君子知我罪我，其在于斯乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243585_comment'></div>绍兴戊寅七月望日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1243585_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年8月12日</a>　在成都，有文。作品：潼川修城堤三桥记碑阴。<div id='poem_1243584' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243584' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243584?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潼川修城堤三桥记碑阴<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十八年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年8月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243584")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243584_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243584'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243584'>绍兴丙子秋九月，余以转运判官行部至梓，登牛头峰以望，江山秀绝，形胜雄伟，而雉堞颓圮，莽为丘墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243584_comment'></div>以问左右，皆曰自癸酉大水之后，陵夷至今，民力凋残，未之能复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243584_comment'></div>居人不宁，偷寓朝夕，常惴惴焉恐涨潦之复至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243584_comment'></div>时太守鄱阳张杞南卿，余故人也，方校类试之士于成都，不及见，则招其子大寿而语之：「为我白而翁，郛郭如此，其何以为邦，盍图之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243584_comment'></div>库有某钱，庾有某粟，以具版筑费」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243584_comment'></div>后得南卿书，欣然即事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243584_comment'></div>起工东北隅，属于南门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243584_comment'></div>经始季冬，至明年四月而罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243584_comment'></div>偶其家不幸，以病死者二人，冬十月南卿又卒于官，而宪车贾直清茂德亦以七月下世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243584_comment'></div>或追咎土功干犯禁忌所致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243584_comment'></div>会余蒙恩移节宪台，十有一月至治所，且摄府事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243584_comment'></div>有诏发廪以赈旱饥，羸瘠之民靡不沾上之泽，以免于沟壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243584_comment'></div>而梓俗尚气，其农家之少壮者，虽糟糠不继，犹耻就给于官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243584_comment'></div>于是上府倅李鄩会用度之出入，裁节冗滥，掇拾遗馀，以兴修城之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243584_comment'></div>高其庸募民，俾食其力，民欢趋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243584_comment'></div>自南门而西，至于北门，又缮捍水长堤，补隍岸之缺，起石桥于三门之外，其详见于今碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243584_comment'></div>将举事，或曰：「公其鉴张侯之祸，姑止若何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243584_comment'></div>余曰：「南卿之举，我实启之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243584_comment'></div>其死适与事会，我若畏祸而辍，是危人而自求全也，幽明之间，得无负乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243584_comment'></div>吉凶，命也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243584_comment'></div>卒为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243584_comment'></div>阅四月而后成，灾厉不作，邦人以安，余与僚属俱无恙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243584_comment'></div>梓之士大夫刻石以记其成，余以为是无足记者，而余发端卒事之本末，则不可以无述，因书之碑阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243584_comment'></div>初，宣和间之修是城也，见于廉访使者王总之奏，为工三十八万九千五百有奇，县私附益者不与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243584_comment'></div>梓去边徼远，承平无事，而创为楼橹一百七十馀区，一路告病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243584_comment'></div>既成，自转运副使、提点刑狱下至督役执事之人，增秩有差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243584_comment'></div>十邑各有分地，岁岁葺之，至靖康乃止，公私之费不可计，父老具能道之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243584_comment'></div>余今并书于此，非伐一时事以暴前人之失，盖欲后之君子知张皇欺罔，害民以徼进，获福无几，遗愧无穷，不可以不戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243584_comment'></div>戊寅八月十二日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1243584_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　在成都，有启贺王刚中除四川制置使。作品：贺成都王制置启。贺成都王制置开藩启。<div id='poem_1243465' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243465' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243465?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺成都王制置启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243465")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243465_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243465'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243465'>光膺明綍，出拥高牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243465_comment'></div>井络折冲，耸全蜀上游之寄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243465_comment'></div>河图寓直，冠西清次对之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243465_comment'></div>除目一传，舆情大慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243465_comment'></div>恭惟某官才猷英特，学术纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243465_comment'></div>昔居韦布之间，早负经纶之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243465_comment'></div>轩墀射策，追晁董以争衡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243465_comment'></div>禁省代言，掩常杨而专美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243465_comment'></div>眷坤维之谋帅，申巽命以任贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243465_comment'></div>独当真主之知，粤副元戎之选，辍论思于近侍，宽忧顾于远民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243465_comment'></div>一劄细书，丁宁德意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243465_comment'></div>万钉宝带，焜耀身章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243465_comment'></div>载颁内帑之资，庸视中朝之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243465_comment'></div>惟疏恩之特异，知注意之逾深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243465_comment'></div>红旆碧油，权暂专于玉垒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243465_comment'></div>紫枢黄阁，名即启于金瓯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243465_comment'></div>某衰晚无堪，驰驱何补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243465_comment'></div>当年倾盖，已轻万户之封；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243465_comment'></div>指日承颜，方借九河之润。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1243465_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1243466' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243466' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243466?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺成都王制置开藩启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243466")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243466_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243466'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243466'>重阃需贤，坤维就镇，拥麾幢而入境，开幕府以建牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243466_comment'></div>凡托部封，莫不欢慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243466_comment'></div>恭惟某官资兼文武，学通古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243466_comment'></div>自得隽于贤科，即受知于明主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243466_comment'></div>登崇甚峻，天下想闻其风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243466_comment'></div>眷注弥深，汉廷无出其右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243466_comment'></div>兹从近侍，来抚上游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243466_comment'></div>谋帅得人，顿觉雪山之重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243466_comment'></div>忘身徇国，岂辞蜀道之难！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243466_comment'></div>草木莫不知名，烟云为之改色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243466_comment'></div>列城企踵，冀六纛之遄征；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243466_comment'></div>多士私忧，恐一封之趣召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243466_comment'></div>某司存有守，迎候未遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243466_comment'></div>贺厦输诚，已记曹之是浼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243466_comment'></div>披云自幸，倾行旆以尤勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243466_comment'></div>淑气渐融，征途尚远，愿益加于保谨，用上副于倚毗。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1243466_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　在成都任转运副使期间，曾与王刚中争礼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年1月</a>　在成都，表贺皇太后八十岁寿辰。作品：皇太后圣算八十贺皇帝表。皇太后升遐慰皇表。<div id='poem_1243277' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243277' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243277?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇太后圣算八十贺皇帝表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243277")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243277_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243277'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243277'>三朝受籍，属临文德之朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243277_comment'></div>万岁称觞，式展慈宁之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243277_comment'></div>化流寰宇，欢动宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243277_comment'></div>恭维皇帝陛下性体尧仁，躬行舜道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243277_comment'></div>于斯为盛，承太姒之徽音；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243277_comment'></div>受祉既多，小鲁侯之燕喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243277_comment'></div>礼成中禁，福集新元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243277_comment'></div>孝感神明，格母仪于上寿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243277_comment'></div>泽施耆艾，慰人子之至情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243277_comment'></div>臣承乏外台，与闻盛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243277_comment'></div>千官入贺，想环佩之丁当；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243277_comment'></div>四海沾恩，快雷风之鼓舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243277_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1243277_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1243278' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243278' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243278?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇太后升遐慰皇帝表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243278'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243278'>夙钟庆祚，诞育清躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243278_comment'></div>艰深百罹，从先皇而北狩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243278_comment'></div>始终七闰，享孝养于东朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243278_comment'></div>方延上寿之期，光抚中兴之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243278_comment'></div>何期窀穸，永隔晨昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243278_comment'></div>恭维皇帝陛下孝慕至深，悲摧罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243278_comment'></div>愿追承于理命，用少抑于圣情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243278_comment'></div>臣使事有拘，不遑奔赴阙廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243278_comment'></div>臣无任衔哀抱痛，擗踊感伤之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243278_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1243278_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href='/Writing/1243509?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺周内翰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年闰6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1243509'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243509'>光奉宸纶，擢专翰苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243509_comment'></div>正是久虚之席，孰如已试之才？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243509_comment'></div>四方耸闻，多士歆宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243509_comment'></div>恭惟某官天资秀颖，道学渊源，早收宏博之科，遍阅清华之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243509_comment'></div>掖垣琐闼，高论思润色之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243509_comment'></div>金马玉堂，极经术文章之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243509_comment'></div>果佥谐于因任，遂亟被于真除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243509_comment'></div>白麻推三代之英，青简擅一家之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243509_comment'></div>飞腾壮岁，冠压近班，风云之契已孚，梦卜之求允属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243509_comment'></div>名书案上，闻御墨之新题；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243509_comment'></div>礼绝坐中，有禁林之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243509_comment'></div>某猥将使指，阻造宾闳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243509_comment'></div>内制得贤，觉朝家之增重，词宗当路，喜吾道之方亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243509_comment'></div>岁律将穷，台符正远，愿谨保绥之节，用承倚注之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1243509_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年7月</a>　在成都，有启贺朱倬除参知政事。作品：贺朱参政启。<div id='poem_1243479' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243479' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243479?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺朱参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243479")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243479_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243479'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243479'>光奉宸恩，进陪国论，真儒得位，寰宇均欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243479_comment'></div>恭惟某官迪德诚明，凝姿敦大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243479_comment'></div>深探道奥，会先圣不传之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243479_comment'></div>洞达时宜，殖当今有用之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243479_comment'></div>夙奋经纶之蕴，荐升华显之途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243479_comment'></div>宪府绳违，正一台之纲纪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243479_comment'></div>露门劝讲，阐六艺之渊源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243479_comment'></div>精忠弥结于主知，公辅久虚于物望，果承天眷，入秉政机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243479_comment'></div>必将下膏泽以醇四海之风，恢远图而永万世之业，跻民仁寿，正位钧衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243479_comment'></div>舆诵所归，斯言可复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243479_comment'></div>某谬蒙荐宠，欣听登庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243479_comment'></div>虽邈在坤维，莫遂踵门之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243479_comment'></div>然仰承晋接，尤深贺厦之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243479_comment'></div>霜令载严，冲襟多裕，愿谨谷神之卫，以符岩石之瞻。</div><div href='/Writing/1243279?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢授太府少卿四川总领到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1243279'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243279'>贰列卿于外府，猥厕廷绅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243279_comment'></div>主经赋于上游，仍将使指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243279_comment'></div>省躬曷称，拜命知荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243279_comment'></div>伏念臣少本拘儒，老为俗吏，偶明时之弗弃，乃烦使之屡更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243279_comment'></div>去朝初自于乞麾，入蜀继叨于移节，驱驰九载，绵历五司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243279_comment'></div>虽殚夙夜之勤，蔑有涓埃之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243279_comment'></div>荐蒙增秩，比复赐环。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243279_comment'></div>雷电取将，已下仙官之敕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243279_comment'></div>蓬瀛且至，却回方士之船。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243279_comment'></div>涣号申颁，训词溢美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243279_comment'></div>亚班联于七寺之长，督馈饷于六师之屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243279_comment'></div>引私讳以有陈，触报闻而莫避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243279_comment'></div>凌竞就列，颠仆是虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243279_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下道配施生，功函动植，公听达四聪之壅，兼收屈群策之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243279_comment'></div>询事考言，判人才之真伪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243279_comment'></div>循名责实，极王政于清明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243279_comment'></div>致若孤踪，亦尘剧任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243279_comment'></div>臣敢不交修食货，兼裕军民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243279_comment'></div>江汉朝宗，徒抱爱君之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243279_comment'></div>井参扪历，益坚许国之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1243279_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年12月</a>　抵达成都任所，上谢宰相启。作品：太府少卿四川总领到任谢宰相启。<div
