class='authorDate'>（1160年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243476")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243476_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243476'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243476'>贰列卿于外府，猥厕廷绅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243476_comment'></div>董经赋于上游，仍将使指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243476_comment'></div>省躬曷称，拜命知荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243476_comment'></div>伏念某少本拘儒，老为俗吏，偶明时之幸会，乃烦使之屡更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243476_comment'></div>去朝初自于乞麾，入蜀继叨于移节，驱驰九载，绵历五司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243476_comment'></div>虽殚夙夜之劳，蔑有涓埃之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243476_comment'></div>荐蒙增秩，比复赐环。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243476_comment'></div>雷电取将，已下仙官之敕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243476_comment'></div>蓬瀛且至，却回方士之船。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243476_comment'></div>涣号申颁，训词溢美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243476_comment'></div>亚班联于七寺之长，督饷馈于六师之屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243476_comment'></div>引私讳以有陈，触报闻而莫避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243476_comment'></div>凌兢就列，颠仆是虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243476_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官先觉真材，具瞻硕辅，以尊主庇民之术，行推贤进善之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243476_comment'></div>名一艺者必庸，用广揽英豪之士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243476_comment'></div>无大故则不弃，尤曲敦贫贱之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243476_comment'></div>至若衰迟，特勤记录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243476_comment'></div>推挽之恩极矣，不进弗休；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243476_comment'></div>抚存之意温然，有加未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243476_comment'></div>重惭凉德，倍费生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243476_comment'></div>某敢不仰体眷私，更鞭驽蹇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243476_comment'></div>交修食货，权四路之盈虚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243476_comment'></div>兼裕军民，俾一方之帖泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243476_comment'></div>庶上宽于忧顾，次少答于陶镕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1243476_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年12月22日</a>　在成都，始视事，视帑庾见在之数。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　在成都，谒崇德庙文。<div id='poem_1243619' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243619' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243619?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谒崇德庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243619")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243619_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243619'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243619'>惟神功利著于古今，英灵震于遐迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243619_comment'></div>父子兄弟，爵号崇极，一门庙食，百世并隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243619_comment'></div>四川之人，罔不奔走祀事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243619_comment'></div>某持节两蜀，于今六载，免抵罪戾，实托神庥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243619_comment'></div>敢不拜谒祠下，恭陈薄荐，用致微诚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1243619_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年3月</a>　在成都，有启贺杨椿除参知政事。作品：贺杨参政启。<div id='poem_1243481' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243481' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243481?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺杨参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243481")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243481_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243481'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243481'>显膺诏綍，荣预政机，海宇同休，簪绅共庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243481_comment'></div>恭惟某官学造圣贤之域，气钟天地之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243481_comment'></div>腾茂蜚英，展也万人之杰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243481_comment'></div>廉贪立懦，卓哉一世之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243481_comment'></div>盖尝推难进之风，将以厚有为之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243481_comment'></div>比及厉精之日，果勤侧席之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243481_comment'></div>爰增重于蓬山，即升华于荷橐，批敕独高于夕拜，司戎旋擢于夏卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243481_comment'></div>秘殿横经，既极名儒之选；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243481_comment'></div>禁林视草，尤符内相之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243481_comment'></div>上方加考慎之图，人皆谓登庸之晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243481_comment'></div>兹进陪于揆路，实简在于渊衷，以旦夕承弼之良，为左右股肱之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243481_comment'></div>子仪彻乐，已闻清德之孚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243481_comment'></div>淮南寝谋，坐有折冲之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243481_comment'></div>伫见白麻之出，益昭黄阁之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243481_comment'></div>某逖在遐方，钦闻休命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243481_comment'></div>台符两两，徒仰睇于馀光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243481_comment'></div>公府潭潭，愿永依于大厦。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1243481_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年4月2日</a>　在成都，闻有边隙，自益昌运粮十万石至武兴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年4月17日</a>　在成都，乞将诸军年额无亏欠和亏欠最者姓名申尚书省。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年4月17日</a>　在成都，上催驱殿最事目，诏诸路依此行事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年5月</a>　在成都，贺吴璘拜四川宣抚使。作品：贺吴宣抚启。<div id='poem_1243482' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243482' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243482?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺吴宣抚启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243482")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243482_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243482'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243482'>九重注意，载颁涣汗之新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243482_comment'></div>四蜀分忧，就付宣威之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243482_comment'></div>华区震叠，庙社奠安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243482_comment'></div>恭惟某官智勇兼资，勋名夙著，三纪壮西南之翰，一门摅忠义之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243482_comment'></div>盖神明默扶子仪，俾再造于王室；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243482_comment'></div>而匈奴素畏李牧，不敢犯于边陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243482_comment'></div>膺具礼于斋坛，视多仪于揆路，分统连营之盛，旋升亚保之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243482_comment'></div>顾凌烟之像，未极于形容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243482_comment'></div>而太常之铭，屡勤于记述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243482_comment'></div>兵欲藉上游掎角之势，公独得中原归附之心，故宏建于高牙，用尽护于诸将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243482_comment'></div>昔岑彭冯异，阐方面之号；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243482_comment'></div>而卫青去病，开幕府之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243482_comment'></div>兹闻兄弟之迭居，足为古今之盛美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243482_comment'></div>况司徒之子公武，尝进璧于淮堧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243482_comment'></div>太傅之侄谢玄，亦陈师于淝水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243482_comment'></div>岂特功业一时之会，实系国家万世之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243482_comment'></div>某久托馀辉，欣聆成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243482_comment'></div>简书有守，莫穷贺厦之私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243482_comment'></div>调度斯兴，当叶同舟之力。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1243482_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年5月29日</a>　在成都，言减兵选兵之计。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　在成都，上札论运米充边备。作品：论运米充边备朝札。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年6月13日</a>　在成都，奏请朝廷宜分司庀职，各得守其职分。作品：措置备边饷馈朝札。<div id='poem_1243383' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243383' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243383?labeling=true' target='_blank'>措置备边饷馈朝劄<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三十一年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年6月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243383")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243383_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243383'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243383'>某今月二十九日伏准宰执通佥劄子，备到北使奏陈语录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243383_comment'></div>五月二十二日三省枢密院同奉圣旨，令诸路都统制并沿边帅守监司照应事体，随宜应变，疾速措置，务要不失机会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243383_comment'></div>某已恭依施行外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243383_comment'></div>今有本职合行申禀事件，画一如后：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1243383'>一、川蜀前来用兵，都转运司领其财赋，而隶于宣抚司，如赵开辈皆宣抚置其所厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243383_comment'></div>宣抚司有便宜，都漕司依倚而行，以为一切之政，故粗能应办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243383_comment'></div>是时兵统于诸帅，财领于都运，而宣抚使兼总之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243383_comment'></div>后来朝廷改置总领，实分版曹之务，仓库皆以户部为名，而以朝臣奉使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243383_comment'></div>赵不弃初除四川总领日，申画一项云：「昨来张成宪应副韩世忠钱粮，申明与宣抚别无统摄，止用公牒行移，乞移张成宪已得指挥」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243383_comment'></div>朝廷降旨从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243383_comment'></div>自是兵与财赋各有攸司，势若提衡，轻重相济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243383_comment'></div>东南二总领责任差轻，又朝廷在近，凡事有所倚重，匮乏可容丐乞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243383_comment'></div>蜀在数千里外，奏报往复，动经数月，与东南事体不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243383_comment'></div>近朝廷以吴少保为宣抚，而应干事务，令王制置同共措置，且量事紧慢，移司近吴，以便计议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243383_comment'></div>四川军事有所统一，甚合事宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243383_comment'></div>是则宣抚制其兵，制置共其谋，而总领主其饷馈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243383_comment'></div>兵未必日交，谋未必日用，而饷馈则一日不可有阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243383_comment'></div>在今日总领所忧责最重，了办为尤难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243383_comment'></div>四川自改总领所以来，未经用兵，一旦有事，与当时不同，恐或诸司各有申明，不相参照，朝廷行下，临时难以酬应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243383_comment'></div>人最所吝惜者财也，最所贪爱者亦财也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243383_comment'></div>总领一司于郡县则急其入，于将士则裁其出，职事所行，大抵皆拂逆人情，为众怨之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243383_comment'></div>若非朝廷主张假借，使有以自立，则缓急之际，殆难以财赋作主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243383_comment'></div>事关军国，利害非轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243383_comment'></div>今吴少保忠义体国，兼爱军民，王阁学明达忧时，务循法度，皆与某心腹相照，可容协济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243383_comment'></div>顾朝廷分司庀职，非为一时，当计久远，处画分明，则易相调护，各得守其职分矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243383_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1243383'>一、绍兴八年七月十二日指挥，川陕宣抚司合用钱粮万数浩瀚，都转运司自合体度，科拨应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243383_comment'></div>缘见今置司去军前颇远，难以应办，理合措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243383_comment'></div>奉圣旨，都转运司可于利州置<span class='inlineComment2'>（先时置司成都。）</span>，令总领所、户部仓库、粮料院并在利州，职当科拨应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243383_comment'></div>若大军一动，其般发转输须合有随军转运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243383_comment'></div>前此或有诸路漕臣兼充，或以宣抚司参议官为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243383_comment'></div>今三都统边面皆属利路，利路漕臣缓急全赖协济，责任最紧，须置两员，更迭出入，庶不乏使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243383_comment'></div>仍宜得彊干有风力者为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243383_comment'></div>其馀三路，惟夔路见今两漕，成都、潼川各止一员，更朝廷详酌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243383_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1243383'>一、朝廷遣王官出使，尽总四川财赋，以军马钱粮为职事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243383_comment'></div>或有出入，自当竭力应副，不容阙乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243383_comment'></div>若与将帅故为异同，不啻缓急使其无以赴功，致误国事，何说以辞诛罚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243383_comment'></div>然主兵者亦当恤其有无，凡所须索，酌度紧慢，据实关报，事通商量，则易于应办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243383_comment'></div>若乘仓卒之际，或相促迫，临时必致狼狈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243383_comment'></div>朝廷宜加训谕，使同心协议，体国从长，事如一家，无有彼我，则功无不济矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243383_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1243383'>一、用兵对敌，有攻有守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243383_comment'></div>蜀中自守之策，盖已屡试，应干费用，粗有准则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243383_comment'></div>若欲出师捣虚，以为牵制，则与守御事体不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243383_comment'></div>其粮运远近，士卒多少，经由去处，计司须预闻梗槩，以为支备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243383_comment'></div>乞行下宣抚、制置司照会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243383_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1243383'>一、据北使所奏，今年九月末北主巡猎陈、蔡、唐、邓之郊，明年二三月方来京兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1243383_comment'></div>若秋冬以后，王师迎击于东，蜀兵牵制于西，遂能奏功于淮汉之间，固大善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1243383_comment'></div>万一冲突关陕，则蜀中来年所备愈重，日月尚远，何以枝梧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1243383_comment'></div>自某到官，多方经画，催驱州县，务要办而不扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1243383_comment'></div>上半年比较诸色所入，已多于往年最高之数二百馀万引，其势极矣，不可复加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1243383_comment'></div>所入虽增，费出亦夥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1243383_comment'></div>只发吴四厢兵老小三千人，并运州寄桩米二十万石水脚钱，及一两处移屯等，已合添用一百一十八万引有奇，其他杂费尚多，难以悉举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1243383_comment'></div>诸军关请器械、帐幕、旗帜之类，方来而未已，皆常岁所无有，将来调发之数皆不在此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1243383_comment'></div>今于经赋之外，既一毫不敢有取，而东南用度至广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1243383_comment'></div>臣子之义，所当体国，非甚不得已，岂忍烦溷朝廷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1243383_comment'></div>以此日夜忧恐，未知攸济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1243383_comment'></div>伏惟钧慈，俯赐矜察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1243383_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年7月22日</a>　在成都，奏请四川财赋当专任总领所，诏从之。作品：论四川总所与东南事体不同札。<div id='poem_1243377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论四川总所与东南事体不同劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年7月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243377")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243377_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243377'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243377'>某契勘东南用兵，将帅统军旅，户部总财赋，而朝廷制其予夺盈虚之柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243377_comment'></div>今四川去朝廷远，而总司不预兵事，凡有调发支费，只得据其所须，色色应副，不过委曲调护而已，比东南事体大段不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243377_comment'></div>所幸宣抚吴璘忠义体国，爱惜财用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243377_comment'></div>不然，总领一司，何以支吾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243377_comment'></div>近蒙累降处分，令诸军与本所务在协和，不生间隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243377_comment'></div>诸将莫不遵禀，本所以自立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243377_comment'></div>斯盖圣朝明见万里之外，远方闻指挥之下，皆大悦服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243377_comment'></div>凡本所应办之难，不敢重言，只乞朝廷以东南调度略行比较，便可以照见也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1243377_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年9月21日</a>　在成都，言军兴移运，当置随军漕臣。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年9月</a>　在成都，有启贺黄祖舜同知枢秘院事。作品：贺黄枢密启。<div id='poem_1243489' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243489' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243489?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺黄枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243489")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243489_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243489'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243489'>显膺纶告，进贰枢廷，增皇朝道德之威，壮天下安荣之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243489_comment'></div>缙绅属目，介胄归心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243489_comment'></div>恭惟某官才乂王家，学探圣域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243489_comment'></div>文章醇正，参垂世之格言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243489_comment'></div>识虑昭融，富经邦之奇蕴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243489_comment'></div>亟蒙睿眷，荐历华涂，资管轺于都曹，职论思于宪部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243489_comment'></div>露门劝讲，开陈默契于渊衷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243489_comment'></div>琐闼绳愆，封驳允符于公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243489_comment'></div>上方奋乾健以清六合，廓离明以烛九幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243489_comment'></div>必使运帷幄之筹，如数计而龟卜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243489_comment'></div>用能夺腥膻之气，使瓦解而冰消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243489_comment'></div>倘非真贤，孰跻兴运？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243489_comment'></div>赞宥密之命，精神已见于折冲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243489_comment'></div>司造化之权，辅相行观于藏用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243489_comment'></div>某肃将隆指，欣颂除音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243489_comment'></div>邈在遐陬，阻遂登龙之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243489_comment'></div>仰倾潭府，徒深贺燕之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243489_comment'></div>春令正妍，灵襟多裕，愿谨鼎茵之节，式符岩石之瞻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1243489_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　在成都，有措置钱监军兵充诸军使唤朝札。<div id='poem_1243376' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243376' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243376?labeling=true' target='_blank'>措置钱监军兵充诸军使唤朝劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243376")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243376_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243376'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243376'>某契勘利州绍兴铸钱监兵士计二百七十馀人，多四方凶恶不逞之徒，苦于上工役，居常思乱，而重兵所驻，不敢为恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243376_comment'></div>今大军尽已调发，无所畏惮，人甚患之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243376_comment'></div>某随宜措置，诸军起发之日，令统制官任靖入监，拣选强壮之士，得一百五十七人，分作三队，给行钱粮，请衮同发赴军前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243376_comment'></div>又拣选次彊者四十三人，及拘收到平南山金牛等巡采打铁炭兵士二百馀人，以充往来般运钱帛，颇赖其用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243376_comment'></div>馀在监老弱七十人，令任鼓铸，人情始安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243376_comment'></div>发遣后数日，得吴宣抚书云：「利州钱监兵窃恐作过，为诸军老小在彼，璘不敢放心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243376_comment'></div>乞权发来军前，不知可否，幸望留念<span class='inlineComment2'>（监兵初五日发去，初十日得此书。）</span>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243376_comment'></div>闻既到彼，皆优加犒劳，募敢死者间入贼境，招纳归附，馀人亦皆可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243376_comment'></div>其钱监铸钱候将来事定，却别行措置。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1243376_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年10月4日</a>　在成都，上札奏乞吴拱襄阳兵钱粮免行科发，户部勘当不从。作品：乞令湖广应副吴拱襄阳官兵钱粮朝札。<div id='poem_1243378' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243378' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243378?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞令湖广应副吴拱襄阳官兵钱粮朝劄<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三十二年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年10月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243378")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243378_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243378'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243378'>某照会昨准尚书省劄子，坐湖广总领所申，将吴拱带行官兵粮草料依循、赣、夔州体例，责令旧应副官发赴襄阳府交纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243378_comment'></div>某已于去年十月初四日、十一月初八日两具事理申明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243378_comment'></div>承朝廷送下户部勘当，未蒙本部照应，所申事理止检送湖广总领所，元申再下本所，令依已降指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243378_comment'></div>某以不才，误膺委使，平时粗知体国，矧艰难之际，苟有利于公家，岂问远近彼此之殊，自当竭力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243378_comment'></div>若于事非便利，力所不及，亦不敢畏避含糊，以误大计，不免冒昧谴斥，再有披陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243378_comment'></div>窃惟四川之地褊隘险绝，财赋所出不比江浙，而于馈饷为尤难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243378_comment'></div>古今称善用蜀者，无如诸葛亮，亮得南中六郡，军资饶富，又一丝一粟不入中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243378_comment'></div>以今准之，事力不侔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243378_comment'></div>亮兵前后四出，其众不满五万，或由祁山，或由散关，或由斜谷，近止数百里，远不踰三数月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243378_comment'></div>木牛流马穷转输之巧，犹每苦粮食之不继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243378_comment'></div>今蜀中大军十馀万，与敌相持于散关一百三十馀日，则兵比亮众为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243378_comment'></div>右取秦、陇、洮、兰，左取陕、华、商、虢，皆仰供亿，则地比亮境为广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243378_comment'></div>又夔州万人防托，亦系本所应副，视亮用蜀之费，不啻数倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243378_comment'></div>若更令越三千里般粮运草，馈襄阳之戍，区区巴蜀，何以胜任？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243378_comment'></div>古所谓千里馈粮者，亦不过旬月计耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243378_comment'></div>若钱粮草料三千里外按月责办，岂能免于阙误？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243378_comment'></div>契勘蜀中屯军，分隶一十八处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243378_comment'></div>其潼川、兴元府、绵、剑、文、渠、金、洋、阶、成、西和、凤州合用粮料，本所每年科支本钱，就逐州夏秋籴买应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243378_comment'></div>其利、阆两州边嘉陵江，系招诱客贩收籴支遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243378_comment'></div>惟鱼关、兴州、大安军三处合用粮料，本所于利、阆州籴买数内运三十四万前去，水路只五六百里，约用船脚钱引七十万道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243378_comment'></div>所有马草，只于屯驻州军收到税草内应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243378_comment'></div>而四川当无事之时，已不堪其劳费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243378_comment'></div>今吴四厢官兵，一岁当用钱粮、草料、春冬衣赐物帛，纽算钱引计一百二万四千五百馀道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243378_comment'></div>上件军兵朝廷已令限一季招填，本所自无此一项阙额衣粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243378_comment'></div>若更移运本所前去襄阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243378_comment'></div>当用水陆脚钱四百三十馀万道，比之应副兴州、鱼关、大安军所费多六七倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243378_comment'></div>虽竭四川公私之力，亦恐难以应办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243378_comment'></div>欲望钧慈特赐指挥，检会前状并今来所申，逐项子细看议利害，免行科拨，下湖广总领所照应施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243378_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1243378'>〔小贴子〕照会襄阳府吴拱官兵合用钱粮，已准朝廷指挥，令湖广总领所取拨京西常平司钱三万馀贯，斛斗二万九千九百馀石，并现管诸色钱斛别色科名应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243378_comment'></div>如更不足，于军前应桩管钱米，及附近州军不以有无拘碍，应干钱斛，移运支遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243378_comment'></div>贴降淮西总领所桩管银五万两，鄂州坐仓和籴到米内取拨二万一百石，共五万石，专充吴拱官兵支使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243378_comment'></div>即是朝廷应副不为不至，自可足办，难以更竭四川事力，三千里外移运粮草前去照会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243378_comment'></div>金州素来凋弊，近都统王彦收复陕、华、商、虢，分屯人马在四川间，捍御强敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243378_comment'></div>金人不住复来侵扰，见今事势未保万全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243378_comment'></div>一邦事力已极困弊，岂可更任襄阳转输之责？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243378_comment'></div>实恐有误国事，伏乞钧照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1243378_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年10月4日</a>　在成都，有启贺吴璘升诏讨使。作品：贺吴宣抚升诏讨使。<div id='poem_1243490' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243490' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243490?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺吴宣抚升招讨启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年10月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243490")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243490_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243490'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243490'>命敷纶綍，益隆委寄之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243490_comment'></div>地控关河，尽付威怀之柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243490_comment'></div>传闻中外，震耸华戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243490_comment'></div>恭惟某官几鉴绝人，勋名盖世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243490_comment'></div>勇无与敌，曾收百战之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243490_comment'></div>智有馀忠，深被九重之眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243490_comment'></div>懋斋坛之宠数，总环列之师屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243490_comment'></div>爵命增崇，峻处三孤之秩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243490_comment'></div>皇灵宣布，独分四蜀之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243490_comment'></div>眷秦晋之奥区，稔祖宗之遗泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243490_comment'></div>江山牢落，久沦戎马之区；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243490_comment'></div>父老咨嗟，常晞日月之照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243490_comment'></div>上方振规恢之长策，公能奋经济之远图，特畀重权，庸清大敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243490_comment'></div>有指疆土，岂惟伐猃狁而至太原；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243490_comment'></div>克诘戎兵，必将封狼居而临瀚海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243490_comment'></div>某久蒙辉润，欣诵诏除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243490_comment'></div>属限官常，阻遂辕门之谒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243490_comment'></div>仰伸庆问，敢稽尺牍之驰！</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1243490_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年10月10日</a>　在成都，奏乞依旧复置陕西路转运司管辖新复州军，措置合行事宜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年10月17日</a>　在成都，言应四川诸军钱粮事务取拨事宜。尚书省准奏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年10月29日</a>　在成都，言本所库管钱引之事。十二月庚子施行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　在成都，叶义问力荐王之望，高宗有擢用之意。王之望上书谢叶义问，又与之论制敌方略。作品：上叶枢密书。与叶枢密论制敌方略书。<div id='poem_1243423' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243423' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243423?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上叶枢密书<span class='inlineComment2'>（谢荐就言事）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243423")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243423_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243423'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243423'>某谨斋沐裁书，效其庆贺感激、区区倾倒之诚，东望再拜，走一介献于枢密相公阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243423_comment'></div>伏审光被畴咨，擢冠宥密，圣朝注意，身佩安危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243423_comment'></div>方天下有事之时，隐然如一敌国，四方万里倚以为重，交口相贺，喜邦家之得贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243423_comment'></div>自非任重致远之资久孚于人望，解纷排难之略深契于事机，则帝眷民心，何以及此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243423_comment'></div>天下幸甚，天下幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243423_comment'></div>某比得行朝相知书，报枢密知院相公初秋对扬，力加论荐，遂忝赐环之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243423_comment'></div>始惊且疑，以为阁下以命世人杰，骤结明主，一二岁间躐居大位，方攘袂以图回天下，而天下之贤能系心属目，愿自托于下风者，不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243423_comment'></div>登庸之始，荐贤报国为莫大之举，宜得异人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243423_comment'></div>而某流落远外，行能无以逾众，且疏远之迹未尝一登龙门，岂所传之妄乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243423_comment'></div>报者狎至，方敢以为信，则激昂奋励之气勃勃乎发于胸中，而不知其齿之既衰，力之不逮，抵掌扼腕，恨未有以为知己死者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243423_comment'></div>回顾其身，不啻如鸿毛之轻也，不知阁下何所闻而取之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243423_comment'></div>夫公卿荐人，必求悉其雅素：大抵其乡曲也，其亲戚也，意气之相投也，父祖之有好也，科第之同时也，宦学之同处也，微贱之日蒙其慰荐之恩者也，穷厄之际得其周旋之力者也，否则，以姻旧之婉转也，权贵之请嘱也，于此数者而择人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243423_comment'></div>不在是者，虽至宝横路，谁复取焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243423_comment'></div>昔崔祐甫当国，除吏八百，多其亲故，曰「非故何以知之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243423_comment'></div>及李吉甫为相，咨裴垍曰「十五年远裔，不知比日人物」，垍为疏三十馀人，吉甫荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243423_comment'></div>尝谓崔祐甫当常衮之后，贤愚同滞之时，故人不以为非，要非天下之公道也，不如李吉甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243423_comment'></div>若吉甫所荐，必求亲故，则何以致元和得人之盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243423_comment'></div>伊尹之俊彦，必曰「旁求」，傅说之俊乂，必曰「旁招」，二子起于耕筑之处，安得亲故而用之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243423_comment'></div>祐甫之言陋于是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243423_comment'></div>夫亲故有私恩，舍之则必致其怨，贤能非旧识，荐之则或蒙其累，人将何择焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243423_comment'></div>自非胸襟器局有大过人，如伊尹、傅说，自任以天下之重者，孰肯旁搜广览，为非常之举哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243423_comment'></div>某不佞，何敢窃议盛德，尝试以其所闻而揆之行事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243423_comment'></div>必也广大英特，慨然有志乎天下，故朝夕汲汲留意人伦，思得一世奇士，致之乎吾君，以共济艰难之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243423_comment'></div>入居政府，席未及煖，其尊主庇民之术有未及陈，而首以荐贤为急务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243423_comment'></div>惟其急于荐贤也，故如某之不肖，亦不暇有所择焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243423_comment'></div>假之岁月，则天下英伟豪杰之士，有不出于阁下之门者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243423_comment'></div>顾某非其人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243423_comment'></div>语曰：「道不同，不相为谋」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243423_comment'></div>故小德役大德，小贤役大贤，同声相应，同气相求之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243423_comment'></div>阁下以端方鲠谅之操，岌乎其难进，陆沈于下僚，逾六十而始遇，故每求士之羁穷郁滞困厄而不振者达之，冀万有一分得或类己者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243423_comment'></div>某既愚且拙，介介自守，无以觊当世之偶，尝得幸于今庙堂诸公，颇蒙谅其平生，怜其穷以老而保持之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243423_comment'></div>向者台谏诸贤，亦复过听，以其姓名应诏，故犹得玷使者之节，驱驰远部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243423_comment'></div>不然，则放迹林泉，躬耕畎亩，一枯槁之田夫耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243423_comment'></div>抑阁下其亦以此而取之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243423_comment'></div>夫君子之难进也，将以有为也，如阁下是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243423_comment'></div>如某辈亦自量其中无所可用，故甘退缩无用之地耳，阁下其何取焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243423_comment'></div>虽然，阁下不俟识面，举于稠人之中，重之以国士之知，某何敢以无所可用不少效其愚乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243423_comment'></div>伏惟阁下以命世人杰，骤结明主，躐居大位，圣朝注意，身佩安危，可谓盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243423_comment'></div>不识阁下以位为乐乎，将以时为忧也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243423_comment'></div>如阁下平昔之所自负，必不以位为乐，其亦皇皇乎忧时而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243423_comment'></div>时所当忧者，得非外敌之凭陵乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243423_comment'></div>以某观之，外敌之凭陵非徒不足忧，乃宗庙之灵、社稷之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243423_comment'></div>自古用兵固有彊弱，而胜负不系焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243423_comment'></div>以南视北，诚若不敌，然北败于南多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1243423_comment'></div>今为我敌者能彊于石虎乎，能贤于苻坚乎，能盛于魏太武乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1243423_comment'></div>三人皆尝图南矣，大则以亡，小则以乱，而区区晋宋曾不为之折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1243423_comment'></div>国家地土绝长补短，犹方万里，带甲数十万，比之晋宋蔑有不及焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1243423_comment'></div>矧主上圣德日新，仁孝天至，海内爱戴，无可乘之衅，固皇天之所眷祐，亦何畏于彼哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1243423_comment'></div>议者狃于靖康、建炎之祸，以为终不可敌，则亦不察矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1243423_comment'></div>彼君非昔日之君，将非昔日之将，谋臣非昔日之谋臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1243423_comment'></div>昔其来也，乘吾久安而无备，一人杖箠，千百遁逃，入吾封疆不涉险阻，所舍者大厦，所享者膏粱，金帛子女之得不可以数计，而吾讫无一人敢与之抗，反为其役焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1243423_comment'></div>此吾之所以不支而彼之所以独克也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1243423_comment'></div>今则不然，淮汉之郊荒凉万里，大川为之限，无粮食之可因，金帛子女可欲之物皆无有也，其亦何以使贪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1243423_comment'></div>而吾人知其可敌，亦不至望风而遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1243423_comment'></div>诚使一日决战，胜负未可知，彼独能无惧哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1243423_comment'></div>内无所贪而外无所惧，则与向来之势固不侔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1243423_comment'></div>或曰：「彼地广民众，兵彊而国富，数倍于我可也，若之何易之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1243423_comment'></div>应之曰：善观天下者，不观其形而观其理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1243423_comment'></div>地广民众，兵彊而国富，用之以其道，不可当也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1243423_comment'></div>若以无道行之，则亦不足畏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1243423_comment'></div>兵法曰：「主孰有道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1243423_comment'></div>将孰有能？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1243423_comment'></div>天地孰得？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1243423_comment'></div>法令孰行？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1243423_comment'></div>兵众孰彊？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1243423_comment'></div>士卒孰练？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1243423_comment'></div>赏罚孰明？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1243423_comment'></div>吾以此知胜负矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1243423_comment'></div>论兵众邪，彼诚彊矣，而客主有劳逸，攻守有难易，亦足以相当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1243423_comment'></div>论地利邪，吾东有重江之阻，西有连山之固，吾为得地矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1243423_comment'></div>论天时邪，彼灾异数见，蝗旱相仍，吾为得天矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1243423_comment'></div>将孰有能，则未知其孰贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1243423_comment'></div>颇闻其国以淫侈相尚，握兵统众者日从事于声色货财之间，非复向来深谋善战之士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1243423_comment'></div>至于主孰有道，则有不可同年而语矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1243423_comment'></div>若夫行法令、明赏罚、练士卒，则在所以自治之如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1243423_comment'></div>通好以来垂二十载，天下以兵为讳，将士日老，器械日钝，守御日懈，财赋日消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1243423_comment'></div>吾谨守誓约，不敢为之所也，迟之数年，将何以为国？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1243423_comment'></div>使彼而有谋，密以十万众分道疾驱，袭吾之不戒，岂不殆哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1243423_comment'></div>彼其张皇声势，吾得徐为之谋，天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1243423_comment'></div>曾一矢之未发，而其所以自困者，固已极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1243423_comment'></div>观其所为，如有狂疾，不度事势，无所不至，若尼玛哈诸人尚在，肯为尔邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1243423_comment'></div>意者必有奸雄之臣，阴蓄异图，使结怨内外以自弊其国，因覆而取之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1243423_comment'></div>此慕容垂、姚苌之徒所以诛苻坚而卒灭之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1243423_comment'></div>内相攻残，土崩瓦解之势，近在旦夕，不动则已，动则溃矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1243423_comment'></div>我于其间得以自警，修边疆战守之备，以待敌之可乘，岂非宗庙之灵、社稷之福乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1243423_comment'></div>阁下其何忧，亦思所以自治而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1243423_comment'></div>孟子曰：「国家闲暇，明其政刑，虽大国必畏之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1243423_comment'></div>今国家之势，谓之闲暇可乎，于此不图，尚将何待？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1243423_comment'></div>我诚图之，敌亦无以为辞，过是则不可为矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1243423_comment'></div>仰惟庙堂之上，英贤毕集，以明佐圣，举无遗策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1243423_comment'></div>固已置彼敌于计中，合谋相辅，建万世之安，在此时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1243423_comment'></div>某中原书生，老于烦使，官有常守，不敢出位而谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1243423_comment'></div>凡此所陈，特天下之大势而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1243423_comment'></div>若虑干机密，事可举行，未敢为阁下言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1243423_comment'></div>近蒙误恩，擢贰九列，就总蜀计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1243423_comment'></div>方以祖讳引避待命，未报，无缘瞻望履舄，引领恩闳，不胜惓惓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1243423_comment'></div>冬寒，钧体何似？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1243423_comment'></div>惟大君子顺时施宜，为天下自重，前膺进拜，以副圣天子责成求治、望太平于期月之意，天下幸甚，天下幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1243423_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1243424' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243424' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243424?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与叶枢密论制敌方略书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243424")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243424_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243424'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243424'>某窃惟某官今日之举，安危所系，必有成算，以全庙胜，所宜明问，探审虚实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243424_comment'></div>增军必先料军食，置戍必探察敌情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243424_comment'></div>屯数移则士卒劳，众屡分则势力弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243424_comment'></div>听言欲广，而迂诞尝试之策每足以误国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243424_comment'></div>求财欲急，而浮夸无实之人常至于败事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243424_comment'></div>此在于精之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243424_comment'></div>若乃临机制变，虽无常形，要先胜后战，则谋不可不素定，愿相公熟计之，狂夫之言或有裨于万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243424_comment'></div>某不胜僣易惶恐之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1243424_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年11月15日</a>　在成都，上宰执书，言钱粮不足，有请于朝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年11月21日</a>　在成都，言吴璘多病，而金人重兵对垒，朝廷应预为之备。作品：论吴璘多病乞吴拱自襄阳归蜀朝札。<div id='poem_1243380' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243380' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243380?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论吴璘多病乞吴拱自襄阳归蜀朝劄<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三十一年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年11月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243380")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243380_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243380'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243380'>某职总四川财赋，专一报发御前军马文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243380_comment'></div>有大利害，公上所宜知者，不敢不以上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243380_comment'></div>若朝廷行与不行，则非某之所敢必也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243380_comment'></div>契勘宣抚吴璘，天资忠义，志在立功，爱惜邦财，不啻己物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243380_comment'></div>今之委寄，诚为得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243380_comment'></div>自闻警报，即至杀金平、仙人原，与贼相持七十馀日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243380_comment'></div>中间取秦、陇、洮、兰等州及仙人原等处城寨，又分遣王彦东取商、虢，委有功绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243380_comment'></div>然金人重兵尽在凤翔府大散关、和尚原一带，多积粮食，守备甚固，其意未可测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243380_comment'></div>此贼不破，川蜀之忧未艾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243380_comment'></div>吴璘日夜措画，以图攻取，事未可期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243380_comment'></div>而其人平时多病，日饵丹砂数十百粒，比暴露之久，时复发作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243380_comment'></div>前欲遣姚仲出秦州而身自攻关，辄苦脏腑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243380_comment'></div>脏腑稍安，又苦肾肠之疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243380_comment'></div>每疾剧时，亦颇危殆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243380_comment'></div>今月十五日下仙人原还兴州医治，却留姚仲在原上弹压兵马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243380_comment'></div>彊敌对垒，人心危惧，四川事势可为寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243380_comment'></div>蜀人前此恃以为安者，以其侄吴拱在此，缓急有赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243380_comment'></div>吴拱移襄阳，渠每以失助为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243380_comment'></div>今疾如此，岂可不预为之所？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243380_comment'></div>某不知东南事体紧慢，吴拱可辍不可辍，只论目今蜀中形势，不若亟令吴拱复还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243380_comment'></div>使吴璘一向安健而得吴拱之助，则军声愈振，可以速成大功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243380_comment'></div>假使疾势增损不常，则此一军亦无他虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243380_comment'></div>吴璘既为宣抚而尚领都统职事，若除吴拱为都统，而吴璘以宣抚使判兴州，于体尤顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243380_comment'></div>窃恐朝廷以吴拱归蜀，襄鄂阙帅为疑，则李师颜见驻峡州，可以就用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243380_comment'></div>夔非冲要，谋帅不难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243380_comment'></div>人命不可知，一方安危，所系至重，望朝廷权事轻重，速赐处置施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1243380_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年11月29日</a>　在成都，奏请四川州县田契税钱由茶马司拘收，应大军支遣。朝廷从之。此举扰民，众咸怨之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年11月</a>　在成都，申奏四川收支及军费缺少数目。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年12月2日</a>　在成都。诏委王之望专一收掌钱引三百万道，逐旋约度合用之，数作料次给降，足以给用即止。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年12月3日</a>　在成都，上札复言吴璘病，乞朝廷权事体轻重，还吴拱于蜀。作品：论吴璘多病乞吴拱自襄阳归蜀朝札。<div id='poem_1243380' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243380' id='poem_sentence_25_1243380_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年1月</a>　在成都，言应付吴拱襄阳官兵钱粮为难，望免行科拨。从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年2月</a>　在成都，有启贺虞允文为兵部尚书、川陕宣谕使。作品：远迎奉使虞尚书启。贺川陕宣谕虞尚书启。<div id='poem_1243491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243491?labeling=true' target='_blank'>远迎奉使虞尚书启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243491")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243491_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243491'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243491'>衔命九重，远抚雍梁之域；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243491_comment'></div>抗旌万里，近临参井之虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243491_comment'></div>士民属目以欢呼，将卒倾心而踊跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243491_comment'></div>恭惟某官器全酬酢，学富经纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243491_comment'></div>夙推开济之才，聿际亨嘉之会，受知圣主，遍历清涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243491_comment'></div>督战淮淝，既运筹而取胜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243491_comment'></div>宣威陇蜀，将传檄以收功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243491_comment'></div>行书竹帛之勋，入总枢机之柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243491_comment'></div>某久违英范，辱在下风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243491_comment'></div>猥限匏瓜，已失争先之睹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243491_comment'></div>载驰竿牍，益深仰止之高。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1243491_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1243492' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243492' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243492?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺川陕宣谕虞尚书启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243492")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243492_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243492'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243492'>位登八座，任重七兵，以六官常伯之尊，膺一面信臣之遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243492_comment'></div>凡居庥庇，举切欢愉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243492_comment'></div>恭惟某官浩气凌云，宏才绝类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243492_comment'></div>雄文奥学，得江汉之洪深；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243492_comment'></div>直节高标，等岷峨之峻拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243492_comment'></div>骤跻华贯，动契清衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243492_comment'></div>珥笔螭坳，妙极一时之选；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243492_comment'></div>演纶凤掖，炳同三代之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243492_comment'></div>当圣哲驰骛之秋，罄侍从论思之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243492_comment'></div>方采石收功于耆定，乃古梁抗志以经营，宣国威灵，谕王德意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243492_comment'></div>召公分陕，聊专二伯之权；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243492_comment'></div>裴度平淮，即晋三司之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243492_comment'></div>某辱知最厚，藉荫甚周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243492_comment'></div>苏代使秦，正赖馀光之振；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243492_comment'></div>相如告蜀，行遵偏檄之驰<span class='inlineComment2'>（《汉滨集》卷一二。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243492_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1243492'>偏：据文意疑当作「遍」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1243492_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年2月18日</a>　在成都，乞依向来体例，人户推割赋税，各有归者。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　在成都，与冯编修书。因老病及大军供输调护之难，王之望有辞官之意。又论先王之政未有不本于人情者。<div id='poem_1243416' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243416' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243416?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与冯编修书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243416")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243416_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243416'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243416'>某顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243416_comment'></div>比承选参枢幕，结课归班，想遂有峻除，便登要近也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243416_comment'></div>瓜洲之变，天下大庆，狂暴之极，势必至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243416_comment'></div>前年元枢书固尝言之，果如所料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243416_comment'></div>尔后累月，亦不闻诸军乘势深入，投机之会，似稍失时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243416_comment'></div>或战或和，进退未决，师老财费，定当如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243416_comment'></div>取地甚易，保之实难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243416_comment'></div>要之，不大歼其众，未可议恢复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243416_comment'></div>大驾至建康，士气必振，将帅有能摧锋而前者否，回銮在何时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243416_comment'></div>蜀中事言之不能尽，敌尚扼散关，守备甚固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243416_comment'></div>岁前吴宣抚使姚仲攻不克，遂令将三万馀人出秦亭以攻巩州，又不能下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243416_comment'></div>此月初退保甘谷城，遣偏将戍秦亭，应接洮、兰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243416_comment'></div>又取河州，见图熙州与德顺军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243416_comment'></div>王彦之众分屯商、虢、陕、华四州间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243416_comment'></div>虢、华为敌取，敌去复得之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243416_comment'></div>陕州亦被攻犯，事未可保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243416_comment'></div>我师十馀万众，与敌相持半年于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243416_comment'></div>供输调护之难，不言可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243416_comment'></div>事变之来，千端万绪，一或失当，便触祸机，处势艰危，无甚于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243416_comment'></div>盖蜀中向来用兵，又吴为宣抚，诸将受其节制，而主财计者皆其腹心之人，故诛求可节，应办差易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243416_comment'></div>今总所以孤立一司有限之积，应三军仓卒无穷之须，朝廷在远，无所倚重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243416_comment'></div>虽使古人居此，亦未必无悔，况如不肖者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243416_comment'></div>兵家举措，事成则乘胜而进，自取功名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243416_comment'></div>逗留则称粮道不继，嫁祸于有司以自解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243416_comment'></div>仆皆先事办具，要使无以为词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243416_comment'></div>当与者，虽多至数十钜万而不吝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243416_comment'></div>不当与者，一钱不可横得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243416_comment'></div>裁之以制，应之以权，而守之以义，不惊不惧，迟速惟宜，亦可谓顽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243416_comment'></div>罢兵日久，敌忽犯塞，警报仓卒，事皆创行，昼夜不得息者五十馀日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243416_comment'></div>水航陆负，自利州至鱼关五六百里之间，相踵不绝，而百姓不与其劳，人皆骇异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243416_comment'></div>粮糗钱帛所在桩积，未尝稍乏，士众悦服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243416_comment'></div>而吴宣抚尤见推重，腹心相照，称叹感激不容于口，以为前后军兴，饷馈未有如今日之裕然者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243416_comment'></div>然于四川常赋盐酒之外，一毫不歛，惟利路以迫近边界，调夫于关外运粮勿已，盖有不得已者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243416_comment'></div>州县间约束素定，绝无行移，而赡军岁入络绎而至，争先取羡，以赴期会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243416_comment'></div>本所未尝遣一卒、差一官、追一胥、起一狱，以相迫促也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243416_comment'></div>岁终籴本、折估比较租额计增二百六十馀万引，比递年最高之数增三百八十馀万引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243416_comment'></div>呜呼，已极不可复加！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243416_comment'></div>昔李巽为度支盐铁转运，涖职一年，征课所入如刘晏之多，明年过之，又明年增一百八十万缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243416_comment'></div>以今视之，可无愧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243416_comment'></div>此皆朝廷采听信任之明，四路同官悉心协济之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243416_comment'></div>仆以不才，得免旷责，岂非幸耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243416_comment'></div>兵兴之初，诸将各营山寨，般粮运帑，为保险自固之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243416_comment'></div>兴元惊扰尤重，守官者往往逃遁而西，流言相怖，远近惶骇，人人莫有固志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243416_comment'></div>虽东西路亦有欲谋移治者，相劝仆迁避者多矣，盖利州无兵之可守，无险之可恃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1243416_comment'></div>仆谓此户部仓库所在，其中贮积甚多，既不容般运，吾将安往？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1243416_comment'></div>事若不测，亦以一家殉于此而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1243416_comment'></div>因泰然不动，处之若事无时，且立赏罚，禁止官吏之奔窜扇摇众心者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1243416_comment'></div>于是人情翕然安定，自剑而西，如不闻有兵，郊邑间熙熙然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1243416_comment'></div>此不待仆言，蜀人皆能道，因书略及耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1243416_comment'></div>许丈到阙，忧本所之不足，请添印钱引百万，渠意甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1243416_comment'></div>此亦未尝增添，恐有币轻之患，姑少缓之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1243416_comment'></div>近申明朝廷，乞陕西行用钱引，已依所请，今甚流通，诸军不复多邀银绢，大为公私之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1243416_comment'></div>度牒五千道，才卖十之一二，今既减价，必速售也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1243416_comment'></div>官告发及五六分，讼词不息，吏缘为奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1243416_comment'></div>有一户八千引而不到官，皆为官吏所乾没，可惜可惜！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1243416_comment'></div>仆之措画，大抵随事消息，以尽变通，务在军民之兼裕，供馈虽广而所费省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1243416_comment'></div>谓如增价以籴月粮，士卒既利而官实得贱米。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1243416_comment'></div>盖既出戍，有添支口食，而家小食月粮不尽，却得高价以资助征夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1243416_comment'></div>又赍见钱就籴于关外四州，比之转输，其直甚减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1243416_comment'></div>四州临边，谷米不自保，而官为增价以收，民固便矣，又得此钱以应率歛，上下无不利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1243416_comment'></div>只此两事，自省百万馀引，其他皆称是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1243416_comment'></div>军行合有糗糒，前此皆诸军自造，数不能多，而民被其扰，仆夏秋间预作措置，兑买四州秋税，造一色糜棋子，凡二百馀万觔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1243416_comment'></div>军中云，只食糜棋子，亦可为数月之粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1243416_comment'></div>此皆前所未有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1243416_comment'></div>凡此等事不可悉数，姑举其一二耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1243416_comment'></div>吴宣抚所以深相照者，盖每事应手，殊不费其力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1243416_comment'></div>闻尝谕其将士云：「老宣抚时，军食不继，折估欠四个月，尔辈所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1243416_comment'></div>今总所钱粮应副如此，若不能立功，他日何所推托邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1243416_comment'></div>军中多为歌谣以赞誉，不欲写去耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1243416_comment'></div>吴宣抚去冬病作，势颇危殆，人心忧惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1243416_comment'></div>十二月后渐平，亦一方之幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1243416_comment'></div>自兵兴后，兵书羽檄及申奏朝省之文，皆仆自亲，已充栋宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1243416_comment'></div>其间多关利害，不能尽致，略录一轴奉呈，可以见其梗槩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1243416_comment'></div>久欲遣人到朝廷，实为无暇，欲少说则不济事，多说则不可尽，所以懒于发信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1243416_comment'></div>兼有事公议，说不说何所损益，独于吾友不可不略述所怀耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1243416_comment'></div>仆自别后，精力之衰，一年不如一年，入春以来尤甚，一病阅月不能出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1243416_comment'></div>今虽勉强，全枝梧不行，方此艰难，又不能便尔求去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1243416_comment'></div>有劄子恳庙堂，乞边事稍定陶铸一宫观差遣，期于必得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1243416_comment'></div>不然须致仕而归，幸于东道力为一言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1243416_comment'></div>虽有投劄，今更纳一本，吾友面致之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1243416_comment'></div>兵用不用，夏间虽见次第，才有定议，便告下手，文字到此亦在秋中，庶可趁时出峡，不容缓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1243416_comment'></div>其私计之不便，劄子中详言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1243416_comment'></div>吾友以谓仆可留乎，不可留乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1243416_comment'></div>朝廷用人未尝不均劳逸，既尽其力，必恤其身，而及其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1243416_comment'></div>以其去留久近、难易、閒剧，比方前人，略相参酌而垂情焉，则足以尽天下人材之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1243416_comment'></div>曰某也才，吾方倚之，于彼岁为此言，然初无毫发异于寻常，而徒久置之于不便之地，然则人孰肯为才乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1243416_comment'></div>皆如仆之不才可矣，若果有才者亦岂肯尽其用乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1243416_comment'></div>人臣之大戒，以东西南北不择事而安之为忠，故《春秋》严君臣之分，不以家事辞王事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1243416_comment'></div>然《北山》之大夫役使不均，辄形于怨刺，其诗曰：「嘉我未老，鲜我方将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1243416_comment'></div>旅力方刚，经营四方」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1243416_comment'></div>说者曰：「嘉、鲜皆善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1243416_comment'></div>王善我未老乎，善我方壮乎，谓我之气力方盛乎，何乃独久使我经营四方也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1243416_comment'></div>其自矜不逊如此，若责以《春秋》之义，自当诛绝，而圣人取之以垂万世，常窃怪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1243416_comment'></div>反复思惟，而后得其旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1243416_comment'></div>《春秋》所以立大法，诗人所以尽下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1243416_comment'></div>夫君上出命，下之人或不能承，在王法有所必诛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1243416_comment'></div>人臣尽瘁，上之人或不加恤，在人情岂容无怨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1243416_comment'></div>下之以情怨上，亦犹上之以法诛下，有不能自已者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1243416_comment'></div>是故文王以天子之命命将帅，遣戍役，歌《采薇》以遣之，《出车》以劳还，《杕杜》以勤归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1243416_comment'></div>叙其征行之久，往来之勤，「靡室靡家，不遑启处」，慰劳而抚摩之，于再于三，以谓不如此不足以承天保之政也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1243416_comment'></div>《北山》之诗与《采薇》、《出车》、《杕杜》，其言大抵相类，而美刺之不同如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1243416_comment'></div>盖《采薇》三诗出于上，而《北山》之诗发于下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1243416_comment'></div>若文王之将帅守卫艰勤，而无《采薇》、《出车》、《杕杜》之思，安知其无《北山》大夫之作乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1243416_comment'></div>虽君子之仕，志存许国，不以通塞易虑，然先王之政，未有不本于人情者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1243416_comment'></div>人情有所不欲，未尝抑而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1243416_comment'></div>圣人以《春秋》、风、雅立大法而尽下情，岂不两得也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1243416_comment'></div>若仆辈初无事劳可纪，而叨冒过当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1243416_comment'></div>光华持节，遍阅诸司，日愧《伐檀》「素餐」之讥，上不敢冀《采薇》将帅之荣，下无从起《北山》大夫之怨，姑因议论所及，以释经义之疑耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1243416_comment'></div>仆老矣，非有倖觊如前政数公之进用，姑欲得一閒官以归东南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1243416_comment'></div>造物照知有素，亦必哀怜之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1243416_comment'></div>所欲言者无穷，病倦不能尽，幸察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_110_1243416_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　在成都，与徐左司书，论军需钱粮。作品：与徐左司论军须钱书。<div id='poem_1243410' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243410' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243410?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与徐左司论军须钱书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243410")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243410_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243410'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243410'>某万里相望，稍疏具记，可量瞻向，某猥以不才，谬当西蜀之剧任，适丁兵兴，大军十二三万人与寇相持者半年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243410_comment'></div>孤立一司，独抗三边，费尽调护，诸帅幸皆无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243410_comment'></div>而湖广总领所横相侵迫，殊不晓所谓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243410_comment'></div>方此扰攘，尤费应酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243410_comment'></div>蜀中向发吴拱下三千二百馀人、数百匹马隶鄂州军，各借请三月去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243410_comment'></div>朝廷令吴璘限一季招填，则已无此额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243410_comment'></div>而湖广申请将元额衣粮草料从蜀中应付，津般之费岁计五百六十馀万引，此为可行乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243410_comment'></div>自古未闻水陆三千里，按月调运供军也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243410_comment'></div>朝廷以给降湖广米五万石、铜钱三万馀贯、银五万两，尽可支办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243410_comment'></div>又有指挥，如不足，许于军前应干桩管钱米，及附近州军不以有无拘碍钱物内移运支遣，何苦力欲困厄于西蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243410_comment'></div>此其不可晓者一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243410_comment'></div>朝廷许湖广于二十九年四川发赴行在银内截拨钱五十万贯，计银一十五万馀两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243410_comment'></div>四川已发过银二十八万馀两，湖广若行截发，不患不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243410_comment'></div>彼其不能违管押官之恳请，容情放过，却一向责办本所催发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243410_comment'></div>其二十九年四川合发之物已皆尽绝，复何催之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243410_comment'></div>此其不可晓者二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243410_comment'></div>又欲兑三十一年经总钱粮银五六十万两，二年共有铁钱一百二十万贯，川价约买得银十七万两而止，夫何误以彼中铜钱算计？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243410_comment'></div>况百二十万贯已发过一百四万七千馀贯，未发仅十五万馀贯铁钱，而欲兑银五六十万两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243410_comment'></div>此其不可晓者三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243410_comment'></div>去年朝廷再令拘截四川经过钱银五十万贯，此项亦合作铜钱算计，为银十五万两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243410_comment'></div>湖广乃并应副江州戚方钱三十万贯，纽作八十万贯，欲银二十四万二千四百馀两，殊不讨究戚方钱三十万贯，即系两年经总钱一百二十四万铁钱之数，差误抑又甚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243410_comment'></div>矧此五十万贯一项，四川已发过银二万六千九百馀两、金二十馀两、绢三百馀匹，焉得有银二十四万馀两乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243410_comment'></div>此其不可晓者四也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243410_comment'></div>今已通发过数言之，所欠甚不多，乃欲先兑那银八十万两，果何所谓？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243410_comment'></div>朝廷元降指挥，系每岁应副江鄂州钱六十万贯，据未起钱数行下合起官司兑那。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243410_comment'></div>所谓合起官司，乃四路宪司耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243410_comment'></div>本所初无与，既无未起数目，其将何自兑那？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243410_comment'></div>凡所申请，分毫无是处，朝廷不曾勘当，便为施行，四方万里何所赴愬？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243410_comment'></div>军期急速，岂不误事耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243410_comment'></div>幸从都司详酌，呼上部吏当面诘问，顷刻可了，殊不难决也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243410_comment'></div>本所每有申明，皆某手自为之，字字有归，事事有理，试一观之，自不逃乎聪明，辱垂领略，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1243410_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　在成都，上何溥书，论四川虽军兴而常赋之外一毫不敛。作品：通何内翰书。<div id='poem_1243412' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243412' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243412?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通何内翰书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243412")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243412_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243412'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243412'>某去秋遣人具问，正初人回，复领教翰，不胜感慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243412_comment'></div>西鄙自去年九月敌近塞，应副军事，晓夕不得休息者两月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243412_comment'></div>向后稍定，孤立一司，独抗三边，与贼对垒半年于此矣，供须调护之难，更不待言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243412_comment'></div>只以东南事势视之，此则可想也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243412_comment'></div>一事失当，便触祸机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243412_comment'></div>所幸区处素定，应合干用军须，率皆前期办具，上自宣帅，下至将士，无不悦服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243412_comment'></div>诸军有意外之求，一切格之以法，彼知一出于公，不敢怨怼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243412_comment'></div>而四川之民常赋之外，一毫不歛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243412_comment'></div>约束州县，不得假托军兴为名，擅有科敷，以此郡县不知用兵，百姓安于田亩，如太平时熙熙然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243412_comment'></div>其如解严未有期，不得不爱养民力，以固根本，庶可持久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243412_comment'></div>蜀人易动难安，官吏并缘侵刻，何事不有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243412_comment'></div>斡旋计虑，倍费心神，未知攸济，阁下其兴怜否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243412_comment'></div>某敢冀而不敢必也，尚祈洞鉴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1243412_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年闰2月16日</a>　在成都。姚仲幕属朱绂投札于王之望，请科敛四川民户出财赏军。王之望怒答书。作品：回朱都干书。<div id='poem_1243413' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243413' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243413?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回朱都干书<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三十二年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年闰2月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243413")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243413_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243413'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243413'>某辱示劄目，见咎不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1243413", 1243413, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>科敷</span>百姓，异哉足下之言也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243413_comment'></div>本所以财赋为职事，应副诸军，自当竭力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243413_comment'></div>若是军须阙乏，有功将士合赏，但于王少卿取办可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243413_comment'></div>至于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1243413", 1243413, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>科敷</span>不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1243413", 1243413, "Clauses/9/Comments/1")'>科敷</span>，他人何预哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243413_comment'></div>仆中原人，蜀中无一毫生业，亦无亲族寓居，其不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1243413", 1243413, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>科敷</span>，何私于蜀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243413_comment'></div>盖以大军十馀万众，仰给于此，不得不爱养其力，否则三军坐困矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243413_comment'></div>如足下辈月俸岁廪不从空虚中来，亦知其所自乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243413_comment'></div>朝廷德意深厚，每务宽恤，东南调度如此，亦不闻歛取于民，四川独可横赋乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243413_comment'></div>国家养兵，所以保民，而足下乃谓「军民不两立」，恐非安民和众丰财之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243413_comment'></div>又云「用兵本约两月，今已四个月，然则解严未可期也」，若本所当时便徇诸处无艺之求，只作两月计，则今日何以支吾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243413_comment'></div>事未可期，则所费无限，不且爱养民力以备方来之须，将如异日何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243413_comment'></div>仆之不歛于民力，所以为诸军也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243413_comment'></div>用兵百三十日，糗粮、草料、银绢、钱引，所在委积，未尝乏兴，而足下乃尔云云，不知军行出入，何处阙钱粮，何处阙草料？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243413_comment'></div>累次喝犒并朝廷支赐，自是诸军应报稽缓，文字才到所，立便给散，略无留阻，祗须俟有功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243413_comment'></div>诸军既无功状，本所凭何支破？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243413_comment'></div>散关前攻不下，闻自有说，莫不为无银绢钱引否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243413_comment'></div>不知散关是险固不可取乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243413_comment'></div>是有可取之理而无银绢钱引之故，士卒不用命乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243413_comment'></div>若可取而士不用命，岂计司之责，必有任其咎者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243413_comment'></div>况闻攻关之日，死伤不少，则非士卒之不用命矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243413_comment'></div>自来兵家行动若逗挠无功，多是以粮道不继嫁祸于有司以自解，亦不闻以无堆垛赏给为词者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243413_comment'></div>国家息兵二十年，将士不战，竭四川之资以奉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243413_comment'></div>一旦临敌，更须堆垛银绢而后可用，则军政可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243413_comment'></div>且如向来和尚原、丁刘圈、杀金平诸军大捷，近日吴宣抚取方山原、秦州等处，王四厢取商、虢等州，吴四厢取唐、邓州，亦不闻先垛银绢，始能破敌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243413_comment'></div>朝廷赏格甚明，本所初无悭吝，如秦州始平之初，得宣司关状，即日行下鱼关支散，何尝稍令阙误？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243413_comment'></div>兼鱼关签厅所备金帛钱物充盈库藏，宣抚不住关揆，岂是有无桩办耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243413_comment'></div>顾生民膏血，不容无功而得耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243413_comment'></div>假令仆重行<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1243413", 1243413, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>科敷</span>，积金至斗，诸军衣粮犒设支赐之外，若无功效，一钱岂容妄得哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243413_comment'></div>若果有功，亦岂容本所以不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1243413", 1243413, "Clauses/103/Comments/0")'>科敷</span>而不赏乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243413_comment'></div>诸军但务立功，无患赏给之不行也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243413_comment'></div>但管取足，无问总所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1243413", 1243413, "Clauses/107/Comments/0")'>科敷</span>与不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1243413", 1243413, "Clauses/107/Comments/1")'>科敷</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243413_comment'></div>刘晏歛不及民，何害李、郭之勋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243413_comment'></div>李晟屯东渭桥，无积资输粮，以忠义感人，卒灭大盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243413_comment'></div>足下以书生为人幕府，不能以此等事规赞主帅，而反咎王人以不歛于民，岂不异哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243413_comment'></div>九月以后，兴元一军已支拨过钱引二十八万道、银绢二千匹两，而糗粮、草料与犒设支赏不与焉，亦不为不应副矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243413_comment'></div>若皆及将士，岂不可以立功？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243413_comment'></div>有功当赏，而未得者何人也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243413_comment'></div>朝廷分司庀职，各有所主，而于财贿出纳为尤严，经由检察，互相关防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243413_comment'></div>所有屡降指挥，凡有支费，宣司审实，总所量度，此古今通义，而圣朝之明制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243413_comment'></div>足下独不便，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243413_comment'></div>来书谓：「攻散关时，若得银绢一二万匹两、钱引一二十万道，桩在凤州，有此重赏而贼不破灭，无有也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243413_comment'></div>桩在凤州与在鱼关何异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243413_comment'></div>方宣抚以攻守之策会问节使时，亦不闻以此为言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243413_comment'></div>今散关、凤翔未破，足下可与军议，取散关要银绢引若干，取凤翔要若干，可以必克，本所当一切办集，足下可结罪保明具申，当以闻于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1243413_comment'></div>如克敌而赏不行，仆之责也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1243413_comment'></div>若本所抱认而不能克，足下当何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1243413_comment'></div>仆前后见将帅多是忠义赴功、捐躯报国之人，只缘幕中导之或非其道，以至害事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1243413_comment'></div>如姚帅之贤，固不肯妄听，然足下自不应为此异论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1243413_comment'></div>万一朝廷闻之，得无不可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1243413_comment'></div>某尝备员剡荐，预有惧焉，且宜勉思婉画，审重语言，勿恤小利以败大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1243413_comment'></div>但得主帅成功，足下复何求哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1243413_comment'></div>信笔不觉喋喋，幸照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1243413_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年闰2月</a>　在成都，与吴璘论出征将士书，时王之望腹疾作。作品：与吴宣抚论出征将士书。<div id='poem_1243414' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243414' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243414?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与吴宣抚论出征将士书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年闰2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243414")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243414_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243414'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243414'>某二十日具手劄上贺，必已呈达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243414_comment'></div>自后腹疾再作，中脘疼痛，妨于语言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243414_comment'></div>今日只差减，殊羸劣也，少意拜禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243414_comment'></div>大散、僧原已得，陕西无不下之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243414_comment'></div>传敌人遁去，若非设计，必有内变也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243414_comment'></div>今则惟在慰安关中、以收人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243414_comment'></div>切望戒戢将士，毋杀戮，毋剽掠，广宣朝廷德泽，以救遗民于死亡之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243414_comment'></div>前所遣红巾本欲令扰劫贼寨，小人无知，闻间有作过者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243414_comment'></div>宜多出榜文禁止，令其速归，不归者听百姓剿杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243414_comment'></div>诸将立功之人，若能不犯吾令，常赏之外，更特与优加犒劳，费三二十万引不妨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243414_comment'></div>本所虽用度至广，亦当那融应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243414_comment'></div>若故违约束，虽有功者亦深治之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243414_comment'></div>如此，则威德盛行，人谁敢犯？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243414_comment'></div>此皆钧虑所及，或已施行，何待他人之言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243414_comment'></div>其所以僭易者，盖同舟而济，休戚实均，深欲门下成此一段功名耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243414_comment'></div>力疾，作字不谨，并乞照察，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1243414_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年闰2月26日</a>　在成都，言于宰执，金人和议甚切，宜审处三事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年闰2月28日</a>　在成都，王之望、虞允文取拨百万钱引以备招军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年3月8日</a>　在成都，以军饷无缺，试太府卿。上谢表。作品：谢授太府卿表。<div id='poem_1243280' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243280' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243280?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢授太府卿表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年8月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243280")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243280_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243280'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243280'>主计坤维，苟逭旷官之责；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243280_comment'></div>升华月寺，忽惊增秩之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243280_comment'></div>更膺修举之褒，愈切叨尘之愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243280_comment'></div>伏念臣早专儒学，初乏吏能，于财赋以何资，尤性资之所短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243280_comment'></div>矧当调饷，乃误使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243280_comment'></div>宿重戍于三边，开新疆于两路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243280_comment'></div>转输粗给，皆朝廷申画之明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243280_comment'></div>凯捷屡腾，实将帅驱驰之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243280_comment'></div>夫何绵薄，猥冒恩光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243280_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下仁孝独隆，德刑并举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243280_comment'></div>聪明睿智而不杀，伟略无前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243280_comment'></div>是非赏罚之已明，微劳必录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243280_comment'></div>故虽疏远，亦被甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243280_comment'></div>然臣衰病日侵，事功难彊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243280_comment'></div>投闲置散，已屡贡于忱诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243280_comment'></div>治剧济烦，恐终辜于寄委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243280_comment'></div>愿回明鉴，俯照丹衷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1243280_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年3月9日</a>　在成都，有启贺吴璘升少傅。作品：贺吴宣抚升少傅启。<div id='poem_1243496' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243496' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243496?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺吴宣抚升少傅启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年3月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243496")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243496_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243496'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243496'>命下广庭，爰懋肤公之报；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243496_comment'></div>宠颁异数，特升亚傅之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243496_comment'></div>中夏耸闻，军民胥悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243496_comment'></div>恭惟某官勋庸盖世，智略兼人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243496_comment'></div>身蔽坤维，著威名于三纪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243496_comment'></div>志存王室，挺忠义于一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243496_comment'></div>属强敌之侵陵，任元戎而敌忾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243496_comment'></div>投醪励众，咸思奋臂以登先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243496_comment'></div>破竹乘机，孰不望旂而远遁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243496_comment'></div>并克关山之险，一空巢穴之群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243496_comment'></div>既伟绩之弥高，宜隆恩之沓至，益峻三孤之秩，中陪多邑之腴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243496_comment'></div>上眷有加，既已极褒迁之典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243496_comment'></div>公心无斁，必将恢久大之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243496_comment'></div>丕展壮猷，嗣迎殊渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243496_comment'></div>某夙蒙辉润，欣诵诏除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243496_comment'></div>属限官常，阻遂辕门之谒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243496_comment'></div>仰伸庆问，敢稽尺牍之驰！</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1243496_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年3月</a>　在成都，回函吴璘，论退师事。作品：回吴宣抚论退师书。<div id='poem_1243415' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243415' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243415?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回吴宣抚论退师书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243415")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243415_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243415'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243415'>某二十四日在金牛，辱二十三日所赐手帖，知钧旆已还河池，不胜感慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243415_comment'></div>豫才闻和议，不审虚实，即日引遁，其畏惮可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243415_comment'></div>但我收复环、原、会州，却在退师之后，豫惩前败，能复与我争否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243415_comment'></div>今大军且在河池相近屯泊，其各分番归元来营寨休养战士，度何时可以复出？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243415_comment'></div>敌知吾回军，敢与不敢却来侵犯？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243415_comment'></div>新复州军，使司必有文字闻于朝廷，略愿知其梗槩，庶几不至牴牾。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1243415_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='c7c9a542949d45febce1dd7068b3bcd7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c7c9a542949d45febce1dd7068b3bcd7");'><span id='c7c9a542949d45febce1dd7068b3bcd7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>，59岁</div><div id='c7c9a542949d45febce1dd7068b3bcd7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年3月</a>　在成都，遗宰相书，奏乞改授一宫观差遣。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　在成都。春，以老病及儿女婚事，乞差宫祠。作品：候边事少宁乞差宫祠朝札。<div id='poem_1243381' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243381' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243381?labeling=true' target='_blank'>候边事少宁乞差宫祠朝劄<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三十二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243381")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243381_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243381'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243381'>某辄有危恳，上干洪造，伏惟宽度，曲赐矜容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243381_comment'></div>某戊辰岁秋自太学博士丐外补，出守荆门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243381_comment'></div>癸酉岁造朝，除湖南提举常平茶盐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243381_comment'></div>乙亥岁，除潼川府路转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243381_comment'></div>丁丑岁，除本路宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243381_comment'></div>戊寅岁，除成都府路转运副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243381_comment'></div>己卯岁，兼权茶马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243381_comment'></div>庚辰秋，除总领四川财赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243381_comment'></div>到官既已逾年，每有申陈，荷朝廷采录，得以粗免旷败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243381_comment'></div>非不欲益鞭驽钝，以赴事功，而入春以来，愈更得病，一卧阅月，职事妨废，昏忘羸劣，勉彊不前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243381_comment'></div>若不展尽区区，投诚于钧播，必致颠隮，上误使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243381_comment'></div>伏念某入蜀八年，私计多行不便，些小生事并诸亲戚皆在台州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243381_comment'></div>第二儿说婚多日，过时不得毕结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243381_comment'></div>第三儿将婚，一女及笄，留滞远方，莫议姻对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243381_comment'></div>奴婢随行者久而不赎，妨其丁壮，朝夕煎聒，在人情亦所不堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243381_comment'></div>犬马之齿，明年六十，求田问舍，正尔茫然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243381_comment'></div>虽一身叨荣，冒膺宠禄，而以一家论之，实皆不得其所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243381_comment'></div>老夫老妇，常婴疾疢，每虑一旦溘先朝露，其为狼狈，何可胜言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243381_comment'></div>中夜念之，心如焦灼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243381_comment'></div>方圣君贤相在上，万物必遂其生，有如孤踪跋疐如此，诚仁人君子之所宜动心者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243381_comment'></div>悉数前后官蜀之人，无如某之久，见今在蜀者，亦无居某之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243381_comment'></div>累政总领去留久近，岁月可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243381_comment'></div>顾今重兵对垒，供馈方急，岂主计者援例求去之时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243381_comment'></div>敢不且竭衰疲，终此调饷，候边事稍定，应办无阙，乞加怜悯，陶铸一宫观差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243381_comment'></div>使十五年流落之身，略归东南，了毕嫁娶，整葺生理，以宽投老之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243381_comment'></div>庶几心志和宁，得从安养，则桑榆暮景，尽出生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243381_comment'></div>感戴恩私，何啻痿人之复起、羁藟之见释也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243381_comment'></div>未委沟壑间，他日或别有驱策，死而后已，其敢有辞！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243381_comment'></div>预布腹心，情辞迫切，不胜惶惧祈哀俟命之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1243381_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年4月15日</a>　在成都，以虞允文须索渐广，王之望移书宰执议论军储，二人始有隙。有书与虞允文论事。作品：与虞宣谕论事书。<div id='poem_1243417' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243417' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243417?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与虞宣谕论事书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年4月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243417")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243417_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243417'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243417'>某得幸大君子七年于兹，非徒小人平时慕用之诚，西南莫比，而门下所以眷遇推许，亦不居众人之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243417_comment'></div>其心腹相照，固无俟于言说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243417_comment'></div>至于当官则各有职事，不敢望以私恩相假借。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243417_comment'></div>尚书蜀人，今出使于蜀，人未必不疑其以故乡而有所私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243417_comment'></div>某素荷知奖，人未必不疑其以旧职而有所庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243417_comment'></div>若每事讨理，明辨其是非，则适足见台座处事之至公，而小人居官之不苟，初无损于心腹之照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243417_comment'></div>所谓和而不同，以共济国事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243417_comment'></div>朝廷闻之，亦必不以为非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243417_comment'></div>其间虽或小有异同，亦无害大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243417_comment'></div>古人转祸为福，因败为功，多此类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243417_comment'></div>如此，则使司所行，或有未尽，本所固不敢有慊；<div class='inline'
