id='poem_sentence_10_1243417_comment'></div>本所所办，或有未合，使司亦不须加怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243417_comment'></div>庶几乎忠臣之节，要归于是而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243417_comment'></div>伏望高明深加恕谅，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1243417_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年4月18日</a>　在利州，将诸州军三十一年库钱增数最多者姓名禀报朝廷。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c15dd4f533f84ce783ddb0c1aaaee70e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c15dd4f533f84ce783ddb0c1aaaee70e");'><span id='c15dd4f533f84ce783ddb0c1aaaee70e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1163')">1162-1163年</a>，59-60岁</div><div id='c15dd4f533f84ce783ddb0c1aaaee70e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年4月27日</a>　在成都，得随军转运判官赵不愚报，向虞允文及朝廷申报粮料之事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　在成都，有启贺汪澈除参知政事。作品：贺汪参政启。<div id='poem_1243497' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243497' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243497?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺汪参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243497")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243497_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243497'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243497'>显擢真儒，荣参大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243497_comment'></div>纶言诞布，丕昭帝眷之隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243497_comment'></div>舆诵佥谐，允副民瞻之峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243497_comment'></div>庇庥所及，庆忭交增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243497_comment'></div>窃观历代之盛衰，系视辅臣之臧否，诚得元弼，始收隽功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243497_comment'></div>未有用无奇之才，而能办非常之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243497_comment'></div>况圣哲驰骛之岁，匪国家閒暇之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243497_comment'></div>毫釐晷刻之差，患遗寰宇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243497_comment'></div>钱谷甲兵之问，日至庙堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243497_comment'></div>必资名世之英，斯展经邦之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243497_comment'></div>天祐明圣，时登俊良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243497_comment'></div>恭惟某官识洞古今，量涵清浊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243497_comment'></div>中和禀粹，浑然九德之资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243497_comment'></div>精密穷微，邃以六经之蕴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243497_comment'></div>曩由公道，自结主知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243497_comment'></div>三院阶升，凛风霜于百辟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243497_comment'></div>一台坐正，肃仪轨于万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243497_comment'></div>众论攸归，上心弥简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243497_comment'></div>属边尘之犯顺，持使节以宣威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243497_comment'></div>势壮荆吴，奋周瑜之雄略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243497_comment'></div>忠输淮蔡，验裴度之嘉谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243497_comment'></div>人皆曰贤，政将焉往？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243497_comment'></div>折冲有赖，已书竹帛之勋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243497_comment'></div>注意既深，即迅钧衡之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243497_comment'></div>某欣闻新渥，阻造崇墉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243497_comment'></div>应龙翔而云雾兴，伫须霖雨之下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243497_comment'></div>大厦成而燕雀贺，永依柱石之穹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243497_comment'></div>溽暑尚烦，灵襟多裕，期茂加于调护，庸宏济于艰难。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1243497_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年5月3日</a>　在成都，乞根据民户嫁资及遗嘱田合纳契税钱，应付赡军支用。从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年5月4日</a>　在成都，言兼权提举秦司所有茶事，未曾承准指挥。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年5月8日</a>　在成都，再乞宫观，朝廷不许。王之望又言钱粮事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年5月13日</a>　在成都，有书与虞允文、吴璘，论论买马招兵及吴璘、姚仲出师事。作品：回虞宣谕吴姚二大将出兵书。<div id='poem_1243418' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243418' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243418?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回虞宣谕吴姚二大将出兵书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年5月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243418")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243418_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243418'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243418'>某今早承局还，伏辱台翰，继递中又拜十三日教赐，不胜感激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243418_comment'></div>王提干马已买得四十六疋，葛彦奇十六疋，渠辈得回岩昌，自然易办矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243418_comment'></div>商、兰两州招纳降附，可喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243418_comment'></div>若有益于国，本所不敢惮供亿之烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243418_comment'></div>所以夙夜辛勤，横身以当众怨者，正欲节省用度，以济大事，非敢靳吝财赋，当用以沮将士之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243418_comment'></div>孔明所谓限之以爵，爵加则知荣，一颦一笑，足以激厉，生民膏血，岂容妄得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243418_comment'></div>赏不当于有功，犹辇金币以塞庐山之壑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243418_comment'></div>归顺之人，须当优假，何所爱乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243418_comment'></div>但向去事大，不知所用几何，若涉大水未知攸济耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243418_comment'></div>适领使檄，买马以百运为限，亦得中数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243418_comment'></div>乞罢招兵，尤为至论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243418_comment'></div>本所岂敢望赐，只得国事利，小人与有获焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243418_comment'></div>方今之弊，不在兵少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243418_comment'></div>孔明街亭之败，归而减卒，兵贵精不贵多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243418_comment'></div>淮南之溃，采矶之捷，其众寡可验矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243418_comment'></div>南北通使，和议必成，亦须一再往返耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243418_comment'></div>移书宣威，且议休息生灵之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243418_comment'></div>某昨日因书止其再出，大暑如此，岂用兵时耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243418_comment'></div>征士征行，百姓发运，皆是危事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243418_comment'></div>师老锐挫，若遇大敌，岂不可忧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243418_comment'></div>此乃安危所系，用度不足言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243418_comment'></div>甚善，甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243418_comment'></div>姚帅年来数奇，不可委以要地，更宜与宣威议之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243418_comment'></div>因粮事不敢必，只得不至过当，足矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1243418_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年5月13日</a>　在成都，有书与吴璘论粮籴本钱事。作品：回虞宣谕论因粮籴本钱书。<div id='poem_1243419' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243419' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243419?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回虞宣谕论因粮籴本钱书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年5月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243419")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243419_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243419'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243419'>某旦日再具劄目，伏想呈彻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243419_comment'></div>是日又领真翰，今日巳时又拜初一日所赐教帖，不胜感慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243419_comment'></div>应副使司，初西县瞻侍之日，便曾上禀，岂敢二三，后缘所索窠名皆乌有先生，不得不详具曲折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243419_comment'></div>前者似蒙稍察，且承指挥，姑止行移，故半月馀日不敢应报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243419_comment'></div>宣抚司文字至今未回，然闻使司已行申奏朝廷，必以为有此一项钱物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243419_comment'></div>今又睹使司所榜州县，依旧说诸军因粮所得籴本水脚等钱，即是台意终未融照，尚以本所为实有此钱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243419_comment'></div>既以上闻于朝廷，下播于百姓民庶，则本所岂得独稽留台府前牒而不报乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243419_comment'></div>他日责逋慢之罪，某何以为辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243419_comment'></div>不免具因依申使司，乞行会问宣抚司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243419_comment'></div>如果有上件省减到钱，则见今本所库中所有自可遣官拘占，不必问本所之可否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243419_comment'></div>如无所省减，却使本所虚抱此名，而为朝廷百姓之所不韪，某么么岂敢任此也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243419_comment'></div>兼应副诸军籴本，非所出于总领，皆百姓之脂膏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243419_comment'></div>以百姓之脂膏供三军之口实，则民无怨讟，而军以效命为当然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243419_comment'></div>今若诸军自因粮而不费百姓之资，则诸军责望于民者益深，而百姓之所以咎本司者亦无所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243419_comment'></div>朝廷亦以总所初无应副，而蜀民无预于军兴，岂不为四川之大祸哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243419_comment'></div>窃望台慈遍会将帅，若会到数目，行下本所，对行出豁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243419_comment'></div>如此，则于使司无一毫之损，而本所与诸帅各得分明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243419_comment'></div>窃意台府所以如此有疑未解者，必亦有所据依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243419_comment'></div>或是诸军各有申到因粮数目，所以显见于榜奏行移之间，而独本所喑不得说，则有无何以自辨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243419_comment'></div>财赋不同他事，可借以虚词，一钱须要一钱下落，皆有出入簿账，岂容有所隐匿也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243419_comment'></div>某衰病如此，或去谅非久于此者，隐匿财物欲以何为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243419_comment'></div>某前者劄呈朝廷，乞以因粮于敌奖励将帅，而大称吴宣抚恢复不曾般运粮草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243419_comment'></div>至于应副博易本钱之多，置之不言，盖欲诱掖劝相，以成将帅之功名，非于本所有对减之利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243419_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1243419'>〔小贴子〕必不得已，则陕西谷贱，可以量给价直，犹愈于搬运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243419_comment'></div>区区之意，但知息四川调夫之苦，非有爱于本所财也，亦非有意与诸帅争功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243419_comment'></div>不意事非始图，转而至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243419_comment'></div>实应副诸军籴博本钱，皆置而不录；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243419_comment'></div>实不曾得诸军粮米，而曰有收，朝廷在远，何以照察？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243419_comment'></div>而四川百姓为全不佐公家用兵之急，将使如朱绂辈所言得行，皆某喑然不为辨白之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243419_comment'></div>尚书聪明，无所不烛，且以忧国爱民为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243419_comment'></div>今将使事之重，上为朝廷所信，中为将帅所承，下为百姓所仰，一言之发，小关利害，大系安危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243419_comment'></div>以为无则实无，以为有则实有，本所岂可受闇昧于疑似之间，不以自明于当路之大贤也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243419_comment'></div>伏惟公恕仁明，谅其事非得已，弗罪其喋喋，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243419_comment'></div>不胜惶恐之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1243419_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年5月13日</a>　在成都，有书与吴璘论买马招兵及吴璘、姚仲出师事。作品：与吴宣抚论再出散关书。<div id='poem_1243421' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243421' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243421?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与吴宣抚论再出散关书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年5月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243421")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243421_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243421'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243421'>某向在领三月二十三日钧翰，欲少歇中伤士卒于河池，后忽闻再出散关，不知何故，莫是有可乘之机否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243421_comment'></div>颇闻此行士卒锐气不及前时，果否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243421_comment'></div>相公智略先定，应变无方，必有成算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243421_comment'></div>方此大暑，师旅征行，百姓转饷，皆是危事，自非万全，岂可轻举？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243421_comment'></div>若果未可动，且宜待时，虽闻于朝廷可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243421_comment'></div>仰恃知照之深，敢尔僣率，伏幸优恕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1243421_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　在成都，与吴璘书，论姚仲原州败事。作品：回吴宣抚报姚仲原州败衄书。<div id='poem_1243420' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243420' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243420?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回吴宣抚报姚仲原州败衄书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243420")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243420_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243420'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243420'>某前月二十九日具手劄，计已呈彻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243420_comment'></div>今月旦日并今日巳时，荐领真翰，不胜感慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243420_comment'></div>姚帅之败、熙河之捷，前已具陈之，再枉钧谕，益详曲折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243420_comment'></div>姚军溃散，人兵莫须收拾得一半否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243420_comment'></div>其馀差占人皆可根刷得，宣抚略为整顿，便当勇气增倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243420_comment'></div>此人之败，未必不反为四川之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243420_comment'></div>所可喜者，熙州既克，幕府威名益振；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243420_comment'></div>敌知姚罢，无可窥伺，自当畏慑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243420_comment'></div>本所除已具录奏去讫，伏乞钧照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1243420_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年5月18日</a>　吴芾入对，言王之望为政尚严，督办财赋之能。高宗比之汉萧何，允大用之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年6月1日</a>　在成都，得吴璘书，报姚仲失律，王之望以书宽譬之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年6月11日</a>　高宗逊位，王之望在成都上贺表。作品：贺太上皇逊位表。茶马司贺太上皇帝逊位表。<div id='poem_1243285' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243285' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243285?labeling=true' target='_blank'>茶马司贺太上皇帝逊位表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年6月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243285")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243285_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243285'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243285'>逊位元良，法大公于尧舜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243285_comment'></div>储神淡泊，娱至道于羲皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243285_comment'></div>旷代希闻，溥天同庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243285_comment'></div>恭维太上皇帝陛下功超邃古，泽被生民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243285_comment'></div>积三纪之忧勤，既臻耆定；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243285_comment'></div>厌万几之繁委，自处冲虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243285_comment'></div>眇大物而游于初，举神器而授之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243285_comment'></div>必得其寿，如圣德何以加兹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243285_comment'></div>不离乎真，非至神孰能与此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243285_comment'></div>臣亲逢阔典，邈在远方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243285_comment'></div>绩效无闻，已辜恩于使节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243285_comment'></div>驰驱既久，徒结恋于君轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243285_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1243285_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年6月11日</a>　孝宗即位，王之望在成都上贺表。作品：贺皇帝登宝位表。茶马司贺皇帝登宝位表。<div id='poem_1243286' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243286' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243286?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺皇帝登宝位表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年6月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243286")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243286_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243286'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243286'>维天与子，聿膺内禅之传；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243286_comment'></div>为民作君，光抚中兴之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243286_comment'></div>九庙有尊安之势，万方同庆戴之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243286_comment'></div>恭维皇帝陛下德本天生，学由日就，英特同符于艺祖，慈祥并美于仁宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243286_comment'></div>方上皇以昭旷宅心，厌钱谷甲兵之问；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243286_comment'></div>宜圣主以元良继体，为讴歌朝觐之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243286_comment'></div>百姓与能，诸神受职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243286_comment'></div>揖让行岩廊之上，孝慈形宇宙之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243286_comment'></div>盛事无前，道已尊于二典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243286_comment'></div>高风所暨，化终格于三苗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243286_comment'></div>臣滥厕卿联，出将使指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243286_comment'></div>飞龙御极，欣逢践阼之辰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243286_comment'></div>流马饷边，莫预称觞之列。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1243286_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1243287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243287?labeling=true' target='_blank'>茶马司贺皇帝登位表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年6月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243287")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243287_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243287'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243287'>监国抚军，方重元良之寄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243287_comment'></div>握符秉箓，遂膺揖逊之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243287_comment'></div>和浃三灵，欢均四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243287_comment'></div>恭维皇帝陛下道参盖轸，英类祖宗，天生德以应期，人与能而归命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243287_comment'></div>帝尧克让，既高黄屋之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243287_comment'></div>夏启有光，果献大横之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243287_comment'></div>爰正重离之位，肆推作解之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243287_comment'></div>臣滥缀卿联，肃将使指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243287_comment'></div>六龙在御，徒仰庆于时乘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243287_comment'></div>百兽旅庭，曾莫陪于率舞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1243287_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年6月11日</a>　在成都，有状谢吴芾传道太上皇帝圣语。作品：谢因吴侍郎传道太上皇帝圣语状。<div id='poem_1243322' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243322' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243322?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢因吴侍郎传道太上皇帝圣语状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年6月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243322")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243322_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243322'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243322'>契勘臣收亲戚权户部侍郎吴芾家书，报云：「芾五月十八日对，上因论财在得人，遂言：『川陕用兵，朕全得一王某之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243322_comment'></div>大军十馀万众，数月与敌角，而蜀人不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243322_comment'></div>卿且道如此用兵，若不是他，如何了得』？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243322_comment'></div>又言：『王某在蜀，几如萧何在关中』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243322_comment'></div>芾奏：『王某与臣是亲戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243322_comment'></div>每得书，说经画有素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243322_comment'></div>虽用兵之久，财赋足办，未尝略以阙乏为言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243322_comment'></div>其人为政尚严，平日在蜀，令行禁止，故于财赋亦不督而办』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243322_comment'></div>上乃云：『朕不知与卿是亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243322_comment'></div>朕今日之言，与卿暗合』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243322_comment'></div>芾又奏：『王某有志于功名，但近来多病，又骨肉亦屡病，心甚念归，前时亦有书来恳庙堂宫观』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243322_comment'></div>上言：『亦见大臣云他婚嫁都未了，亦欲令归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243322_comment'></div>但蜀中少他不得，怎奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243322_comment'></div>只得教他在彼，候事稍定，朕却大用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243322_comment'></div>卿既与之是亲，因通家问，且与朕道此意，教他且在彼少留，后日当大用之』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243322_comment'></div>须至奏闻者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243322_comment'></div>右吴芾传道太上皇帝圣语，臣具录在前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243322_comment'></div>伏念臣疏远小臣，滥膺寄委，典司蜀计，适值军兴，赖朝廷申画之明，每事遵禀，得以少稽旷败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243322_comment'></div>不谓太上皇帝误简圣知，因吴芾登对，过形奖谕，比拟非伦，仍令少留，以须后用，顾问纤悉，下及其私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243322_comment'></div>恩荣所加，非臣凉薄所克负荷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243322_comment'></div>伏读惊感，涕泪交零，虽糜捐此身，何以图报万一？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243322_comment'></div>谨当更励衰病，国尔忘家，以仰副君父记怜戒敕之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243322_comment'></div>臣不敢上章德寿，而事当奏复，不容但已，谨具录奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243322_comment'></div>伏望圣慈降下尚书省，为臣备奏太上皇帝御前，庶知愚臣今已恭承睿训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243322_comment'></div>伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1243322_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年9月18日</a>　在成都，除权户部侍郎、充川陕宣谕使。上谢启。作品：除权户部侍郎川陕宣谕使谢宰相启。<div id='poem_1243499' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243499' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243499?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除权户部侍郎川陕宣谕使谢宰相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年9月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243499")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243499_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243499'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243499'>奏蜀计以归班，方趋召节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243499_comment'></div>贰民曹而谕旨，就拜除书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243499_comment'></div>辞避莫伸，凌竞罔措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243499_comment'></div>伏念某幼专儒学，初乏吏能，偶不弃于明时，遂寖更于烦使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243499_comment'></div>关山万里，几为庄舄之吟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243499_comment'></div>尘土一官，久失邯郸之步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243499_comment'></div>升华月士，总赋坤维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243499_comment'></div>适丁用武之难，粗免乏兴之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243499_comment'></div>中缘抱疾，数恳奉祠，赐环已戒于趣涂，出綍遽惊于即授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243499_comment'></div>名参从橐，朝宗辍江汉之行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243499_comment'></div>身拥使轺，扪历跨井参之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243499_comment'></div>被宠灵而特异，仰造化以知归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243499_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官大度包荒，至仁恤远，阐尊主庇民之略，行拔贤进善之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243499_comment'></div>镇静物情，掩风流于江左；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243499_comment'></div>陶成士类，悯留滞于周南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243499_comment'></div>遂俾衰踪，亦叨重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243499_comment'></div>某敢不更坚晚节，益励孤忠！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243499_comment'></div>陈力无堪，曷展驱驰之效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243499_comment'></div>投閒有请，终希坱圠之恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1243499_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年9月18日</a>　在成都，除权户部侍郎、充川陕宣谕使。上谢表。作品：谢权户部侍郎充川陕宣谕表。<div id='poem_1243288' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243288' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243288?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢权户部侍郎充川陕宣谕表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年9月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243288")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243288_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243288'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243288'>解外计以坤维，方趋召节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243288_comment'></div>摄贰卿于民守，就假使轺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243288_comment'></div>恳避莫伸，凌竞罔措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243288_comment'></div>伏念臣早更多难，晚遇明时，以疏拙之腐儒，玷光华之烦使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243288_comment'></div>并总四川之赋，粤跻九列之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243288_comment'></div>未乏军兴，实禀朝庭之令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243288_comment'></div>初无吏最，偶宽司败之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243288_comment'></div>属衰病之寖加，觉事为之难彊，惧瘝剧任，屡丐真祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243288_comment'></div>俄奉命以造朝，已理装而即路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243288_comment'></div>宸纶载下，从橐超升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243288_comment'></div>留二星参井之墟，停八月斗牛之泛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243288_comment'></div>维版使设文昌之副，未始外除；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243288_comment'></div>而王人专德意之宣，必由中遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243288_comment'></div>夫何凡品，独误殊恩！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243288_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下道本心传，学由日就，以重华文命之懿，承贞观开元之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243288_comment'></div>询事考言，特谨人材之用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243288_comment'></div>循名责实，坐观王政之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243288_comment'></div>遂使孤踪，亦叨重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243288_comment'></div>臣敢不爰咨远俗，诞布皇灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243288_comment'></div>陈力无堪，徒抱捐躯之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243288_comment'></div>投閒有请，终希从欲之仁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1243288_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年9月</a>　在成都，有启贺张焘除同知枢密院。作品：贺同知张枢密启。<div id='poem_1243498' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243498' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243498?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺同知张枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243498")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243498_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243498'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243498'>宠膺诏綍，起赞事枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243498_comment'></div>肆国家右武之秋，居廊庙本兵之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243498_comment'></div>精神所聚，形势自张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243498_comment'></div>窃惟圣贤出处之方，必顺天地盈虚之数，卓然慷慨，谨尔行藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243498_comment'></div>奉身而退，则视富贵如一毫之轻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243498_comment'></div>投袂而来，则使社稷增九鼎之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243498_comment'></div>恭惟某官德尊硕辅，学粹钜儒，忠诚表于四朝，门望光于百辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243498_comment'></div>三仕无喜，孰窥特立之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243498_comment'></div>万钟何加，独养至高之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243498_comment'></div>早联近侍，最号名臣，后生咸仰其风流，当世久希于膏泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243498_comment'></div>逮真人之继绍，屈巨哲以登庸，允赖壮猷，克宁雅俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243498_comment'></div>趣召走貂珰之使，给扶优轩陛之仪，任隆股肱，恩极体貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243498_comment'></div>一夔足矣，知公论之佥同；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243498_comment'></div>二老归之，信敌情之率服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243498_comment'></div>伟哉用江左之杰，信尔寝淮南之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243498_comment'></div>惟具瞻之既孚，岂爰立之可缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243498_comment'></div>基命宥密，暂烦帷幄之筹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243498_comment'></div>谟明弼谐，行正钧衡之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243498_comment'></div>某远叨将指，侧听除音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243498_comment'></div>梦绕门阑，虽阻深于庆谒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243498_comment'></div>诚驰竿牍，姑少见于欢悰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1243498_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年9月</a>　在成都，有奏议论造弓箭衣甲。作品：论造弓箭衣甲奏议。<div id='poem_1243323' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243323' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243323?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论造弓箭衣甲奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243323")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243323_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243323'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243323'>臣辄效愚忠，上冒宸听，其所陈述，实蹈危机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243323_comment'></div>感两宫圣知至深，拔用特达，此身既已许国，宁敢顾避而默默乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243323_comment'></div>臣谓方今用武之时，将帅专任，军中有阙，何患其不自言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243323_comment'></div>朝廷事量度应副足矣，何必他人更为之请？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243323_comment'></div>如吴璘谨畏体国，自不肯过当须求，他将闻之，岂免轻有邀索？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243323_comment'></div>此门一开，臣恐朝廷异日不胜其应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243323_comment'></div>若宣抚虞允文见得此军果须衣甲，则合密具事因，泛乞制造，以备缓急，而令吴璘量数取拨，不宜便指此一军而有请也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243323_comment'></div>虞允文既罢买马，又所招效用不多，而带行钱物无所归附，故欲用以造甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243323_comment'></div>谓此二万弓箭手虽非吾招，俾得吾甲而后为用，亦与招军无异，而不问其人之未可用，甲亦未至阙少也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243323_comment'></div>今年八月间，虞允文累檄总领所于宣抚司已交甲库中取甲三千九百馀副，以为所招效用之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243323_comment'></div>臣为关宣抚司，而吴璘尽数拨与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243323_comment'></div>臣十月五日主管宣谕职事，以此甲无用，遂尽还与璘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243323_comment'></div>允文既知吴璘下弓箭手阙披带，何为虚占上甲而不与也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243323_comment'></div>缘虞允文初到蜀中，力主姚仲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243323_comment'></div>仲败事，恐吴璘有言求，所以百方慰悦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243323_comment'></div>举隅可见，如前日衲袄一事是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243323_comment'></div>初，臣在总领所，与吴璘商议，虑士卒寒冷，乃进期于七月内支衣，令逐家制造冬服，足以卒岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243323_comment'></div>虞允文忽遣属官任慥密谕制置王刚中，令科下四川造衲袄四万领，民间所费百馀万引，郡县骚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243323_comment'></div>臣谓若诸军阙衣，则宣抚见在军前，与士卒同其暴露，自当来告，乃移牒制置司及诸路漕臣，未得制造；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243323_comment'></div>而会问宣抚司，若果须此，总领所当以官钱制造，不以扰民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243323_comment'></div>盖总所去军前为近，般运差省，州郡为之，则劳费数倍，而仓卒之际，并缘为奸，何所不至？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243323_comment'></div>会问宣抚司，久而不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243323_comment'></div>然此声既出，不可但已，总领所遂以官钱造布衫布裤各六万事与之，并脚钱之类，共只费十五万引，一月而办，送往军前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243323_comment'></div>吴璘止令于河池寄库，至今未支散，未尽者尚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243323_comment'></div>可见当时衲袄之不须作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243323_comment'></div>今之造甲，与此何异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243323_comment'></div>虞允文方赴阙奏事，必须更有献陈，识者皆以为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243323_comment'></div>圣鉴聪明，何所不烛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243323_comment'></div>但蜀地至远，朝廷必以使人为可信，一误诏令，为害实深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243323_comment'></div>更在陛下详之、审之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243323_comment'></div>军戎财赋，国之大事，安危所系，尤当重于听纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243323_comment'></div>臣愿陛下取允文前后所奏，试加考覈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243323_comment'></div>若前之言，后皆可迹，则信而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243323_comment'></div>或听其说而可喜，责其实而无验，则不可以不察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243323_comment'></div>臣孤远一身，朝无党援，非不知忤贵近之取祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243323_comment'></div>但以事关利害，职在咨询，茍雷同不言，使一方受弊，非臣所以报陛下愿忠之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243323_comment'></div>伏惟圣慈密赐采择，无使臣陷于失身之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243323_comment'></div>须至奏闻者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1243323_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年9月</a>　在成都，又有奏议论造弓箭衣甲。作品：又论虞允文乞造衣甲状。<div id='poem_1243324' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243324' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243324?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又论虞允文乞造衣甲状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243324")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243324_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243324'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243324'>臣近准朝廷两降劄命，令四川制造衣甲，甚为紧急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243324_comment'></div>臣已具宣抚司见在甲数奏闻，上宽圣虑去讫，所有本司虞允文留下招军例物钱，已尽数桩管，应副支使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243324_comment'></div>又令诸路于就近州郡有本司钱物去处，一面先次取拨不住。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243324_comment'></div>据制置司、提刑、转运及州郡公文称，期限逼促，劳费骚扰，四川为之鼎沸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243324_comment'></div>缘上件事朝廷专委制置司制造，总领所催促，但合支招军例物钱，别不敢干预，各令依已降指挥施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243324_comment'></div>然臣官名宣谕，以采访事宜为使指，若耳有所闻，意有所见，不以上闻，则是畏避怀奸，顾惜官职，以误器使，非陛下所以拔擢委任之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243324_comment'></div>或者必以臣为姑息蜀民太过，不肯体国，有乏军须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243324_comment'></div>臣中原人，蜀中并无产业，亦无亲族寓居，何私于蜀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243324_comment'></div>其所以爱惜民力者，正以边事方急，未有休息之期，欲为陛下系远方民心，保固根本，以备无穷之用耳，于臣何利焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243324_comment'></div>至于军前合用之物，自当协力济办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243324_comment'></div>在总领所二年，何尝令一事阙乏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243324_comment'></div>军之胜负，不特系国安危，于臣一身一家利害之重，岂敢立异，不体缓急乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243324_comment'></div>若乃得已而不已，以致扰民，臣若不言，谁任其咎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243324_comment'></div>谨再条具下项。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243324_comment'></div>右具如前，臣非不知衣甲武事所急，虽无前件，弓箭手亦当预备，但宜量紧慢，旋旋为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243324_comment'></div>今许尹所乞造二万副，尚有七八千副未了，而又造此二万副，虽得其新，复失其旧，于事何益？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243324_comment'></div>臣谓若以此招军例物钱分下诸路宪漕，各度事力，于有作院去处接续制造，比旧稍加工力，不须大段急其期限，以致骚扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243324_comment'></div>于旧欠七八千副外，更尽此钱而止，别听指挥，岂不公私两便？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243324_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1243324_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年11月</a>　在成都，有状论诸军见攻德顺，独王彦未到。作品：论诸军见攻德顺独王彦未到状。<div id='poem_1243326' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243326' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243326?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论诸军见攻德顺独王彦未到状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243326")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243326_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243326'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243326'>臣自十一月十三日金人离德顺军，将入水洛城一带作过，已具状劄录探报事，申三省枢密院机速房去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243326_comment'></div>见今贼马只在彼处，去秦州五七十里，中间更无关隘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243326_comment'></div>秦州见令兵守治平寨，贼出没剽掠，附近新民却皆顺蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243326_comment'></div>德顺军人马平安，粮草不阙，只是正路阻隔，银牌马由间道往来，亦有被擒者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243326_comment'></div>此寇初来，未敢轻进，我久无兵马救援，遂宿留修城下寨，渐为住计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243326_comment'></div>欲断德顺粮道以迫秦州，吴璘、吴拱、王彦、李师颜诸帅皆在此，而兵少不能进发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243326_comment'></div>王彦之军早来，则德顺攻寨之时，吴璘已出，彼必遁去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243326_comment'></div>及初犯水洛城一带时，若有官军迫逐，亦须却回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243326_comment'></div>王彦之师至今未报起发月日，自商州到此计程一月，正使即日已来，亦须半月以后可到，即今已是误事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243326_comment'></div>臣问吴璘有何方略，吴璘云已令间道往德顺抽兵六千人、马三四千匹来秦州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243326_comment'></div>此间除守杀金平、和尚原等处外，、吴拱、李师颜兵及秦州守戍，共有万二三千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243326_comment'></div>欲于秦州臈家城治平寨诸处摆布，候彼续更抽德顺军人马会合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243326_comment'></div>若吴璘师出，更藉吴拱等声势，敌或可退，不然须至决战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243326_comment'></div>观吴璘之意，其出须在旬日之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243326_comment'></div>据节次探报，敌众约有三万、马二万匹，亦自疲弊，别无生兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243326_comment'></div>吴璘语臣不须忧，终无所害，但深恨王彦军马后期，致失机会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243326_comment'></div>夏人只在会州上下，吴璘云但得金人退，夏人易与，不足虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243326_comment'></div>臣见在河池，所有德顺军功赏书填告劄事，缘德顺军三月间获捷，虽已推排，未曾奏明给据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243326_comment'></div>八月以后立功之人，皆在军前守御，推排未得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243326_comment'></div>吴璘之意，欲并前后功书填，少减超转，而事有窒碍，商量未定，兼为军务丛冗，工力不及，以此尚未报应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243326_comment'></div>臣见不住催促，及出榜晓谕，须至奏闻者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1243326_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　在成都，调护吴璘、王彦二人关系。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年12月</a>　在成都，上乞宫祠札子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　在成都，任宣谕使期间，奏杜莘老课绩为诸郡最上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　在成都。春，有札子奏乞重臣权位出诸帅之右者，倍道入蜀镇抚。作品：乞遣重臣入蜀镇抚奏札。<div id='poem_1243327' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243327' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243327?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞遣重臣入蜀镇抚奏劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243327")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243327_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243327'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243327'>臣契勘德顺归师失律，已节次奏闻，及申三省枢密院去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243327_comment'></div>四川精锐皆属吴璘，吴璘精锐尽在德顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243327_comment'></div>德顺正军三万馀人，今据吴拱所申，实收到人未及七千，统制将佐所存无几，但云未知下落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243327_comment'></div>自西南用兵，无此狼狈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243327_comment'></div>见今除皂郊一带王彦、吴拱、杨从仪、梅彦等所屯共有一万四千馀人外，其杀金平至和尚原一万六七千人，半是诸州威彊并兴洋义士，非皆劲卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243327_comment'></div>又德顺将士暴露之久，疲弊隔绝，事失机会，以致陷没，连营恸哭，声震原野，人怀怨心，公肆怒骂，其事难以尽述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243327_comment'></div>而王彦招到大汉等军，吴璘降到雷千户并食粮军兵五六千人，或在成州，或在大安军屯驻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243327_comment'></div>疑而不敢用，聚而不敢散，反费兵将防守，名为弹压，而人数不多不足相制，既成猜阻，得无反侧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243327_comment'></div>此辈老小皆在敌境，势难持久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243327_comment'></div>兼有前后擒到番人，往往配隶内郡作院，其数不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243327_comment'></div>近利州一夕逃去七十人，若或啸聚，亦足为患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243327_comment'></div>四川之忧，不但外虞，敌方安集故疆，未必便来深入，向去宁免侵犯？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243327_comment'></div>彼俘我将士，因之以三路解体之民，而关外四州尤剧困弊，重以签刺敢勇，人心离怨，往往逃窜山谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243327_comment'></div>四川事势可谓寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243327_comment'></div>吴璘丧师之后，方寸忧乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243327_comment'></div>往者无及，岂容更有疏虞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243327_comment'></div>为朝廷计，莫若速遣腹心重臣，权位出诸帅之右者，倍道入蜀镇抚而经理之，庶几可以保固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243327_comment'></div>救焚拯溺，正在此时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243327_comment'></div>伏望圣慈与大臣熟议，早赐裁取施行，实宗社生灵之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243327_comment'></div>须至奏闻者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1243327_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　在成都，再上乞宫祠札子。作品：再乞宫祠札子。<div id='poem_1243330' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243330' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243330?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再乞宫祠劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243330")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243330_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243330'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243330'>臣今月七日具劄子奏闻，缘臣宿疾发作，枝梧不前，兼吴璘已回兴州，任责措置，把截川口去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243330_comment'></div>见今宣谕一司，别无职事，官属吏卒，虚费廪给，乞改授一宫观差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243330_comment'></div>尚虑天听高远，未孚蝼蚁之诚，不免再冒诛夷，上干覆育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243330_comment'></div>伏念臣九年宦蜀，两蒙趣召，将行复止，委寄愈隆，叨窃宠荣，超逾涯分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243330_comment'></div>岂不欲以涓埃自效，少答生成，而衰病所婴，不容勉强，既怀忧责，难冀痊安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243330_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣精力已凋，如盖帷之久弊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243330_comment'></div>念臣死亡在即，俾骸骨以生还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243330_comment'></div>天地父母之恩，始终如是，臣非木石，当如何报也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243330_comment'></div>若他日幸臻勿药，自可捐躯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243330_comment'></div>或此身遂至填沟，亦当结草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243330_comment'></div>情词迫切，无任惶惧战慄、延企俟罪之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243330_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1243330_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年4月15日</a>　在成都，除集英殿修撰，提举江州太平兴国宫。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
淮安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fe002f7b06274f9d80c14f8a6fa98a30_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fe002f7b06274f9d80c14f8a6fa98a30");'><span id='fe002f7b06274f9d80c14f8a6fa98a30_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>，60岁</div><div id='fe002f7b06274f9d80c14f8a6fa98a30' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年11月</a>　在淮安，出疆，有诗纪行。作品：出疆次副使淮阴行。<div id='poem_66579' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_66579' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/66579?labeling=true' target='_blank'>出疆次副使淮阴舟行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_66579")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_66579_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_66579'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_66579'>丁年慕请缨，白首翻攘袂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_66579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_66579'>輶轩遽凭轼，魏阙频回睇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_66579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_66579'>两淮经战争，万物皆憔悴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_66579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_66579'>云繁雪霰舞，风猛波涛沸。<div id='poem_sentence_3_66579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_66579'>椎凌仅通航，鼓夜无停枻。<div id='poem_sentence_4_66579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_66579'>依樯闻喜鹊，酌斝烹鲜鳜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_66579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_66579'>出塞那复古，涉川今已利。<div id='poem_sentence_6_66579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_66579'>一节谁与持，同舟心靡异。<div id='poem_sentence_7_66579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_66579'>奋身徇主忧，图国忘私计。<div id='poem_sentence_8_66579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_66579'>昌黎去怀妾，定远老思妹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_66579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_66579'>高情独无戚，慧眼不留翳。<div id='poem_sentence_10_66579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_66579'>岂惟诗酒豪，抑亦文武备。<div id='poem_sentence_11_66579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_66579'>开馆昔登瀛，奉车元起沛。<div id='poem_sentence_12_66579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_66579'>君遭功名迫，我堪閒散置。<div id='poem_sentence_13_66579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_66579'>他年洛下吟，忆君徒拥鼻。<div id='poem_sentence_14_66579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_66579'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_66579_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年11月26日</a>　在淮安，帝手诏王之望等，待命境上。而令胡昉等先往，谕金以四州不可割之意。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
盱眙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e1e32caf24774874be73beafcd423227_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e1e32caf24774874be73beafcd423227");'><span id='e1e32caf24774874be73beafcd423227_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>，61岁</div><div id='e1e32caf24774874be73beafcd423227' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　在盱眙，年初，上书奏乞朝廷速决或和或守。作品：乞熟议和守奏议。<div id='poem_1243334' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243334' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243334?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞熟议和守奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243334")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243334_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243334'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243334'>臣等窃观布萨忠义擅回书牒，语言不顺，亟欲进兵，执辱吾审议官，意在梗绝和好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243334_comment'></div>金主父子虑其生事，故取二小使而释之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243334_comment'></div>其专权怙乱，势岂能久？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243334_comment'></div>君臣之间，必将有变，但恐金主之力未足以制之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243334_comment'></div>斯人不死，祸难未歇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243334_comment'></div>今大言虚喝而未能侵犯者，盖野无青草，马乏刍秣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243334_comment'></div>深春以后，岂可必其不来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243334_comment'></div>审议官虽回，而不受礼物，则所议不成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243334_comment'></div>或虽见允从，而别有邀索，朝廷必有以处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243334_comment'></div>吾欲援契丹旧例，而彼以契丹为非所拟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243334_comment'></div>吾欲修景德故事，而彼以景德为不可用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243334_comment'></div>吾以国信通问，而彼欲遣使报谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243334_comment'></div>又责吾缄封越式，礼体平易，既不许我称「大」字，又不肯号彼「北朝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243334_comment'></div>未论四州之地、归正等人，只此浮礼，尚尔争执，则凡今国书、誓草及称呼礼数，皆与敌意相违，持是以往，必不合矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243334_comment'></div>审议官不专使事，名位尚卑，故虽遭无礼而卒得放还，欲以致使副之来尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243334_comment'></div>使副若往，必不止此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243334_comment'></div>臣等虽能死节，何补于国？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243334_comment'></div>和议既尔，则边事其可以不虑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243334_comment'></div>臣等至盱眙四十日，问之将帅刘宝辈，深以兵少力分不足制敌为惧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243334_comment'></div>问之漕臣宋晓辈，亦钱粮阙乏支用不继为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243334_comment'></div>泗州虽城壁，而楼橹器械未具，敌骑出没，斥候全无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243334_comment'></div>议者谓贼若犯边必由淮右，淮右空阔，利于驰突。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243334_comment'></div>若自淮右绕出真、扬，则泗州虽能坚守，不过自保而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243334_comment'></div>淮东形势，清河口为最急，而堤备草草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243334_comment'></div>泗州去清河口一百六十馀里，非控阨之所，见今屯兵近四万众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243334_comment'></div>两淮事势单弱，而委四万众以保一城，其他要害之地，恐守御者有所不足也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243334_comment'></div>自敌人用兵，未尝由泗州入寇，城中诸将以为可守者，盖徼倖其不来耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243334_comment'></div>此臣等所亲见，其馀诸处传闻，事体尚不论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243334_comment'></div>今日之事，或和或守，宜速决大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243334_comment'></div>必欲和议之成，不知朝廷能曲从敌人意否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243334_comment'></div>既不能从，不若早为之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243334_comment'></div>敌人狡计，常持两端以款我而误我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243334_comment'></div>向国家靖康中和战并议，两说互疑，自春至冬，卒无定策，敌至河上，犹集议而不决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243334_comment'></div>覆辙未远，可为龟鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243334_comment'></div>臣等愿陛下与大臣熟议，权利害之轻重而审处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243334_comment'></div>欲和邪，如何而可以必合？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243334_comment'></div>欲守邪，如何而可以必固？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243334_comment'></div>和而不可合，守而不可固，迁延时月，或误大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243334_comment'></div>臣等心有所见，不敢隐默，冒昧诛殛，上渎圣聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243334_comment'></div>惟赦其狂愚而采择之，天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1243334_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南京
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='43ec5385293c496ea062f4aa1f53bc57_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("43ec5385293c496ea062f4aa1f53bc57");'><span id='43ec5385293c496ea062f4aa1f53bc57_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1165')">1164-1165年</a>，61-62岁</div><div id='43ec5385293c496ea062f4aa1f53bc57' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年7月17日</a>　到建康。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年7月19日</a>　在建康，劾陈汉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　在建康，到淮西宣谕使任后，有奏议乞修城。作品：乞修城壁壕堑关隘札。<div id='poem_1243343' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243343' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243343?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞修城壁壕堑关隘劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243343")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243343_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243343'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243343'>臣近准三省枢密院劄子：奉圣旨，令将紧要城壁濠堑疾速措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243343_comment'></div>臣今到淮西，见得利害，守城最为下策，前所修筑皆类儿戏，止可为虚名文具，岂足抗敌，枉费财力耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243343_comment'></div>兼军民才获休息，未宜劳动，而暑雨霖潦，亦非土工之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243343_comment'></div>且辍那工夫修创关隘，关隘若固，敌自不至城下，果至城下，城岂可守？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243343_comment'></div>如寿春、合淝，敌来即当退保，清野以困之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243343_comment'></div>惟濠州城有少未圆处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243343_comment'></div>见今相度淮西比来宁帖，北耗无它，亦无贼盗，诸军喜悦，百姓安堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243343_comment'></div>将来所忧，惟在淮东海、泗州耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243343_comment'></div>目今未烦圣虑，纷纷兴讹喜乱之语，不必垂天听，缓急臣等自奏闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1243343_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　在建康，到淮西宣谕使任后，有奏议论措置淮西漕运储积。作品：措置淮西漕运储积奏议。<div id='poem_1243344' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243344' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243344?labeling=true' target='_blank'>措置淮西漕运储积奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243344")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243344_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243344'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243344'>臣蒙朝廷降到事目，内一项，相度转漕储积去处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243344_comment'></div>臣与江东漕臣薛良朋及知水陆道路人讲究利害，将来江北不欲多置粮食，只于芜湖县储积，逐旋津发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243344_comment'></div>其淮西屯兵去处，系和州、巢县、桐城、庐州一带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243344_comment'></div>和州者，由当利河运；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243344_comment'></div>昭关、褒禅等处密近含山县者，由太阳河口入历湖运；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243344_comment'></div>巢县、庐州者，由裕河入焦湖运；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243344_comment'></div>桐城县者，由枞阳江口运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243344_comment'></div>以上皆近芜湖，见有仓廒可以顿放，或只系舟岸下，节次发放，实为稳便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243344_comment'></div>惟寿春、濠州最为回远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243344_comment'></div>自真州瓜州入闸，经由扬州、高邮、楚州入淮，过盱眙之西，又一百八十里至濠州，须著水运，又四百七十里至寿春，漕运为费力，且有敌境抄略之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243344_comment'></div>今寿春不欲多屯人，兵人既不多，可以措置陆运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243344_comment'></div>庐州至寿春二百里，大率千钱斗米可致一石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243344_comment'></div>若屯千人，则岁用粮九千石，并马料不过费钱万馀缗、米千馀斗，比之水运甚为省便，可保无虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243344_comment'></div>光州、麻城由巴河运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243344_comment'></div>自江入巴河，出陆一百五十里至麻城，又二百四十里至光州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243344_comment'></div>所屯人数不多，可以和籴相添应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243344_comment'></div>今具画图于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243344_comment'></div>除已具图册进呈外，伏望圣慈更赐详酌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243344_comment'></div>如或可用，即乞行下总领、转运遵依，措置施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243344_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1243344_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　在建康，到淮西宣谕使任后，有奏议乞沿淮创置斥堠烽火。作品：乞沿淮创置斥堠烽火奏议。<div id='poem_1243345' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243345' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243345?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞沿淮创置斥堠烽火奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243345")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243345_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243345'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243345'>臣前准朝廷降到事目，内一项，敌人沿淮清野，合如何措置斥堠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243345_comment'></div>臣契勘淮西平川广野，敌骑可以疾驱而自来，不置烽燧，只用探马，所以多至误事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243345_comment'></div>臣今与诸将措置，候将来防秋，各于贼马所由道路，登高瞭望，依旧日陕西、河东体例，创置斥堠烽火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243345_comment'></div>顷刻之间，达数百里，非徒缓急官与民间皆可预备，亦使敌人知我边境与向来不同，以伐其掩袭之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243345_comment'></div>兼诸军不入队人甚多，足以充役，不占破出战之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243345_comment'></div>遇防秋，即权罢其探马，亦令依旧，委实利便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243345_comment'></div>伏望圣慈行下诸军，更赐催促，令作速措置，仍具所置去处闻奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1243345_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　在建康，到淮西宣谕使任后，有奏议乞措置建康楼船。作品：乞招抚司与江东帅司措置建康楼船奏议。<div id='poem_1243346' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243346' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243346?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞招抚司与江东帅司措置建康楼船奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243346")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243346_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243346'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243346'>臣契勘淮西诸水不通淮河，由焦湖而北，可至庐州之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243346_comment'></div>庐州不宜置船，恐万一资寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243346_comment'></div>若得舟楫于庐州，则可由焦湖而入于江，此曹操窥兵之路也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243346_comment'></div>故淮西水军当尽在建康采石一带，以壮长江之势，而量以一二千人游战艘于江湖以疑敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243346_comment'></div>彼若深入，则乘间出合淝以扰其后，亦一奇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243346_comment'></div>建康战船殊未如法，楼船绝少，惟海鳅稍多，不足以威敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243346_comment'></div>前所招神劲军，皆东南乌合，其人脆弱，不耐江北风土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243346_comment'></div>向驻于泗州盱眙者多病死，又喜逃亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243346_comment'></div>宜以为水军而驻于建康、镇江之间，既风土相宜，可无疾夭，又舟师临阵，不容奔北，可以尽其死力，委实利便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243346_comment'></div>其船上器用什物往往未备，合速令计置，仍更添造楼船。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243346_comment'></div>将来踏车之人当用民兵及脩船之类，事干建康府，乞令招抚司与江东帅司同共措置。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1243346_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年8月23日</a>　在建康，劾刘敏士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年8月29日</a>　在建康，上奏议陈和、战二策。作品：论和议奏议。<div id='poem_1243349' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243349' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243349?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论和议奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年8月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243349")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243349_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243349'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243349'>臣十一日夜半准金字牌递到御劄，恭承圣问淮西事理、王彦军情，且令臣频具奏来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243349_comment'></div>臣自前月十七日到建康，日夜督诸将营建官寨烽火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243349_comment'></div>王彦地分已修了昭关山寨并关门，闻颇雄壮，见接续修褒禅、旷口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243349_comment'></div>时俊地分已修石湖岭，戚方亦修北峡关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243349_comment'></div>王彦今日亲过江北，巡历本地，方及时俊地分，自旷口一带转入巢县诸军，亲行按视，约半月日可回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243349_comment'></div>诸处烽燧，诸将相关措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243349_comment'></div>戚方、皇甫倜已申到处所，馀亦见次第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243349_comment'></div>后月上旬间，二事可了，候了日奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243349_comment'></div>乞从御前密差人检校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243349_comment'></div>今月初三日建康教阅水军，大小仅千艘，车战船四百七十馀只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243349_comment'></div>臣询问众人，皆云前所未有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243349_comment'></div>今见增置用修葺舟船，委可以壮长江之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243349_comment'></div>问淮西军民，见所修关隘，颇恃以安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243349_comment'></div>王彦一军都无事，钱粮足备，不闻减剋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243349_comment'></div>王彦御军，此间人颇议其宽，或闻行在传以为太严，甚不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243349_comment'></div>但军中事务，精力有所不逮，于文移词状之类遣决不敏，臣就其所短而扶持之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243349_comment'></div>建康即今军民安恬，只濠、寿间归正等人时为寇攘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243349_comment'></div>近寿春顿遇申，擒获二百馀人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243349_comment'></div>而濠州孔福申，以为拥去平民老小七八百口，玉石未分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243349_comment'></div>臣已约束，不得广有禁系，正贼之外，如有一时驱逐之人，仰释放存恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243349_comment'></div>继承朝廷指挥，委属官体究，见在施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243349_comment'></div>孔福在濠州，抚定弹压，人渐安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243349_comment'></div>夹淮之民号跳河子，以作过为生，近缘更戍未定，又北界招诱，故易相扇动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243349_comment'></div>逐州守臣可以措置，非久诸军出戍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243349_comment'></div>若尚不息，以千百人巡逴，自当消弭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243349_comment'></div>光州皇甫倜钱粮，前因改淮西总领应副之初，所以不继，今复委湖广总领，可免阙乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243349_comment'></div>又有知顺昌府孟新一项，侨寄光州梁安滩，有南北私商征税之利，皇甫倜甚不便之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243349_comment'></div>近孟新称避水，移来固始，与皇甫倜互有争诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243349_comment'></div>臣各移文调护，无得生事，别听指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243349_comment'></div>今朝廷令臣体度与孟新差遣，臣已遣人招之，候到面问，取其所便而处之，自此必无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243349_comment'></div>其馀如孙立者，如冯湛者，如李泽者，头项甚多，或就加抚存，或招来建康，皆有归著，暗消患害多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243349_comment'></div>若一处稍失事宜，便为衅不小，如陈八者是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243349_comment'></div>大抵当极弊之后，事如棼丝，急之则愈乱，须缓缓为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243349_comment'></div>甚费料理，心力俱尽，寝食不遑，然不敢屑屑奏闻，正恐贻君父之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243349_comment'></div>方张浚初罢，更张军政，臣孤单么䯢，滥当事任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243349_comment'></div>万目暌暌，伺其疏缺，日虞祸衅，不自意全，仰赖圣恩，得至今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243349_comment'></div>惟当尽力效死，罄竭愚忠，以报万分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243349_comment'></div>前朝廷既通北书，未有耗间，颇传议论不一，近闻已得回答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243349_comment'></div>臣远外不知其说，不敢妄议，但一意激厉将帅，为战守之备，以待不虞，不问和与不和也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243349_comment'></div>但为自治，不问敌彊不彊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243349_comment'></div>臣向者累次面对及具奏劄，其语甚详，陛下必尚记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243349_comment'></div>敌不肯和，必不回书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243349_comment'></div>既相报，复和意可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1243349_comment'></div>然语言必不肯便顺，须为彊项，有所邀索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1243349_comment'></div>吾既捐四州，彼若肯和，休兵息民，以成陛下之至仁，固天下莫大之福，臣之愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1243349_comment'></div>事若可从，陛下且以生灵为念，勿较小节，勿吝小费，能信顺而理直，天地鬼神实临之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1243349_comment'></div>若太不可从，则怕他不得，须稍见吾彊壮有立之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1243349_comment'></div>闻敌中自河而南，水旱飞蝗之灾尤甚于我，其动众亦难，张皇威势，半是虚声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1243349_comment'></div>我若一向伏弱，适足害事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1243349_comment'></div>子产曰「国不竞亦陵」，此至言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1243349_comment'></div>今日之事，不容再错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1243349_comment'></div>若和得成，须朝廷一一议定，然后遣使，勿独掇与使人，令辱国启衅，以误大事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1243349_comment'></div>伏惟圣慈裁择，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1243349_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年9月19日</a>　在建康，除参知政事。上谢表。作品：谢除参知政事表。除参知政事谢德寿宫表。<div id='poem_1243292' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243292' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243292?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除参知政事表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年9月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243292")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243292_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243292'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243292'>备争臣而谕旨，蔑著勋庸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243292_comment'></div>跻政地以出纶，骤膺亲擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243292_comment'></div>控忱诚之恳切，颁训告以频烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243292_comment'></div>拜命若惊，省躬甚惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243292_comment'></div>窃以虞舜绍唐尧之绪，五臣举而至治章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243292_comment'></div>武王恢周室之基，十乱升而大勋立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243292_comment'></div>惟辅理承化者非一贤之略，必同寅协恭而广众正之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243292_comment'></div>矧今三边未宁，庶事多舛，民生既匮，国是易摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243292_comment'></div>天灾时变之占，每深寅畏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243292_comment'></div>旰食宵衣之虑，特轸忧勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243292_comment'></div>陛下妙简臣邻，旁招俊哲，列之丞弼，责以谋谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243292_comment'></div>盖将外抚四夷，内修百度，振艺祖创垂之统，酬光尧付托之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243292_comment'></div>自非兼文武之弛张，效忠嘉于启沃，学邃古今而通其变，才周军国而措之宜，则何以上赞辰猷，下符佥论？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243292_comment'></div>如臣者斗筲小器，铅椠腐儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243292_comment'></div>徒以险阻艰难之备尝，稍谙俗状；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243292_comment'></div>故于东西南北而不择，自励公程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243292_comment'></div>久绝望于荣涂，复何心于晚节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243292_comment'></div>向者召从巴蜀，归觐阙庭，初无左右之容，遽被神明之照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243292_comment'></div>未更一岁，殆及九迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243292_comment'></div>版部铨曹，缀献纳论思之末；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243292_comment'></div>禁林谏苑，充文辞言语之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243292_comment'></div>皆席暖之未遑，已抗旃而于迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243292_comment'></div>心欲为而不逮者精力，劳则有而何取于事功！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243292_comment'></div>迟休榆塞之防秋，丐老菟裘而卒岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243292_comment'></div>敢期侥倖，乃尔超逾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243292_comment'></div>除二府之自外方，追庆历名臣之殊遇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243292_comment'></div>由七人而参大政，盖本朝历世之罕闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243292_comment'></div>萃此宠光，若为负荷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243292_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下圣聪旁达，睿断无疑，照谗诬若七政之明，定许予若四时之信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243292_comment'></div>祗承于帝，思铺张不世之休；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243292_comment'></div>无竞维人，每梦想非常之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243292_comment'></div>遂令猥琐，亦玷登庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243292_comment'></div>臣敢不鞭策疲驽，支持衰病，仰体丁宁之旨，对扬特达之知！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243292_comment'></div>际会风云，方快睹亨嘉之运；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243292_comment'></div>奉承教令，期助成宏远之规。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1243292_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1243293' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243293' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243293?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除参知政事谢德寿宫表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年9月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243293")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243293_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243293'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243293'>禁闼备官，冒缀七人之列；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243293_comment'></div>岩廊陪议，骤参四辅之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243293_comment'></div>仍兼总于知枢，俾窃闻于国论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243293_comment'></div>恩荣不次，指目谓何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243293_comment'></div>伏念臣识昧经邦，才非济务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243293_comment'></div>少专末学，粗知涉猎之勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243293_comment'></div>晚际昌期，积有超逾之愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243293_comment'></div>自横经于太学，旋揭节于外台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243293_comment'></div>虽崎嵚流落之备尝，顾智略谋猷之莫效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243293_comment'></div>绣衣直指，曾微肤使之称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243293_comment'></div>华衮是褒，罙益孤臣之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243293_comment'></div>逮嗣圣绍开于景运，宜熙朝并列于群材，藐是陈人，跻于法从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243293_comment'></div>矧帷幄方恢于远驭，而干戈未戢于中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243293_comment'></div>毕千虑以陈愚，冀宽宵旰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243293_comment'></div>罄一心而尽瘁，曷补涓尘？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243293_comment'></div>敢意孤踪，遽叨巨用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243293_comment'></div>此盖伏遇光尧寿圣太上皇帝陛下轸深仁而念旧，扩大度以包荒，曲尽初终，致兹图任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243293_comment'></div>君臣胥契，真成千载之逢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243293_comment'></div>神圣相承，曷副重离之照？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243293_comment'></div>维坚素节，以报洪私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1243293_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年10月17日</a>　在建康，兼同知枢密院事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年10月17日</a>　在建康，兼同知枢密院事。吴芾以姻家乞回避。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　在建康。冬，与杨存中、李侍郎书，论两淮屯兵。作品：与殿帅杨郡王论两淮移屯利害书。与李侍郎书论两淮兵屯。<div id='poem_1243406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与殿帅杨郡王论两淮移屯利害书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243406")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243406'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243406'>某比承钧旆之来，得以款诲，欣慰无量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243406_comment'></div>奉违信宿，已深倾企，递中两辱诲示，益荷眷勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243406_comment'></div>即日雪晴苦寒，伏惟折冲有相，钧候万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243406_comment'></div>承谕张马帅已离和州，既不可回，且令来长芦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243406_comment'></div>又令员琦与宋受来瓜步，想此经画，非钧意之得已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243406_comment'></div>然其利害，前日商量甚详，宜更审处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243406_comment'></div>大敌在近，而军无定处，旋营寨栅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243406_comment'></div>扬州所患兵少势孤，今复员琦、宋受远去；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243406_comment'></div>和州见忧敌人窥伺，今复移却张守忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243406_comment'></div>郡王重臣宿将，谙练兵机，似此果无后虑否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243406_comment'></div>军旅之事，某未之学也，深以为疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243406_comment'></div>大军临敌，岂可数数轻动？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243406_comment'></div>张守忠既来长芦，未应遽回，且徐徐图之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243406_comment'></div>员、宋若尚未动，令往扬州，如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243406_comment'></div>国事至重，苟有所见，不敢不以忠告，尚幸裁处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243406_comment'></div>馀冀保重，前膺册拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1243406_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1243407' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243407' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243407?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与李侍郎书论两淮兵屯</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243407")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243407_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243407'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243407'>某前日尝获承教，慰甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243407_comment'></div>遽复睽异，倾企如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243407_comment'></div>即日雪后寒凛，伏惟台候万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243407_comment'></div>瓜步却依前议，深以为忧，想只为张马帅既来长芦，不得已而为此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243407_comment'></div>然马帅之动，既已非策，若更以员琦、宋受来瓜步，恐又增一失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243407_comment'></div>勍敌迫近，而大军数移，可为寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243407_comment'></div>员、宋不屯真州，上意也，不令在真州，则当往六合、扬州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243407_comment'></div>今却令往瓜步，缓急之际，声势不相接，奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243407_comment'></div>某采访于人，皆以员、宋往扬州为得策，淮东兵合于扬州，则军威自震，且六合有所资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243407_comment'></div>若令往瓜步，去扬州更远，虽与六合相近，恐未必能相救援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243407_comment'></div>张守忠移屯之后，和州一带空虚，亦甚可忧，侍郎深宜婉画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243407_comment'></div>今张帅业已到长芦，若宋、员未动，且令往扬州，如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243407_comment'></div>大抵规摹须要素定，先自扰扰，则为贼所窥，非计之得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243407_comment'></div>侍郎其审处之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1243407_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年11月6日</a>　在建康，督视江淮军马。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年12月7日</a>　在建康，同都督江淮军马。力辞。己丑，罢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年13月13日</a>　在建康，太学生数十人复阙上书，乞斩汤思退、王之望、尹穑三人，以谢天下。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年14月22日</a>　在建康，朝辞，往江淮劳师。上札。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年闰11月24日</a>　罢参政，以端明殿学士提举太平兴国宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年1月17日</a>　王稽中奏王之望谋国前后反复异词。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年2月17日</a>　自左中大夫罢为端明殿学士、提举江州太平兴国宫。乞致仕。作品：乞追寝职名宫观守本官致仕奏议。<div id='poem_1243354' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243354' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243354?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞追寝职名宫观守本官致仕奏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年2月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243354")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243354_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243354'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243354'>臣近三具奏劄，乞赐罢免，仍重行黜责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243354_comment'></div>今二月十七日准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨除端明殿学士，在外宫观，任便居住。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243354_comment'></div>臣闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243354_comment'></div>伏念臣出将使指，入辅政机，无毫发补报，而人言荐至，罪戾山积，虽窜戮不足以谢天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243354_comment'></div>圣恩深厚，未忍加诛，乃叨秘殿之华资，窃珍祠之厚禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243354_comment'></div>保全终始之遇，非臣犬马所能上报万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243354_comment'></div>但罪应黜责而未正典刑，恐于公论有所未允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243354_comment'></div>所有上件恩命，臣不敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243354_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特赐追寝，令臣守本官致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243354_comment'></div>臣虽疾病之馀，死亡无日，犹当效结草之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243354_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1243354_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年2月17日</a>　自左中大夫罢为端明殿学士、提举江州太平兴国宫。上谢表。作品：谢除端明殿学士表。<div id='poem_1243294' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243294' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243294?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除端明殿学士表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年2月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243294")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243294_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243294'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243294'>辅政岩廊，实旷近司之职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243294_comment'></div>奉祠珍馆，犹叨秘殿之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243294_comment'></div>抗章爰罄于恳辞，出綍重勤于申谕，危衷易感，衰涕交零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243294_comment'></div>伏念臣滥得虚名，本无实用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243294_comment'></div>虽屡膺于烦使，曾靡效于微劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243294_comment'></div>召于久外之中，遽有非常之遇，粤由侍从，擢置疑丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243294_comment'></div>自知绵力之不称，几犯威颜而引避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243294_comment'></div>属边隅之正扰，致志愿之未伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243294_comment'></div>卒繇罔功，上辜殊奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243294_comment'></div>人言荐至，宜典宪之必加；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243294_comment'></div>圣度优容，暴愆尤而弗忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243294_comment'></div>曲全体貌，以示眷怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243294_comment'></div>深惭颠扑之馀，特费保持之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243294_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下聪明天纵，忠厚风移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243294_comment'></div>嘉善而矜不能，士无失职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243294_comment'></div>观过各于其党，民用归仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243294_comment'></div>故俾孤踪，获逃重谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243294_comment'></div>臣敢不杜门念咎，击壤待终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243294_comment'></div>尊主庇民，已负平生之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243294_comment'></div>杀身报德，空馀未死之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1243294_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年2月17日</a>　自左中大夫罢为端明殿学士、提举江州太平兴国宫。乞致仕。上谢表。作品：除端明殿学士谢德寿宫表。<div id='poem_1243295' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243295' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243295?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除端明学士谢德寿宫表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年2月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243295")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243295_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243295'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243295'>预政罔功，已旷辅臣之职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243295_comment'></div>奉祠窃食，尚叨秘殿之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243295_comment'></div>抚己知惭，拜恩有腼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243295_comment'></div>伏念臣本无实用，滥得虚名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243295_comment'></div>曩烦使之屡更，曾微劳之莫效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243295_comment'></div>召从远外，服在论思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243295_comment'></div>所除者乃中外之要权，所任者皆安危之重事，遂由谏省，起置政涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243295_comment'></div>独深明主之知，躐处群工之右，实道家之所忌，宜众怨之必归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243295_comment'></div>虽英贤任此以犹难，以罪戾居之而岂免？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243295_comment'></div>果婴物议，致圣神曲费于保持；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243295_comment'></div>特屈刑章，俾体貌得全于终始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243295_comment'></div>危踪未陨，厚德难名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243295_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇光尧寿圣太上皇帝陛下视远维明，允恭克逊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243295_comment'></div>彰善瘅恶，炳日月之照临；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243295_comment'></div>忘过计功，廓乾坤之覆育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243295_comment'></div>故如孤弱，亦逭颠隮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243295_comment'></div>臣敢不自讼前非，益坚素守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243295_comment'></div>桑榆晚景，知莫报于涓涘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243295_comment'></div>松柏岁寒，誓弗渝于金石。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1243295_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年4月</a>　起知福州、福建路安抚使。<br /></div>
