-----title
福州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='82ce778c3abb4f81b649119052c3b2c5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("82ce778c3abb4f81b649119052c3b2c5");'><span id='82ce778c3abb4f81b649119052c3b2c5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1168')">1165-1168年</a>，62-65岁</div><div id='82ce778c3abb4f81b649119052c3b2c5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　在福州，增修院试监舍。秋试，有告谕举子文。作品：福唐解试告谕举子文。<div id='poem_1243390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243390?labeling=true' target='_blank'>福唐解试告谕举子文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243390")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243390_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243390'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243390'>福唐今年秋赋，投家状于有司者万有七千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243390_comment'></div>乡举之众，天下莫比，亦闽中昔日之所未有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243390_comment'></div>可谓盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243390_comment'></div>前榜自大魁而下联甲科者五人，与胪唱者六七十人，国家于此邦人士诚无负矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243390_comment'></div>本州仰体朝廷之意，以科举为重事，开斥贡院，编排坐次，增添内外执事之人，种种如法，州郡于此邦举子亦不苟矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243390_comment'></div>诸君盍澡身厉行，思称宾兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243390_comment'></div>父兄戒其子弟，长老训其后生，朋友之间更相劝约，咸趋礼义，尽革嚣浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243390_comment'></div>毋怙众以作非，毋自轻而取侮，绝博塞之戏，息锥刀之争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243390_comment'></div>出于里巷之间，必有矜持之色，众庶归重，儒服自尊，凡所观瞻，孰不起敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243390_comment'></div>士风如此，顾不美欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243390_comment'></div>或有不靖之徒，多士宜共疾之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243390_comment'></div>岁律三更，科诏一下，贤材待时藏器，指日奋身，岂容猖狂，以致颠沛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243390_comment'></div>且大开选举，精考艺能，乃功名富贵所由之途，非凶暴豪强兴争之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243390_comment'></div>正使捷如庆忌，勇若孟贲，何取于翰墨之场乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243390_comment'></div>一犯严科，即罹公法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243390_comment'></div>与夫鹿鸣开燕，黄堂享劝驾之仪，豹变还乡，绿袂耀观光之宠者，荣华缪辱，乌可同日道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243390_comment'></div>又阔步既腾，亨衢甚坦，稽古所获，奚止于斯？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243390_comment'></div>夫以万七千人群萃于此，其间琐碎，宁无短长，在于宽和，无事阔略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243390_comment'></div>三日借路，岂责其全；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243390_comment'></div>一忿忘身，虽悔无及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243390_comment'></div>将来引试，切忌搀先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243390_comment'></div>题目出于有司，必待举人尽入，何须竞进，以冒隘途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243390_comment'></div>虽少迁延，未淹晷刻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243390_comment'></div>远于蹂践，方免忧危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243390_comment'></div>宅心既宁，下笔熟洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243390_comment'></div>至如案设既定，尺寸有分，移徙乱行，扰动实众，我欲自便，人将谓何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243390_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243390_comment'></div>在丑不争，先圣之格言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243390_comment'></div>畏威如疾，前贤之明戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243390_comment'></div>凡我应书之众，勿屑细故，以远大期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243390_comment'></div>鸿鹄秋天一飞，万里安可量也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243390_comment'></div>惟诸君勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243390_comment'></div>故兹告谕，各请知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1243390_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　在福州，为赡学田，按图籍复旧疆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　在福州，复旧九仙楼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　在福州，命名雅歌堂。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　在福州。夏，祈雨于灵泽庙、利泽庙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　在福州，有《自公堂诗》<div id='poem_66515' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_66515' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/66515?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自公堂诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_66515")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_66515_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_66515'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_66515'>丛石当轩峙，横池傍砌深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_66515_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_66515'>还将修竹绕，半入古榕阴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_66515_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_66515'>昼赏风澜皱，宵怜月影侵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_66515_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_66515'>聊纾江海志，寄此小山林<span class='inlineComment2'>（《淳熙三山志》卷七）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_66515_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_66515'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_66515_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　在福州，增城外草市社如城内忠义社。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年4月23日</a>　在福州，诏赐夏药。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　林之奇驰函王之望，称王之望在闽有民望。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年6月</a>　在福州，以与王之望有隙，韩元吉改知江州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年10月</a>　在福州，加资政殿大学士，移知温州。上谢宰相启。作品：知温州谢宰相启。<div id='poem_1243522' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243522' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243522?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知温州谢宰相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28578, "宋", "王之望", "poem_title_1243522")'>王之望</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243522_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243522'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243522'>分帅阃于三山，许辞重计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243522_comment'></div>移守符于孤屿，载冒优恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243522_comment'></div>顾惭衰朽之踪，倍费维持之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243522_comment'></div>伏念某艰穷滋甚，疲薾奚堪，知涯分之已逾，惧祸灾之叵测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243522_comment'></div>残年多病，嗟药石之何功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243522_comment'></div>只影自怜，吊糟糠之不淑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243522_comment'></div>心既凋于忧患，力难勉于事为，仰干从欲之仁，曲遂便私之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243522_comment'></div>投閒置散，未容奉香火于殊庭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243522_comment'></div>辞尊居卑，犹俾宣诏条于名郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243522_comment'></div>获伸志愿，实赖敷陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243522_comment'></div>此盖恭遇某官德业皋夔，机谋伊管，收贤才以凝庶绩，笃故旧以变浇风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243522_comment'></div>有奋庸熙载之能，已冠帝臣之选；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243522_comment'></div>抚养生送死之感，首蒙王道之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243522_comment'></div>方托馀庥，庶逃大戾，更藉陶钧之运，早酬田里之归。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1243522_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年12月18日</a>　在福州，荐魏掞之于朝。<br /></div>
